b\u00ecnh\n- Projects \u01b0u ti\u00ean boilerplate t\u1ed1i thi\u1ec3u\n- \u1ee8ng d\u1ee5ng c\u1ea7n hi\u1ec7u su\u1ea5t t\u1ed1t kh\u00f4ng c\u1ea7n t\u1ed1i \u01b0u ph\u1ee9c t\u1ea1p\n- Teams mu\u1ed1n th\u1ee9 g\u00ec \u0111\u00f3 m\u1ea1nh h\u01a1n Context nh\u01b0ng \u0111\u01a1n gi\u1ea3n h\u01a1n Redux\n- Projects s\u1eed d\u1ee5ng TypeScript\n- \u1ee8ng d\u1ee5ng c\u1ea7n truy c\u1eadp state ngo\u00e0i React components\n\n---\n\n## So S\u00e1nh Chi Ti\u1ebft\n\n| T\u00ednh n\u0103ng | Context API | Redux | Zustand |\n| ---------------------- | ------------ | ------------------ | --------------- |\n| **Bundle Size** | 0 (t\u00edch h\u1ee3p) | ~12KB (v\u1edbi RTK) | ~1KB |\n| **Learning Curve** | Th\u1ea5p | Cao | Th\u1ea5p |\n| **Boilerplate** | Trung b\u00ecnh | Cao (Th\u1ea5p v\u1edbi RTK) | R\u1ea5t th\u1ea5p |\n| **Hi\u1ec7u su\u1ea5t** | C\u1ea7n t\u1ed1i \u01b0u | T\u1ed1t | Xu\u1ea5t s\u1eafc |\n| **DevTools** | Kh\u00f4ng c\u00f3 | Xu\u1ea5t s\u1eafc | T\u1ed1t |\n| **Middleware** | Kh\u00f4ng c\u00f3 | Phong ph\u00fa | T\u00edch h\u1ee3p |\n| **TypeScript Support** | T\u1ed1t | Xu\u1ea5t s\u1eafc | Xu\u1ea5t s\u1eafc |\n| **C\u1ed9ng \u0111\u1ed3ng** | R\u1ea5t l\u1edbn | R\u1ea5t l\u1edbn | \u0110ang ph\u00e1t tri\u1ec3n |\n| **Setup Complexity** | Th\u1ea5p | Trung b\u00ecnh | R\u1ea5t th\u1ea5p |\n| **Async Support** | Th\u1ee7 c\u00f4ng | Xu\u1ea5t s\u1eafc | T\u1ed1t |\n| **Time-Travel Debug** | Kh\u00f4ng | C\u00f3 | Gi\u1edbi h\u1ea1n |\n\n---\n\n## H\u01b0\u1edbng D\u1eabn Quy\u1ebft \u0110\u1ecbnh: B\u1ea1n N\u00ean Ch\u1ecdn G\u00ec?\n\n### Ch\u1ecdn **Context API** n\u1ebfu:\n\n- \u2713 B\u1ea1n qu\u1ea3n l\u00fd state \u0111\u01a1n gi\u1ea3n, \u00edt thay \u0111\u1ed5i\n- \u2713 B\u1ea1n mu\u1ed1n zero dependencies b\u1ed5 sung\n- \u2713 App c\u1ee7a b\u1ea1n c\u00f3 quy m\u00f4 nh\u1ecf \u0111\u1ebfn trung b\u00ecnh\n- \u2713 B\u1ea1n chia s\u1ebb static configuration (theme, locale, auth)\n- \u2713 B\u1ea1n tho\u1ea3i m\u00e1i v\u1edbi vi\u1ec7c t\u1ed1i \u01b0u re-renders th\u1ee7 c\u00f4ng\n\n### Ch\u1ecdn **Redux** n\u1ebfu:\n\n- \u2713 B\u1ea1n x\u00e2y d\u1ef1ng \u1ee9ng d\u1ee5ng l\u1edbn, ph\u1ee9c t\u1ea1p\n- \u2713 B\u1ea1n c\u1ea7n debugging m\u1ea1nh m\u1ebd v\u1edbi time-travel\n- \u2713 Team c\u1ee7a b\u1ea1n \u0111\u00e3 quen v\u1edbi Redux\n- \u2713 B\u1ea1n c\u00f3 logic state ph\u1ee9c t\u1ea1p v\u1edbi nhi\u1ec1u dependencies\n- \u2713 B\u1ea1n c\u1ea7n middleware phong ph\u00fa cho side effects\n- \u2713 T\u00ednh d\u1ef1 \u0111o\u00e1n v\u00e0 testability l\u00e0 \u01b0u ti\u00ean h\u00e0ng \u0111\u1ea7u\n- \u2713 B\u1ea1n l\u00e0m vi\u1ec7c tr\u00ean d\u1ef1 \u00e1n doanh nghi\u1ec7p v\u1edbi patterns nghi\u00eam ng\u1eb7t\n\n### Ch\u1ecdn **Zustand** n\u1ebfu:\n\n- \u2713 B\u1ea1n mu\u1ed1n boilerplate t\u1ed1i thi\u1ec3u v\u1edbi n\u0103ng su\u1ea5t t\u1ed1i \u0111a\n- \u2713 Hi\u1ec7u su\u1ea5t l\u00e0 \u01b0u ti\u00ean kh\u00f4ng c\u1ea7n t\u1ed1i \u01b0u th\u1ee7 c\u00f4ng\n- \u2713 B\u1ea1n \u0111ang x\u00e2y d\u1ef1ng \u1ee9ng d\u1ee5ng React hi\u1ec7n \u0111\u1ea1i\n- \u2713 B\u1ea1n mu\u1ed1n th\u1ee9 g\u00ec \u0111\u00f3 m\u1ea1nh h\u01a1n Context nh\u01b0ng \u0111\u01a1n gi\u1ea3n h\u01a1n Redux\n- \u2713 Bundle size quan tr\u1ecdng v\u1edbi b\u1ea1n\n- \u2713 B\u1ea1n c\u1ea7n truy c\u1eadp state ngo\u00e0i React components\n- \u2713 B\u1ea1n tho\u1ea3i m\u00e1i v\u1edbi h\u1ec7 sinh th\u00e1i nh\u1ecf h\u01a1n (nh\u01b0ng \u0111ang ph\u00e1t tri\u1ec3n)\n\n---\n\n## C\u00f3 Th\u1ec3 K\u1ebft H\u1ee3p Ch\u00fang Kh\u00f4ng?\n\nHo\u00e0n to\u00e0n c\u00f3 th\u1ec3! Nhi\u1ec1u \u1ee9ng d\u1ee5ng production s\u1eed d\u1ee5ng nhi\u1ec1u gi\u1ea3i ph\u00e1p qu\u1ea3n l\u00fd state:\n\n**Patterns Ph\u1ed5 Bi\u1ebfn:**\n\n- **Context API cho global config** + **Zustand cho feature-specific state**\n- **Context API cho auth** + **Redux cho business logic ph\u1ee9c t\u1ea1p**\n- **Zustand cho UI state** + **Redux cho server state** (ho\u1eb7c React Query)\n\nV\u00ed d\u1ee5:\n\n```jsx\n// D\u00f9ng Context cho theme (\u1ed5n \u0111\u1ecbnh, hi\u1ebfm khi thay \u0111\u1ed5i)\n\n {/* D\u00f9ng Zustand cho shopping cart (c\u1eadp nh\u1eadt th\u01b0\u1eddng xuy\u00ean) */}\n \n;\n\n// Trong ShoppingCart\nconst items = useCartStore((state) => state.items);\nconst { theme } = useTheme();\n```\n\n---\n\n## L\u1ed9 Tr\u00ecnh Migration\n\n### T\u1eeb Context API sang Zustand\n\nZustand stores c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c gi\u1edbi thi\u1ec7u d\u1ea7n d\u1ea7n song song v\u1edbi Context providers. B\u1eaft \u0111\u1ea7u v\u1edbi c\u00e1c ph\u1ea7n quan tr\u1ecdng v\u1ec1 hi\u1ec7u su\u1ea5t c\u1ee7a state.\n\n### T\u1eeb Redux sang Zustand\n\nC\u00e2n nh\u1eafc \u0111i\u1ec1u n\u00e0y n\u1ebfu code Redux c\u1ee7a b\u1ea1n qu\u00e1 d\u00e0i d\u00f2ng v\u00e0 b\u1ea1n kh\u00f4ng c\u1ea7n t\u1ea5t c\u1ea3 t\u00ednh n\u0103ng c\u1ee7a Redux. Migrate t\u1eebng feature m\u1ed9t.\n\n### T\u1eeb Zustand sang Redux\n\n\u0110i\u1ec1u n\u00e0y hi\u1ebfm khi x\u1ea3y ra nh\u01b0ng c\u00f3 \u00fd ngh\u0129a khi app c\u1ee7a b\u1ea1n ph\u00e1t tri\u1ec3n \u0111\u1ebfn m\u1ee9c c\u1ea7n h\u1ec7 sinh th\u00e1i middleware v\u00e0 kh\u1ea3 n\u0103ng debugging c\u1ee7a Redux.\n\n---\n\n## Khuy\u1ebfn Ngh\u1ecb C\u1ee7a T\u00f4i\n\n\u0110\u1ed1i v\u1edbi h\u1ea7u h\u1ebft c\u00e1c d\u1ef1 \u00e1n React hi\u1ec7n \u0111\u1ea1i n\u0103m 2026, t\u00f4i khuy\u00ean:\n\n**B\u1eaft \u0111\u1ea7u v\u1edbi Context API** cho state \u0111\u01a1n gi\u1ea3n, \u1ed5n \u0111\u1ecbnh nh\u01b0 theme v\u00e0 auth. **S\u1eed d\u1ee5ng Zustand** cho m\u1ecdi th\u1ee9 kh\u00e1c c\u1ea7n global. Ch\u1ec9 ch\u1ecdn **Redux** n\u1ebfu b\u1ea1n th\u1ef1c s\u1ef1 c\u1ea7n s\u1ee9c m\u1ea1nh c\u1ee7a n\u00f3 cho logic state ph\u1ee9c t\u1ea1p ho\u1eb7c n\u1ebfu b\u1ea1n \u0111ang l\u00e0m vi\u1ec7c tr\u00ean \u1ee9ng d\u1ee5ng doanh nghi\u1ec7p l\u1edbn v\u1edbi y\u00eau c\u1ea7u nghi\u00eam ng\u1eb7t.\n\nH\u1ec7 sinh th\u00e1i React \u0111\u00e3 tr\u01b0\u1edfng th\u00e0nh \u0111\u1ebfn m\u1ee9c b\u1ea1n kh\u00f4ng c\u1ea7n \u0111\u01b0a ra m\u1ed9t l\u1ef1a ch\u1ecdn cho m\u1ecdi th\u1ee9. S\u1eed d\u1ee5ng c\u00f4ng c\u1ee5 ph\u00f9 h\u1ee3p cho t\u1eebng nhu c\u1ea7u qu\u1ea3n l\u00fd state c\u1ee5 th\u1ec3.\n\n---\n\n## K\u1ebft Lu\u1eadn\n\nKh\u00f4ng c\u00f3 gi\u1ea3i ph\u00e1p qu\u1ea3n l\u00fd state \"t\u1ed1t nh\u1ea5t\" ph\u1ed5 qu\u00e1t - n\u00f3 ph\u1ee5 thu\u1ed9c v\u00e0o nhu c\u1ea7u c\u1ee5 th\u1ec3 c\u1ee7a b\u1ea1n:\n\n- **Context API** v\u01b0\u1ee3t tr\u1ed9i v\u1ec1 t\u00ednh \u0111\u01a1n gi\u1ea3n v\u00e0 chia s\u1ebb state kh\u00f4ng ph\u1ee5 thu\u1ed9c\n- **Redux** v\u1eabn l\u00e0 v\u00f4 \u0111\u1ecbch cho qu\u1ea3n l\u00fd state ph\u1ee9c t\u1ea1p, c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 d\u1ef1 \u0111o\u00e1n \u1edf quy m\u00f4 l\u1edbn\n- **Zustand** \u0111\u1ea1t \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c s\u1ef1 c\u00e2n b\u1eb1ng ho\u00e0n h\u1ea3o gi\u1eefa s\u1ee9c m\u1ea1nh v\u00e0 s\u1ef1 \u0111\u01a1n gi\u1ea3n cho c\u00e1c app React hi\u1ec7n \u0111\u1ea1i\n\nB\u1eaft \u0111\u1ea7u \u0111\u01a1n gi\u1ea3n, v\u00e0 ch\u1ec9 th\u00eam \u0111\u1ed9 ph\u1ee9c t\u1ea1p khi b\u1ea1n c\u1ea7n. H\u1ea7u h\u1ebft c\u00e1c \u1ee9ng d\u1ee5ng s\u1ebd ho\u00e0n to\u00e0n h\u00e0i l\u00f2ng v\u1edbi Context API v\u00e0 Zustand. D\u00e0nh Redux cho khi b\u1ea1n th\u1ef1c s\u1ef1 c\u1ea7n c\u00e1c kh\u1ea3 n\u0103ng c\u1ee7a n\u00f3.\n\nGi\u1ea3i ph\u00e1p qu\u1ea3n l\u00fd state \u01b0a th\u00edch c\u1ee7a b\u1ea1n l\u00e0 g\u00ec? Chia s\u1ebb tr\u1ea3i nghi\u1ec7m c\u1ee7a b\u1ea1n trong ph\u1ea7n b\u00ecnh lu\u1eadn b\u00ean d\u01b0\u1edbi!\n\n---\n\n**\u0110\u1ecdc Th\u00eam:**\n\n- [React Context API Documentation](https://react.dev/reference/react/useContext)\n- [Redux Toolkit Official Guide](https://redux-toolkit.js.org/)\n- [Zustand GitHub Repository](https://github.com/pmndrs/zustand)\n- [React State Management in 2026: H\u01b0\u1edbng D\u1eabn \u0110\u1ea7y \u0110\u1ee7](#)\n\n---\n\n_Ch\u00fac b\u1ea1n code vui v\u1ebb! \ud83d\ude80_\n"}], "grading": null}, {"id": "jwt-authentication-with_skill", "prompt": "Write blog post about JWT authentication from brief bullet points", "eval_id": 4, "outputs": [{"name": "blog-post-en.md", "type": "text", "content": "# JWT Authentication: A Comprehensive Guide to Modern Authentication\n\n> **For developers who want to deeply understand JWT and implement secure authentication**\n\nUser authentication is the foundation of every modern web application. But how do you authenticate securely, scalably, and effectively in distributed systems? JSON Web Token (JWT) has become the most popular solution to this problem. In this article, we'll dive deep into JWT from basic concepts to security best practices.\n\n## Part 1: What is JWT?\n\n### 1.1 Definition and Structure\n\nJSON Web Token (JWT) is an open standard (RFC 7519) for securely transmitting information between parties as a JSON object. JWT is designed to be compact, self-contained, and verifiable for integrity.\n\nA JWT token consists of 3 parts, separated by dots (`.`):\n\n```\neyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9.eyJzdWIiOiIxMjM0NTY3ODkwIiwibmFtZSI6IkpvaG4gRG9lIiwiaWF0IjoxNTE2MjM5MDIyfQ.SflKxwRJSMeKKF2QT4fwpMeJf36POk6yJV_adQssw5c\n```\n\n**Structure:**\n\n```\nHEADER.PAYLOAD.SIGNATURE\n```\n\n#### Header\n\nContains information about the token type and encryption algorithm:\n\n```json\n{\n \"alg\": \"HS256\",\n \"typ\": \"JWT\"\n}\n```\n\n#### Payload\n\nContains claims (information about the user and metadata):\n\n```json\n{\n \"sub\": \"1234567890\",\n \"name\": \"John Doe\",\n \"email\": \"john@example.com\",\n \"role\": \"admin\",\n \"iat\": 1516239022,\n \"exp\": 1516242622\n}\n```\n\n#### Signature\n\nCreated by encoding the header and payload with a secret key:\n\n```\nHMACSHA256(\n base64UrlEncode(header) + \".\" +\n base64UrlEncode(payload),\n secret\n)\n```\n\n### 1.2 Why is JWT Popular?\n\nJWT solves many problems of traditional authentication methods (session-based):\n\n| Criteria | Session-Based | JWT-Based |\n| :------------------ | :----------------------------------------- | :---------------------------------------- |\n| **Server storage** | Requires session storage | No storage needed (stateless) |\n| **Scalability** | Hard to scale (needs shared session store) | Easy to scale (each server self-verifies) |\n| **Cross-domain** | Difficult (CORS issues) | Easy (token in header) |\n| **Mobile-friendly** | Complex with native apps | Simple, just send token |\n| **Microservices** | Needs shared session store | Each service self-verifies |\n\n**Real-world example:**\n\n```javascript\n// Client sends login request\nconst response = await fetch(\"/api/login\", {\n method: \"POST\",\n headers: { \"Content-Type\": \"application/json\" },\n body: JSON.stringify({ email, password }),\n});\n\nconst { accessToken } = await response.json();\n\n// Then client uses token for requests\nconst data = await fetch(\"/api/protected-resource\", {\n headers: {\n Authorization: `Bearer ${accessToken}`,\n },\n});\n```\n\nThe server doesn't need to store anything about the session. Every time it receives a request with JWT, the server just needs to verify the signature and read information from the payload.\n\n---\n\n## Part 2: Access Token vs Refresh Token\n\n### 2.1 Why Do We Need Two Types of Tokens?\n\nA common question: if JWT already contains all the information, why not use a single token?\n\n**Problems with a single token:**\n\n- If token has long expiry time (e.g., 30 days) \u2192 User doesn't need to login again but **high security risk** if token is stolen\n- If token has short expiry time (e.g., 15 minutes) \u2192 **More secure** but user must login constantly \u2192 Bad UX\n\n**Solution: Dual Token Strategy**\n\nUse a combination of 2 token types with different purposes and lifecycles:\n\n### 2.2 Access Token\n\n**Characteristics:**\n\n- **Short expiry time**: 5-15 minutes\n- **Purpose**: Access protected resources (API endpoints)\n- **Storage**: In memory (JavaScript variable) or sessionStorage\n- **Risk**: Low because expires quickly\n\n**Payload example:**\n\n```json\n{\n \"sub\": \"user123\",\n \"role\": \"user\",\n \"permissions\": [\"read:posts\", \"write:comments\"],\n \"iat\": 1710000000,\n \"exp\": 1710000900 // 15 minutes later\n}\n```\n\n### 2.3 Refresh Token\n\n**Characteristics:**\n\n- **Long expiry time**: 7-30 days\n- **Purpose**: Generate new access token when access token expires\n- **Storage**: HttpOnly cookie (most secure)\n- **Risk**: Higher but has preventive mechanisms (token rotation)\n\n**Payload example:**\n\n```json\n{\n \"sub\": \"user123\",\n \"tokenFamily\": \"abc123\", // To detect reuse attacks\n \"iat\": 1710000000,\n \"exp\": 1712592000 // 30 days later\n}\n```\n\n### 2.4 Detailed Comparison\n\n| Feature | Access Token | Refresh Token |\n| :-------------- | :------------------------- | :-------------------------- |\n| **Purpose** | Access API | Renew access token |\n| **Expiry** | Short (5-15 mins) | Long (7-30 days) |\n| **Sent to** | Every API request | Only `/refresh` endpoint |\n| **Storage** | Memory/sessionStorage | HttpOnly cookie |\n| **Can revoke?** | No (expires automatically) | Yes (revoke list on server) |\n| **Size** | Larger (more claims) | Smaller (fewer claims) |\n\n### 2.5 Complete Workflow\n\n```\n\u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510 \u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510\n\u2502 Client \u2502 \u2502 Server \u2502\n\u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u252c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518 \u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u252c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518\n \u2502 \u2502\n \u2502 1. POST /login (email, password) \u2502\n \u2502\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500>\u2502\n \u2502 \u2502\n \u2502 2. Access Token + Refresh Token \u2502\n \u2502 (Refresh via httpOnly cookie) \u2502\n \u2502<\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2502\n \u2502 \u2502\n \u2502 3. GET /api/posts \u2502\n \u2502 Authorization: Bearer \u2502\n \u2502\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500>\u2502\n \u2502 \u2502\n \u2502 4. Response data \u2502\n \u2502<\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2502\n \u2502 \u2502\n \u2502 [15 minutes later - access token expires] \u2502\n \u2502 \u2502\n \u2502 5. GET /api/posts \u2502\n \u2502 Authorization: Bearer \u2502\n \u2502\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500>\u2502\n \u2502 \u2502\n \u2502 6. 401 Unauthorized \u2502\n \u2502<\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2502\n \u2502 \u2502\n \u2502 7. POST /refresh \u2502\n \u2502 (Cookie: refresh_token automatic) \u2502\n \u2502\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500>\u2502\n \u2502 \u2502\n \u2502 8. New Access Token \u2502\n \u2502<\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2502\n \u2502 \u2502\n \u2502 9. Retry GET /api/posts \u2502\n \u2502 Authorization: Bearer \u2502\n \u2502\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500>\u2502\n \u2502 \u2502\n \u2502 10. Response data \u2502\n \u2502<\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2502\n```\n\n---\n\n## Part 3: Token Storage - Security Tradeoffs\n\n### 3.1 The Most Important Question\n\n**Where to store tokens?** This is a decision that directly impacts application security. There are 3 common options:\n\n1. LocalStorage\n2. SessionStorage\n3. HttpOnly Cookies\n\nEach method has its own security tradeoffs. No solution is 100% perfect.\n\n### 3.2 Option 1: LocalStorage\n\n**How it works:**\n\n```javascript\n// Store token\nlocalStorage.setItem(\"accessToken\", token);\n\n// Read token\nconst token = localStorage.getItem(\"accessToken\");\n\n// Use it\nfetch(\"/api/data\", {\n headers: {\n Authorization: `Bearer ${token}`,\n },\n});\n```\n\n**Advantages:**\n\n- \u2705 Simple, easy to implement\n- \u2705 Persists after closing browser (user doesn't need to login again)\n- \u2705 Can be accessed from JavaScript\n\n**Disadvantages:**\n\n- \u274c **Vulnerable to XSS attacks** (Cross-Site Scripting)\n- \u274c Any script on the page can read it\n- \u274c Doesn't auto expire when closing tab\n\n**When to use:**\n\n- Simple app, no user-generated content\n- Strong XSS protection already in place\n- Convenience more important than maximum security\n\n### 3.3 Option 2: SessionStorage\n\n**How it works:**\n\n```javascript\n// Like localStorage but clears when tab closes\nsessionStorage.setItem(\"accessToken\", token);\nconst token = sessionStorage.getItem(\"accessToken\");\n```\n\n**Advantages:**\n\n- \u2705 Auto clears when closing tab/window\n- \u2705 Slightly better than localStorage (session-only)\n\n**Disadvantages:**\n\n- \u274c Still vulnerable to XSS attacks\n- \u274c Worse UX (must login again for each new tab)\n- \u274c Doesn't work with multi-tab scenarios\n\n**When to use:**\n\n- App requires higher security than localStorage\n- Accept UX trade-off (re-login each session)\n\n### 3.4 Option 3: HttpOnly Cookies (Recommended)\n\n**How it works:**\n\n```javascript\n// Server-side: Set cookie on login\nres.cookie(\"refreshToken\", token, {\n httpOnly: true, // JavaScript CANNOT access\n secure: true, // Only send over HTTPS\n sameSite: \"strict\", // Prevent CSRF\n maxAge: 7 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000, // 7 days\n});\n\n// Client-side: Cookie automatically sent with every request\n// Developer doesn't need to do anything!\n```\n\n**Advantages:**\n\n- \u2705 **Cannot be accessed from JavaScript** \u2192 Immune to XSS\n- \u2705 Automatically sent with every request (no code needed)\n- \u2705 `sameSite` attribute prevents CSRF attacks\n- \u2705 Server controls expiry and revocation\n\n**Disadvantages:**\n\n- \u274c **Can still be vulnerable to CSRF attacks** if misconfigured\n- \u274c Doesn't work with cross-domain requests (needs careful CORS setup)\n- \u274c More complex with mobile apps and third-party clients\n\n**When to use:**\n\n- Production applications with high security requirements\n- Web apps (not pure API servers)\n- Control both frontend and backend\n\n### 3.5 Best Practice: Hybrid Approach\n\n**Best strategy:**\n\n```\n\u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510\n\u2502 Dual Token Strategy \u2502\n\u251c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2524\n\u2502 \u2502\n\u2502 Access Token (short-lived): \u2502\n\u2502 \u2192 Store in memory (JS variable) \u2502\n\u2502 \u2192 Or sessionStorage \u2502\n\u2502 \u2192 Use for API requests \u2502\n\u2502 \u2502\n\u2502 Refresh Token (long-lived): \u2502\n\u2502 \u2192 Store in httpOnly cookie \u2502\n\u2502 \u2192 Only send to /refresh endpoint \u2502\n\u2502 \u2192 Server can revoke \u2502\n\u2502 \u2502\n\u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518\n```\n\n**Implementation:**\n\n```javascript\n// Client-side: Token management service\nclass TokenService {\n // Access token in memory (only exists during session)\n #accessToken = null;\n\n setAccessToken(token) {\n this.#accessToken = token;\n }\n\n getAccessToken() {\n return this.#accessToken;\n }\n\n clearAccessToken() {\n this.#accessToken = null;\n }\n\n // Refresh token is set by server via httpOnly cookie\n // Client doesn't need to manage it!\n}\n\n// Auto-refresh logic\nasync function fetchWithAuth(url, options = {}) {\n const accessToken = tokenService.getAccessToken();\n\n let response = await fetch(url, {\n ...options,\n headers: {\n ...options.headers,\n Authorization: `Bearer ${accessToken}`,\n },\n });\n\n // If 401, try to refresh\n if (response.status === 401) {\n const newToken = await refreshAccessToken();\n tokenService.setAccessToken(newToken);\n\n // Retry request with new token\n response = await fetch(url, {\n ...options,\n headers: {\n ...options.headers,\n Authorization: `Bearer ${newToken}`,\n },\n });\n }\n\n return response;\n}\n\nasync function refreshAccessToken() {\n // Refresh token automatically sent via cookie\n const response = await fetch(\"/api/refresh\", {\n method: \"POST\",\n credentials: \"include\", // Send cookies\n });\n\n const { accessToken } = await response.json();\n return accessToken;\n}\n```\n\n### 3.6 Security Comparison\n\n| Storage Method | XSS Protection | CSRF Protection | Best For |\n| :------------------ | :------------: | :-------------: | :-------------- |\n| **localStorage** | \u274c Vulnerable | \u2705 Safe | Simple apps |\n| **sessionStorage** | \u274c Vulnerable | \u2705 Safe | Short sessions |\n| **httpOnly Cookie** | \u2705 Protected | \u26a0\ufe0f Needs config | Production apps |\n| **Memory only** | \u2705 Protected | \u2705 Protected | Access tokens |\n| **Hybrid** | \u2705 Protected | \u2705 Protected | **Recommended** |\n\n---\n\n## Part 4: Token Refresh Flow - Detailed Implementation\n\n### 4.1 Why Do We Need a Refresh Mechanism?\n\nSuppose your access token expires after 15 minutes:\n\n- **Without refresh:** User must login again after every 15 minutes \u2192 Bad UX\n- **With refresh:** App automatically renews token, user is not interrupted\n\nThe refresh flow is the bridge between security (short-lived tokens) and UX (seamless authentication).\n\n### 4.2 Basic Refresh Flow\n\n**Step-by-step:**\n\n```\n1. User login\n \u2193\n2. Server creates access token (15 min) + refresh token (7 days)\n \u2193\n3. Client stores access token (memory)\n Server sets refresh token (httpOnly cookie)\n \u2193\n4. Client uses access token for all API requests\n \u2193\n5. Access token expires \u2192 API returns 401\n \u2193\n6. Client calls /refresh endpoint (automatically sends refresh token via cookie)\n \u2193\n7. Server verifies refresh token \u2192 creates new access token\n \u2193\n8. Client stores new access token and retries failed request\n```\n\n### 4.3 Server-Side Implementation\n\n**Backend (Node.js + Express):**\n\n```javascript\nconst express = require(\"express\");\nconst jwt = require(\"jsonwebtoken\");\nconst cookieParser = require(\"cookie-parser\");\n\nconst app = express();\napp.use(cookieParser());\napp.use(express.json());\n\n// Secret keys (MUST store in environment variables!)\nconst ACCESS_SECRET = process.env.ACCESS_SECRET;\nconst REFRESH_SECRET = process.env.REFRESH_SECRET;\n\n// Token storage (production: use Redis)\nconst refreshTokens = new Set();\n\n// 1. Login endpoint\napp.post(\"/api/login\", async (req, res) => {\n const { email, password } = req.body;\n\n // Verify credentials (simplified)\n const user = await verifyCredentials(email, password);\n if (!user) {\n return res.status(401).json({ error: \"Invalid credentials\" });\n }\n\n // Generate tokens\n const accessToken = jwt.sign(\n {\n sub: user.id,\n email: user.email,\n role: user.role,\n },\n ACCESS_SECRET,\n { expiresIn: \"15m\" },\n );\n\n const refreshToken = jwt.sign({ sub: user.id }, REFRESH_SECRET, {\n expiresIn: \"7d\",\n });\n\n // Store refresh token (production: Redis with expiry)\n refreshTokens.add(refreshToken);\n\n // Set refresh token in httpOnly cookie\n res.cookie(\"refreshToken\", refreshToken, {\n httpOnly: true,\n secure: process.env.NODE_ENV === \"production\",\n sameSite: \"strict\",\n maxAge: 7 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000, // 7 days\n });\n\n // Return access token in response body\n res.json({ accessToken });\n});\n\n// 2. Refresh endpoint\napp.post(\"/api/refresh\", (req, res) => {\n const refreshToken = req.cookies.refreshToken;\n\n if (!refreshToken) {\n return res.status(401).json({ error: \"No refresh token\" });\n }\n\n // Verify refresh token is still valid\n if (!refreshTokens.has(refreshToken)) {\n return res.status(403).json({ error: \"Invalid refresh token\" });\n }\n\n try {\n // Verify JWT signature\n const payload = jwt.verify(refreshToken, REFRESH_SECRET);\n\n // Generate new access token\n const newAccessToken = jwt.sign(\n {\n sub: payload.sub,\n email: payload.email,\n role: payload.role,\n },\n ACCESS_SECRET,\n { expiresIn: \"15m\" },\n );\n\n res.json({ accessToken: newAccessToken });\n } catch (error) {\n return res.status(403).json({ error: \"Invalid or expired token\" });\n }\n});\n\n// 3. Protected endpoint example\napp.get(\"/api/protected\", verifyAccessToken, (req, res) => {\n res.json({\n message: \"Protected data\",\n user: req.user,\n });\n});\n\n// 4. Logout endpoint\napp.post(\"/api/logout\", (req, res) => {\n const refreshToken = req.cookies.refreshToken;\n\n // Remove from whitelist\n refreshTokens.delete(refreshToken);\n\n // Clear cookie\n res.clearCookie(\"refreshToken\");\n\n res.json({ message: \"Logged out\" });\n});\n\n// Middleware to verify access token\nfunction verifyAccessToken(req, res, next) {\n const authHeader = req.headers.authorization;\n\n if (!authHeader || !authHeader.startsWith(\"Bearer \")) {\n return res.status(401).json({ error: \"No access token\" });\n }\n\n const token = authHeader.substring(7);\n\n try {\n const payload = jwt.verify(token, ACCESS_SECRET);\n req.user = payload;\n next();\n } catch (error) {\n return res.status(401).json({ error: \"Invalid or expired access token\" });\n }\n}\n```\n\n### 4.4 Client-Side Implementation\n\n**Frontend (React with Axios):**\n\n```javascript\nimport axios from \"axios\";\n\n// Axios instance with interceptors\nconst api = axios.create({\n baseURL: \"http://localhost:3000/api\",\n withCredentials: true, // Send cookies\n});\n\n// Store access token in memory\nlet accessToken = null;\n\nexport function setAccessToken(token) {\n accessToken = token;\n}\n\nexport function getAccessToken() {\n return accessToken;\n}\n\n// Request interceptor: automatically add Authorization header\napi.interceptors.request.use(\n (config) => {\n if (accessToken) {\n config.headers.Authorization = `Bearer ${accessToken}`;\n }\n return config;\n },\n (error) => Promise.reject(error),\n);\n\n// Response interceptor: automatically refresh on 401\napi.interceptors.response.use(\n (response) => response, // Success case: do nothing\n async (error) => {\n const originalRequest = error.config;\n\n // If 401 error and not retried yet\n if (error.response?.status === 401 && !originalRequest._retry) {\n originalRequest._retry = true;\n\n try {\n // Call refresh endpoint\n const response = await axios.post(\n \"http://localhost:3000/api/refresh\",\n {},\n { withCredentials: true },\n );\n\n const newAccessToken = response.data.accessToken;\n setAccessToken(newAccessToken);\n\n // Retry request with new token\n originalRequest.headers.Authorization = `Bearer ${newAccessToken}`;\n return api(originalRequest);\n } catch (refreshError) {\n // Refresh failed \u2192 logout user\n setAccessToken(null);\n window.location.href = \"/login\";\n return Promise.reject(refreshError);\n }\n }\n\n return Promise.reject(error);\n },\n);\n\n// Login function\nexport async function login(email, password) {\n const response = await api.post(\"/login\", { email, password });\n const { accessToken } = response.data;\n setAccessToken(accessToken);\n return response.data;\n}\n\n// Logout function\nexport async function logout() {\n await api.post(\"/logout\");\n setAccessToken(null);\n}\n\nexport default api;\n```\n\n**Usage in React components:**\n\n```javascript\nimport React, { useEffect, useState } from \"react\";\nimport api from \"./apiClient\";\n\nfunction Dashboard() {\n const [data, setData] = useState(null);\n\n useEffect(() => {\n // Call protected API - auto refresh if needed\n api\n .get(\"/protected\")\n .then((res) => setData(res.data))\n .catch((err) => console.error(err));\n }, []);\n\n return
{data && 
{JSON.stringify(data, null, 2)}
}
;\n}\n```\n\n### 4.5 Advanced: Token Rotation\n\n**Problem with basic refresh:**\n\nIf a refresh token is stolen, the attacker can use it to generate access tokens continuously until the refresh token expires (7-30 days).\n\n**Solution: Refresh Token Rotation**\n\nEach time refresh is called, the server:\n\n1. Verifies old refresh token\n2. Generates new access token\n3. **Generates new refresh token** (replaces old token)\n4. Revokes old refresh token\n\n```javascript\n// Server: refresh with rotation\napp.post(\"/api/refresh\", async (req, res) => {\n const oldRefreshToken = req.cookies.refreshToken;\n\n if (!refreshTokens.has(oldRefreshToken)) {\n return res.status(403).json({ error: \"Invalid refresh token\" });\n }\n\n try {\n const payload = jwt.verify(oldRefreshToken, REFRESH_SECRET);\n\n // Generate NEW tokens\n const newAccessToken = jwt.sign(\n { sub: payload.sub, email: payload.email, role: payload.role },\n ACCESS_SECRET,\n { expiresIn: \"15m\" },\n );\n\n const newRefreshToken = jwt.sign({ sub: payload.sub }, REFRESH_SECRET, {\n expiresIn: \"7d\",\n });\n\n // Rotate: delete old, add new\n refreshTokens.delete(oldRefreshToken);\n refreshTokens.add(newRefreshToken);\n\n // Set new refresh token cookie\n res.cookie(\"refreshToken\", newRefreshToken, {\n httpOnly: true,\n secure: true,\n sameSite: \"strict\",\n maxAge: 7 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000,\n });\n\n res.json({ accessToken: newAccessToken });\n } catch (error) {\n return res.status(403).json({ error: \"Invalid token\" });\n }\n});\n```\n\n**Benefits:**\n\n- \u2705 Reduces time window for token theft\n- \u2705 Detects reuse attacks (old token already revoked)\n- \u2705 Automatic cleanup of expired tokens\n\n---\n\n## Part 5: Security Concerns - What You Need to Know\n\n### 5.1 XSS (Cross-Site Scripting) Attacks\n\n**Threat scenario:**\n\nAttacker injects malicious script into website:\n\n```html\n\n\n```\n\n**Mitigation strategies:**\n\n1. **Don't store sensitive tokens in localStorage**\n\n ```javascript\n // \u274c BAD\n localStorage.setItem(\"accessToken\", token);\n\n // \u2705 GOOD - use memory or httpOnly cookie\n let accessToken = null; // Memory variable\n ```\n\n2. **Content Security Policy (CSP)**\n\n ```javascript\n // Server response headers\n app.use((req, res, next) => {\n res.setHeader(\n \"Content-Security-Policy\",\n \"default-src 'self'; script-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline'\",\n );\n next();\n });\n ```\n\n3. **Sanitize user input**\n\n ```javascript\n import DOMPurify from \"dompurify\";\n\n // Before rendering user content\n const cleanHTML = DOMPurify.sanitize(userInput);\n ```\n\n4. **HttpOnly cookies for refresh tokens**\n ```javascript\n res.cookie(\"refreshToken\", token, {\n httpOnly: true, // JavaScript cannot access\n secure: true,\n sameSite: \"strict\",\n });\n ```\n\n### 5.2 CSRF (Cross-Site Request Forgery) Attacks\n\n**Threat scenario:**\n\nUser is logged into `yourbank.com`. Attacker sends email with link:\n\n```html\n\n\n```\n\nBrowser automatically sends user's cookies \u2192 Request is executed!\n\n**Mitigation strategies:**\n\n1. **SameSite Cookie Attribute**\n\n ```javascript\n res.cookie(\"refreshToken\", token, {\n httpOnly: true,\n secure: true,\n sameSite: \"strict\", // Or 'lax'\n });\n ```\n\n | SameSite Value | Protection | Use Case |\n | :------------- | :--------- | :------------------------------------------------ |\n | `strict` | Strongest | Cookie NOT sent with cross-site requests |\n | `lax` | Medium | Cookie sent with top-level navigations (GET only) |\n | `none` | Weakest | Cookie sent with all requests (requires HTTPS) |\n\n2. **CSRF Token Pattern**\n\n ```javascript\n // Server: generate CSRF token\n const csrfToken = generateRandomToken();\n req.session.csrfToken = csrfToken;\n\n // Client: send token in header or form\n fetch(\"/api/transfer\", {\n method: \"POST\",\n headers: {\n \"X-CSRF-Token\": csrfToken,\n },\n body: JSON.stringify({ to, amount }),\n });\n\n // Server: verify token\n function verifyCsrfToken(req, res, next) {\n const token = req.headers[\"x-csrf-token\"];\n if (token !== req.session.csrfToken) {\n return res.status(403).json({ error: \"Invalid CSRF token\" });\n }\n next();\n }\n ```\n\n3. **Double Submit Cookie Pattern**\n\n ```javascript\n // Simpler: no session storage needed\n // Server sets CSRF token in cookie (readable from JS)\n res.cookie(\"csrf-token\", csrfToken, {\n httpOnly: false, // Client needs to read it\n secure: true,\n sameSite: \"strict\",\n });\n\n // Client reads from cookie and sends back in header\n const csrfToken = getCookie(\"csrf-token\");\n fetch(\"/api/action\", {\n headers: {\n \"X-CSRF-Token\": csrfToken,\n },\n });\n ```\n\n### 5.3 JWT Security Best Practices\n\n#### 5.3.1 Secret Key Management\n\n```javascript\n// \u274c NEVER hardcode secrets\nconst SECRET = \"mySecretKey123\";\n\n// \u2705 Use environment variables\nconst SECRET = process.env.JWT_SECRET;\n\n// \u2705 Use strong secrets (32+ characters, random)\n// openssl rand -base64 32\nconst SECRET = \"Xy7K9mP4vN2qW8tE6rA3sD5fG7hJ1kL4\";\n```\n\n#### 5.3.2 Token Expiry Time\n\n```javascript\n// \u274c Access token too long\njwt.sign(payload, SECRET, { expiresIn: \"30d\" });\n\n// \u2705 Access token short\njwt.sign(payload, ACCESS_SECRET, { expiresIn: \"15m\" });\n\n// \u2705 Refresh token longer but with rotation\njwt.sign(payload, REFRESH_SECRET, { expiresIn: \"7d\" });\n```\n\n#### 5.3.3 Sensitive Data in Payload\n\n```javascript\n// \u274c NEVER store sensitive data\nconst payload = {\n userId: user.id,\n email: user.email,\n password: user.password, // \u274c DANGEROUS!\n creditCard: user.creditCard, // \u274c DANGEROUS!\n ssn: user.ssn, // \u274c DANGEROUS!\n};\n\n// \u2705 Only store identifiers and public info\nconst payload = {\n sub: user.id, // User ID\n email: user.email, // Public info\n role: user.role, // Authorization info\n iat: Date.now(),\n};\n```\n\n**Reason:** JWT can be easily decoded (base64):\n\n```javascript\n// Anyone can decode JWT\nconst [header, payload, signature] = token.split(\".\");\nconst decodedPayload = JSON.parse(atob(payload));\nconsole.log(decodedPayload); // Everything is readable!\n```\n\n#### 5.3.4 Algorithm Confusion Attack\n\n```javascript\n// \u274c Don't verify algorithm\njwt.verify(token, SECRET);\n\n// \u2705 Specify algorithms explicitly\njwt.verify(token, SECRET, {\n algorithms: [\"HS256\"], // Only accept HS256\n});\n\n// \u274c NEVER use 'none' algorithm in production\n// Attacker can create unsigned tokens\n```\n\n#### 5.3.5 Token Revocation Strategy\n\nJWT is **stateless** \u2192 Cannot revoke a specific token. Solutions:\n\n**Option 1: Blacklist** (Redis)\n\n```javascript\n// On logout or fraud detection\nawait redis.setex(`blacklist:${tokenId}`, TTL, \"1\");\n\n// Verify middleware checks blacklist\nasync function verifyToken(req, res, next) {\n const token = extractToken(req);\n const payload = jwt.verify(token, SECRET);\n\n // Check blacklist\n const isBlacklisted = await redis.exists(`blacklist:${payload.jti}`);\n if (isBlacklisted) {\n return res.status(401).json({ error: \"Token revoked\" });\n }\n\n req.user = payload;\n next();\n}\n```\n\n**Option 2: Whitelist** (for refresh tokens)\n\n```javascript\n// Only accept refresh tokens in whitelist\nconst validRefreshTokens = new Set();\n\n// Add on login\nvalidRefreshTokens.add(refreshToken);\n\n// Check on refresh\nif (!validRefreshTokens.has(refreshToken)) {\n return res.status(403).json({ error: \"Invalid token\" });\n}\n\n// Remove on logout\nvalidRefreshTokens.delete(refreshToken);\n```\n\n**Option 3: Short expiry + refresh rotation**\n\n- Access token short (5-15 min) \u2192 Expires quickly\n- Refresh token has rotation \u2192 Old tokens automatically invalid\n\n### 5.4 HTTPS is Mandatory\n\n```javascript\n// \u274c NEVER use JWT over HTTP\n// Tokens can be intercepted in transit\n\n// \u2705 Force HTTPS in production\nif (process.env.NODE_ENV === \"production\" && !req.secure) {\n return res.redirect(\"https://\" + req.headers.host + req.url);\n}\n\n// \u2705 Set secure flag for cookies\nres.cookie(\"refreshToken\", token, {\n httpOnly: true,\n secure: true, // Only send over HTTPS\n sameSite: \"strict\",\n});\n```\n\n### 5.5 Rate Limiting\n\n```javascript\nconst rateLimit = require(\"express-rate-limit\");\n\n// Limit login attempts\nconst loginLimiter = rateLimit({\n windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutes\n max: 5, // Max 5 requests\n message: \"Too many login attempts, please try again later\",\n});\n\napp.post(\"/api/login\", loginLimiter, handleLogin);\n\n// Limit refresh attempts\nconst refreshLimiter = rateLimit({\n windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000,\n max: 10,\n message: \"Too many refresh attempts\",\n});\n\napp.post(\"/api/refresh\", refreshLimiter, handleRefresh);\n```\n\n### 5.6 Security Checklist\n\nBefore deploying JWT authentication:\n\n- [ ] Access tokens have short expiry (\u2264 15 minutes)\n- [ ] Refresh tokens use httpOnly cookies\n- [ ] Secret keys stored in environment variables (not hardcoded)\n- [ ] Secret keys are strong (32+ characters, random)\n- [ ] HTTPS enforced in production\n- [ ] sameSite='strict' for cookies\n- [ ] CSRF protection enabled\n- [ ] Content Security Policy headers configured\n- [ ] User input is sanitized (prevent XSS)\n- [ ] Rate limiting for login and refresh endpoints\n- [ ] Token rotation implemented for refresh tokens\n- [ ] Logging and monitoring for suspicious activities\n- [ ] Sensitive data NOT stored in JWT payload\n- [ ] Algorithm explicitly specified when verifying\n- [ ] Blacklist/whitelist mechanism for revocation\n\n---\n\n## Conclusion\n\nJWT authentication is a powerful tool but needs to be implemented carefully. Key takeaways:\n\n**1. Dual Token Strategy**\n\n- Short access token (15 minutes) in memory\n- Long refresh token (7 days) in httpOnly cookie\n- Combines both security and UX\n\n**2. Storage Matters**\n\n- **DON'T** store tokens in localStorage (XSS vulnerability)\n- **DO** use httpOnly cookies for refresh tokens\n- **DO** use memory variables for access tokens\n\n**3. Refresh Flow**\n\n- Auto-refresh when access token expires\n- Token rotation to reduce risk\n- Proper error handling and retry logic\n\n**4. Security First**\n\n- HTTPS mandatory\n- Strong secrets in environment variables\n- CSRF protection with sameSite cookies\n- XSS protection with CSP and input sanitization\n- Rate limiting for sensitive endpoints\n- Token revocation strategy\n\n**5. Production Checklist**\n\n- Environment variables for secrets\n- Short expiry times\n- Proper cookie configuration\n- HTTPS enforcement\n- Monitoring and logging\n\nJWT is not a silver bullet for every use case, but when implemented correctly with these best practices, it's a powerful, scalable, and secure authentication solution for modern web applications.\n\n---\n\n**Next Steps:**\n\n- Implement JWT authentication in your project\n- Set up proper testing for authentication flows\n- Monitor security logs for suspicious activities\n- Consider OAuth 2.0 for third-party integrations\n- Explore alternative authentication methods (OAuth, SAML, WebAuthn)\n\n**Resources:**\n\n- [RFC 7519 - JWT Standard](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7519)\n- [OWASP JWT Security Cheat Sheet](https://cheatsheetseries.owasp.org/cheatsheets/JSON_Web_Token_for_Java_Cheat_Sheet.html)\n- [jwt.io - JWT Debugger](https://jwt.io/)\n"}, {"name": "blog-post-vi.md", "type": "text", "content": "# JWT Authentication: H\u01b0\u1edbng D\u1eabn To\u00e0n Di\u1ec7n V\u1ec1 X\u00e1c Th\u1ef1c Hi\u1ec7n \u0110\u1ea1i\n\n> **D\u00e0nh cho developers mu\u1ed1n hi\u1ec3u s\u00e2u v\u1ec1 JWT v\u00e0 implement authentication m\u1ed9t c\u00e1ch an to\u00e0n**\n\nX\u00e1c th\u1ef1c ng\u01b0\u1eddi d\u00f9ng (authentication) l\u00e0 n\u1ec1n t\u1ea3ng c\u1ee7a m\u1ecdi \u1ee9ng d\u1ee5ng web hi\u1ec7n \u0111\u1ea1i. Nh\u01b0ng l\u00e0m sao \u0111\u1ec3 x\u00e1c th\u1ef1c \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c an to\u00e0n, c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 m\u1edf r\u1ed9ng, v\u00e0 ho\u1ea1t \u0111\u1ed9ng t\u1ed1t trong m\u00f4i tr\u01b0\u1eddng ph\u00e2n t\u00e1n (distributed systems)? JSON Web Token (JWT) \u0111\u00e3 tr\u1edf th\u00e0nh gi\u1ea3i ph\u00e1p ph\u1ed5 bi\u1ebfn nh\u1ea5t cho v\u1ea5n \u0111\u1ec1 n\u00e0y. Trong b\u00e0i vi\u1ebft n\u00e0y, ch\u00fang ta s\u1ebd \u0111i s\u00e2u v\u00e0o JWT t\u1eeb nh\u1eefng kh\u00e1i ni\u1ec7m c\u01a1 b\u1ea3n \u0111\u1ebfn c\u00e1c best practices v\u1ec1 security.\n\n## Ph\u1ea7n 1: JWT L\u00e0 G\u00ec?\n\n### 1.1 \u0110\u1ecbnh Ngh\u0129a v\u00e0 C\u1ea5u Tr\u00fac\n\nJSON Web Token (JWT) l\u00e0 m\u1ed9t chu\u1ea9n m\u1edf (RFC 7519) \u0111\u1ec3 truy\u1ec1n t\u1ea3i th\u00f4ng tin m\u1ed9t c\u00e1ch an to\u00e0n gi\u1eefa c\u00e1c b\u00ean d\u01b0\u1edbi d\u1ea1ng JSON object. JWT \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c thi\u1ebft k\u1ebf \u0111\u1ec3 compact (nh\u1ecf g\u1ecdn), self-contained (t\u1ef1 ch\u1ee9a \u0111\u1ea7y \u0111\u1ee7 th\u00f4ng tin), v\u00e0 c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 verify \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c t\u00ednh to\u00e0n v\u1eb9n.\n\nM\u1ed9t JWT token g\u1ed3m 3 ph\u1ea7n, ng\u0103n c\u00e1ch b\u1edfi d\u1ea5u ch\u1ea5m (`.`):\n\n```\neyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9.eyJzdWIiOiIxMjM0NTY3ODkwIiwibmFtZSI6IkpvaG4gRG9lIiwiaWF0IjoxNTE2MjM5MDIyfQ.SflKxwRJSMeKKF2QT4fwpMeJf36POk6yJV_adQssw5c\n```\n\n**C\u1ea5u tr\u00fac:**\n\n```\nHEADER.PAYLOAD.SIGNATURE\n```\n\n#### Header (Ph\u1ea7n \u0111\u1ea7u)\n\nCh\u1ee9a th\u00f4ng tin v\u1ec1 lo\u1ea1i token v\u00e0 thu\u1eadt to\u00e1n m\u00e3 h\u00f3a:\n\n```json\n{\n \"alg\": \"HS256\",\n \"typ\": \"JWT\"\n}\n```\n\n#### Payload (Ph\u1ea7n d\u1eef li\u1ec7u)\n\nCh\u1ee9a c\u00e1c claims (th\u00f4ng tin v\u1ec1 user v\u00e0 metadata):\n\n```json\n{\n \"sub\": \"1234567890\",\n \"name\": \"John Doe\",\n \"email\": \"john@example.com\",\n \"role\": \"admin\",\n \"iat\": 1516239022,\n \"exp\": 1516242622\n}\n```\n\n#### Signature (Ch\u1eef k\u00fd)\n\n\u0110\u01b0\u1ee3c t\u1ea1o b\u1eb1ng c\u00e1ch m\u00e3 h\u00f3a header v\u00e0 payload v\u1edbi secret key:\n\n```\nHMACSHA256(\n base64UrlEncode(header) + \".\" +\n base64UrlEncode(payload),\n secret\n)\n```\n\n### 1.2 T\u1ea1i Sao JWT \u0110\u01b0\u1ee3c \u01afa Chu\u1ed9ng?\n\nJWT gi\u1ea3i quy\u1ebft nhi\u1ec1u v\u1ea5n \u0111\u1ec1 c\u1ee7a ph\u01b0\u01a1ng ph\u00e1p authentication truy\u1ec1n th\u1ed1ng (session-based):\n\n| Ti\u00eau Ch\u00ed | Session-Based | JWT-Based |\n| :------------------ | :---------------------------------- | :------------------------------ |\n| **L\u01b0u tr\u1eef server** | C\u1ea7n l\u01b0u session tr\u00ean server | Kh\u00f4ng c\u1ea7n l\u01b0u tr\u1eef (stateless) |\n| **Scalability** | Kh\u00f3 scale (c\u1ea7n session store chung) | D\u1ec5 scale (m\u1ed7i server t\u1ef1 verify) |\n| **Cross-domain** | Kh\u00f3 kh\u0103n (CORS issues) | D\u1ec5 d\u00e0ng (token trong header) |\n| **Mobile-friendly** | Ph\u1ee9c t\u1ea1p v\u1edbi native apps | \u0110\u01a1n gi\u1ea3n, ch\u1ec9 c\u1ea7n g\u1eedi token |\n| **Microservices** | C\u1ea7n shared session store | M\u1ed7i service t\u1ef1 verify |\n\n**V\u00ed d\u1ee5 th\u1ef1c t\u1ebf:**\n\n```javascript\n// Client g\u1eedi login request\nconst response = await fetch(\"/api/login\", {\n method: \"POST\",\n headers: { \"Content-Type\": \"application/json\" },\n body: JSON.stringify({ email, password }),\n});\n\nconst { accessToken } = await response.json();\n\n// Sau \u0111\u00f3 client s\u1eed d\u1ee5ng token cho c\u00e1c requests\nconst data = await fetch(\"/api/protected-resource\", {\n headers: {\n Authorization: `Bearer ${accessToken}`,\n },\n});\n```\n\nServer kh\u00f4ng c\u1ea7n l\u01b0u g\u00ec v\u1ec1 session. M\u1ed7i khi nh\u1eadn request v\u1edbi JWT, server ch\u1ec9 c\u1ea7n verify signature v\u00e0 \u0111\u1ecdc th\u00f4ng tin t\u1eeb payload.\n\n---\n\n## Ph\u1ea7n 2: Access Token vs Refresh Token\n\n### 2.1 T\u1ea1i Sao C\u1ea7n Hai Lo\u1ea1i Token?\n\nM\u1ed9t c\u00e2u h\u1ecfi ph\u1ed5 bi\u1ebfn: n\u1ebfu JWT \u0111\u00e3 ch\u1ee9a \u0111\u1ee7 th\u00f4ng tin, t\u1ea1i sao kh\u00f4ng d\u00f9ng m\u1ed9t token duy nh\u1ea5t?\n\n**V\u1ea5n \u0111\u1ec1 v\u1edbi single token:**\n\n- N\u1ebfu token c\u00f3 expiry time d\u00e0i (vd: 30 ng\u00e0y) \u2192 User kh\u00f4ng c\u1ea7n login l\u1ea1i nh\u01b0ng **r\u1ee7i ro security cao** n\u1ebfu token b\u1ecb \u0111\u00e1nh c\u1eafp\n- N\u1ebfu token c\u00f3 expiry time ng\u1eafn (vd: 15 ph\u00fat) \u2192 **An to\u00e0n h\u01a1n** nh\u01b0ng user ph\u1ea3i login li\u00ean t\u1ee5c \u2192 UX t\u1ec7\n\n**Gi\u1ea3i ph\u00e1p: Dual Token Strategy**\n\nS\u1eed d\u1ee5ng k\u1ebft h\u1ee3p 2 lo\u1ea1i token v\u1edbi m\u1ee5c \u0111\u00edch v\u00e0 lifecycle kh\u00e1c nhau:\n\n### 2.2 Access Token (Token Truy C\u1eadp)\n\n**\u0110\u1eb7c \u0111i\u1ec3m:**\n\n- **Expiry time ng\u1eafn**: 5-15 ph\u00fat\n- **C\u00f4ng d\u1ee5ng**: Truy c\u1eadp protected resources (API endpoints)\n- **L\u01b0u tr\u1eef**: Trong memory (JavaScript variable) ho\u1eb7c sessionStorage\n- **R\u1ee7i ro**: Th\u1ea5p v\u00ec expire nhanh\n\n**V\u00ed d\u1ee5 payload:**\n\n```json\n{\n \"sub\": \"user123\",\n \"role\": \"user\",\n \"permissions\": [\"read:posts\", \"write:comments\"],\n \"iat\": 1710000000,\n \"exp\": 1710000900 // 15 ph\u00fat sau\n}\n```\n\n### 2.3 Refresh Token (Token L\u00e0m M\u1edbi)\n\n**\u0110\u1eb7c \u0111i\u1ec3m:**\n\n- **Expiry time d\u00e0i**: 7-30 ng\u00e0y\n- **C\u00f4ng d\u1ee5ng**: Generate access token m\u1edbi khi access token h\u1ebft h\u1ea1n\n- **L\u01b0u tr\u1eef**: HttpOnly cookie (an to\u00e0n nh\u1ea5t)\n- **R\u1ee7i ro**: Cao h\u01a1n nh\u01b0ng c\u00f3 c\u01a1 ch\u1ebf ph\u00f2ng ng\u1eeba (token rotation)\n\n**V\u00ed d\u1ee5 payload:**\n\n```json\n{\n \"sub\": \"user123\",\n \"tokenFamily\": \"abc123\", // \u0110\u1ec3 detect reuse attacks\n \"iat\": 1710000000,\n \"exp\": 1712592000 // 30 ng\u00e0y sau\n}\n```\n\n### 2.4 So S\u00e1nh Chi Ti\u1ebft\n\n| \u0110\u1eb7c \u0110i\u1ec3m | Access Token | Refresh Token |\n| :----------------- | :--------------------- | :--------------------------- |\n| **M\u1ee5c \u0111\u00edch** | Truy c\u1eadp API | Renew access token |\n| **Expiry** | Ng\u1eafn (5-15 ph\u00fat) | D\u00e0i (7-30 ng\u00e0y) |\n| **G\u1eedi \u0111\u1ebfn** | M\u1ecdi API request | Ch\u1ec9 `/refresh` endpoint |\n| **L\u01b0u tr\u1eef** | Memory/sessionStorage | HttpOnly cookie |\n| **C\u00f3 th\u1ec3 revoke?** | Kh\u00f4ng (expire t\u1ef1 \u0111\u1ed9ng) | C\u00f3 (revoke list tr\u00ean server) |\n| **K\u00edch th\u01b0\u1edbc** | L\u1edbn h\u01a1n (nhi\u1ec1u claims) | Nh\u1ecf h\u01a1n (\u00edt claims) |\n\n### 2.5 Workflow Ho\u00e0n Ch\u1ec9nh\n\n```\n\u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510 \u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510\n\u2502 Client \u2502 \u2502 Server \u2502\n\u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u252c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518 \u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u252c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518\n \u2502 \u2502\n \u2502 1. POST /login (email, password) \u2502\n \u2502\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500>\u2502\n \u2502 \u2502\n \u2502 2. Access Token + Refresh Token \u2502\n \u2502 (Refresh via httpOnly cookie) \u2502\n \u2502<\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2502\n \u2502 \u2502\n \u2502 3. GET /api/posts \u2502\n \u2502 Authorization: Bearer \u2502\n \u2502\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500>\u2502\n \u2502 \u2502\n \u2502 4. Response data \u2502\n \u2502<\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2502\n \u2502 \u2502\n \u2502 [15 ph\u00fat sau - access token h\u1ebft h\u1ea1n] \u2502\n \u2502 \u2502\n \u2502 5. GET /api/posts \u2502\n \u2502 Authorization: Bearer \u2502\n \u2502\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500>\u2502\n \u2502 \u2502\n \u2502 6. 401 Unauthorized \u2502\n \u2502<\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2502\n \u2502 \u2502\n \u2502 7. POST /refresh \u2502\n \u2502 (Cookie: refresh_token t\u1ef1 \u0111\u1ed9ng) \u2502\n \u2502\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500>\u2502\n \u2502 \u2502\n \u2502 8. New Access Token \u2502\n \u2502<\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2502\n \u2502 \u2502\n \u2502 9. Retry GET /api/posts \u2502\n \u2502 Authorization: Bearer \u2502\n \u2502\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500>\u2502\n \u2502 \u2502\n \u2502 10. Response data \u2502\n \u2502<\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2502\n```\n\n---\n\n## Ph\u1ea7n 3: N\u01a1i L\u01b0u Tr\u1eef Tokens - Security Tradeoffs\n\n### 3.1 V\u1ea5n \u0110\u1ec1 Quan Tr\u1ecdng Nh\u1ea5t\n\n**L\u01b0u tokens \u1edf \u0111\u00e2u?** \u0110\u00e2y l\u00e0 quy\u1ebft \u0111\u1ecbnh \u1ea3nh h\u01b0\u1edfng tr\u1ef1c ti\u1ebfp \u0111\u1ebfn security c\u1ee7a application. C\u00f3 3 options ph\u1ed5 bi\u1ebfn:\n\n1. LocalStorage\n2. SessionStorage\n3. HttpOnly Cookies\n\nM\u1ed7i c\u00e1ch c\u00f3 security tradeoffs ri\u00eang. Kh\u00f4ng c\u00f3 gi\u1ea3i ph\u00e1p n\u00e0o ho\u00e0n h\u1ea3o 100%.\n\n### 3.2 Option 1: LocalStorage\n\n**C\u00e1ch ho\u1ea1t \u0111\u1ed9ng:**\n\n```javascript\n// L\u01b0u token\nlocalStorage.setItem(\"accessToken\", token);\n\n// \u0110\u1ecdc token\nconst token = localStorage.getItem(\"accessToken\");\n\n// S\u1eed d\u1ee5ng\nfetch(\"/api/data\", {\n headers: {\n Authorization: `Bearer ${token}`,\n },\n});\n```\n\n**\u01afu \u0111i\u1ec3m:**\n\n- \u2705 \u0110\u01a1n gi\u1ea3n, d\u1ec5 implement\n- \u2705 Persist sau khi \u0111\u00f3ng browser (user kh\u00f4ng c\u1ea7n login l\u1ea1i)\n- \u2705 C\u00f3 th\u1ec3 access t\u1eeb JavaScript\n\n**Nh\u01b0\u1ee3c \u0111i\u1ec3m:**\n\n- \u274c **D\u1ec5 b\u1ecb XSS attacks** (Cross-Site Scripting)\n- \u274c B\u1ea5t k\u1ef3 script n\u00e0o tr\u00ean page \u0111\u1ec1u c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 \u0111\u1ecdc\n- \u274c Kh\u00f4ng t\u1ef1 \u0111\u1ed9ng expire khi \u0111\u00f3ng tab\n\n**Khi n\u00e0o d\u00f9ng:**\n\n- App \u0111\u01a1n gi\u1ea3n, kh\u00f4ng c\u00f3 user-generated content\n- \u0110\u00e3 c\u00f3 strong XSS protection\n- Convenience quan tr\u1ecdng h\u01a1n maximum security\n\n### 3.3 Option 2: SessionStorage\n\n**C\u00e1ch ho\u1ea1t \u0111\u1ed9ng:**\n\n```javascript\n// Gi\u1ed1ng localStorage nh\u01b0ng clear khi \u0111\u00f3ng tab\nsessionStorage.setItem(\"accessToken\", token);\nconst token = sessionStorage.getItem(\"accessToken\");\n```\n\n**\u01afu \u0111i\u1ec3m:**\n\n- \u2705 T\u1ef1 \u0111\u1ed9ng clear khi \u0111\u00f3ng tab/window\n- \u2705 T\u1ed1t h\u01a1n localStorage m\u1ed9t ch\u00fat (session-only)\n\n**Nh\u01b0\u1ee3c \u0111i\u1ec3m:**\n\n- \u274c V\u1eabn d\u1ec5 b\u1ecb XSS attacks\n- \u274c UX t\u1ec7 h\u01a1n (ph\u1ea3i login l\u1ea1i m\u1ed7i tab m\u1edbi)\n- \u274c Kh\u00f4ng work v\u1edbi multi-tab scenarios\n\n**Khi n\u00e0o d\u00f9ng:**\n\n- App y\u00eau c\u1ea7u security cao h\u01a1n localStorage\n- Ch\u1ea5p nh\u1eadn UX trade-off (re-login m\u1ed7i session)\n\n### 3.4 Option 3: HttpOnly Cookies (Recommended)\n\n**C\u00e1ch ho\u1ea1t \u0111\u1ed9ng:**\n\n```javascript\n// Server-side: Set cookie khi login\nres.cookie(\"refreshToken\", token, {\n httpOnly: true, // JavaScript KH\u00d4NG th\u1ec3 access\n secure: true, // Ch\u1ec9 g\u1eedi qua HTTPS\n sameSite: \"strict\", // Prevent CSRF\n maxAge: 7 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000, // 7 ng\u00e0y\n});\n\n// Client-side: Cookie t\u1ef1 \u0111\u1ed9ng g\u1eedi v\u1edbi m\u1ecdi request\n// Developer kh\u00f4ng c\u1ea7n l\u00e0m g\u00ec!\n```\n\n**\u01afu \u0111i\u1ec3m:**\n\n- \u2705 **Kh\u00f4ng th\u1ec3 access t\u1eeb JavaScript** \u2192 Immune to XSS\n- \u2705 T\u1ef1 \u0111\u1ed9ng g\u1eedi v\u1edbi m\u1ecdi request (no code needed)\n- \u2705 `sameSite` attribute ng\u0103n CSRF attacks\n- \u2705 Server control expiry v\u00e0 revocation\n\n**Nh\u01b0\u1ee3c \u0111i\u1ec3m:**\n\n- \u274c **V\u1eabn c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 b\u1ecb CSRF attacks** n\u1ebfu config sai\n- \u274c Kh\u00f4ng work v\u1edbi cross-domain requests (c\u1ea7n setup CORS c\u1ea9n th\u1eadn)\n- \u274c Ph\u1ee9c t\u1ea1p h\u01a1n v\u1edbi mobile apps v\u00e0 third-party clients\n\n**Khi n\u00e0o d\u00f9ng:**\n\n- Production applications v\u1edbi security requirements cao\n- Web apps (kh\u00f4ng ph\u1ea3i pure API servers)\n- C\u00f3 ki\u1ec3m so\u00e1t c\u1ea3 frontend v\u00e0 backend\n\n### 3.5 Best Practice: Hybrid Approach\n\n**Chi\u1ebfn l\u01b0\u1ee3c t\u1ed1t nh\u1ea5t:**\n\n```\n\u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510\n\u2502 Dual Token Strategy \u2502\n\u251c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2524\n\u2502 \u2502\n\u2502 Access Token (ng\u1eafn h\u1ea1n): \u2502\n\u2502 \u2192 L\u01b0u trong memory (JS variable) \u2502\n\u2502 \u2192 Ho\u1eb7c sessionStorage \u2502\n\u2502 \u2192 D\u00f9ng cho API requests \u2502\n\u2502 \u2502\n\u2502 Refresh Token (d\u00e0i h\u1ea1n): \u2502\n\u2502 \u2192 L\u01b0u trong httpOnly cookie \u2502\n\u2502 \u2192 Ch\u1ec9 g\u1eedi \u0111\u1ebfn /refresh endpoint \u2502\n\u2502 \u2192 Server c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 revoke \u2502\n\u2502 \u2502\n\u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518\n```\n\n**Implementation:**\n\n```javascript\n// Client-side: Token management service\nclass TokenService {\n // Access token in memory (ch\u1ec9 t\u1ed3n t\u1ea1i trong session)\n #accessToken = null;\n\n setAccessToken(token) {\n this.#accessToken = token;\n }\n\n getAccessToken() {\n return this.#accessToken;\n }\n\n clearAccessToken() {\n this.#accessToken = null;\n }\n\n // Refresh token \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c server set qua httpOnly cookie\n // Client kh\u00f4ng c\u1ea7n manage!\n}\n\n// Auto-refresh logic\nasync function fetchWithAuth(url, options = {}) {\n const accessToken = tokenService.getAccessToken();\n\n let response = await fetch(url, {\n ...options,\n headers: {\n ...options.headers,\n Authorization: `Bearer ${accessToken}`,\n },\n });\n\n // N\u1ebfu 401, th\u1eed refresh\n if (response.status === 401) {\n const newToken = await refreshAccessToken();\n tokenService.setAccessToken(newToken);\n\n // Retry request v\u1edbi token m\u1edbi\n response = await fetch(url, {\n ...options,\n headers: {\n ...options.headers,\n Authorization: `Bearer ${newToken}`,\n },\n });\n }\n\n return response;\n}\n\nasync function refreshAccessToken() {\n // Refresh token t\u1ef1 \u0111\u1ed9ng g\u1eedi qua cookie\n const response = await fetch(\"/api/refresh\", {\n method: \"POST\",\n credentials: \"include\", // G\u1eedi cookies\n });\n\n const { accessToken } = await response.json();\n return accessToken;\n}\n```\n\n### 3.6 So S\u00e1nh B\u1ea3o M\u1eadt\n\n| Storage Method | XSS Protection | CSRF Protection | Best For |\n| :------------------ | :------------: | :-------------: | :-------------- |\n| **localStorage** | \u274c Vulnerable | \u2705 Safe | Simple apps |\n| **sessionStorage** | \u274c Vulnerable | \u2705 Safe | Short sessions |\n| **httpOnly Cookie** | \u2705 Protected | \u26a0\ufe0f Needs config | Production apps |\n| **Memory only** | \u2705 Protected | \u2705 Protected | Access tokens |\n| **Hybrid** | \u2705 Protected | \u2705 Protected | **Recommended** |\n\n---\n\n## Ph\u1ea7n 4: Token Refresh Flow - Chi Ti\u1ebft Implementation\n\n### 4.1 T\u1ea1i Sao C\u1ea7n Refresh Mechanism?\n\nGi\u1ea3 s\u1eed access token c\u1ee7a b\u1ea1n expire sau 15 ph\u00fat:\n\n- **Kh\u00f4ng c\u00f3 refresh:** User ph\u1ea3i login l\u1ea1i sau m\u1ed7i 15 ph\u00fat \u2192 UX t\u1ec7\n- **C\u00f3 refresh:** App t\u1ef1 \u0111\u1ed9ng renew token, user kh\u00f4ng b\u1ecb interrupt\n\nRefresh flow l\u00e0 c\u1ea7u n\u1ed1i gi\u1eefa security (short-lived tokens) v\u00e0 UX (seamless authentication).\n\n### 4.2 Basic Refresh Flow\n\n**Step-by-step:**\n\n```\n1. User login\n \u2193\n2. Server t\u1ea1o access token (15 min) + refresh token (7 days)\n \u2193\n3. Client l\u01b0u access token (memory)\n Server set refresh token (httpOnly cookie)\n \u2193\n4. Client d\u00f9ng access token cho m\u1ecdi API requests\n \u2193\n5. Access token h\u1ebft h\u1ea1n \u2192 API tr\u1ea3 401\n \u2193\n6. Client g\u1ecdi /refresh endpoint (t\u1ef1 \u0111\u1ed9ng g\u1eedi refresh token qua cookie)\n \u2193\n7. Server verify refresh token \u2192 t\u1ea1o access token m\u1edbi\n \u2193\n8. Client l\u01b0u access token m\u1edbi v\u00e0 retry request failed\n```\n\n### 4.3 Server-Side Implementation\n\n**Backend (Node.js + Express):**\n\n```javascript\nconst express = require(\"express\");\nconst jwt = require(\"jsonwebtoken\");\nconst cookieParser = require(\"cookie-parser\");\n\nconst app = express();\napp.use(cookieParser());\napp.use(express.json());\n\n// Secret keys (PH\u1ea2I l\u01b0u trong environment variables!)\nconst ACCESS_SECRET = process.env.ACCESS_SECRET;\nconst REFRESH_SECRET = process.env.REFRESH_SECRET;\n\n// Token storage (production: d\u00f9ng Redis)\nconst refreshTokens = new Set();\n\n// 1. Login endpoint\napp.post(\"/api/login\", async (req, res) => {\n const { email, password } = req.body;\n\n // Verify credentials (simplified)\n const user = await verifyCredentials(email, password);\n if (!user) {\n return res.status(401).json({ error: \"Invalid credentials\" });\n }\n\n // Generate tokens\n const accessToken = jwt.sign(\n {\n sub: user.id,\n email: user.email,\n role: user.role,\n },\n ACCESS_SECRET,\n { expiresIn: \"15m\" },\n );\n\n const refreshToken = jwt.sign({ sub: user.id }, REFRESH_SECRET, {\n expiresIn: \"7d\",\n });\n\n // L\u01b0u refresh token (production: Redis v\u1edbi expiry)\n refreshTokens.add(refreshToken);\n\n // Set refresh token v\u00e0o httpOnly cookie\n res.cookie(\"refreshToken\", refreshToken, {\n httpOnly: true,\n secure: process.env.NODE_ENV === \"production\",\n sameSite: \"strict\",\n maxAge: 7 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000, // 7 ng\u00e0y\n });\n\n // Tr\u1ea3 access token trong response body\n res.json({ accessToken });\n});\n\n// 2. Refresh endpoint\napp.post(\"/api/refresh\", (req, res) => {\n const refreshToken = req.cookies.refreshToken;\n\n if (!refreshToken) {\n return res.status(401).json({ error: \"No refresh token\" });\n }\n\n // Verify refresh token c\u00f2n valid\n if (!refreshTokens.has(refreshToken)) {\n return res.status(403).json({ error: \"Invalid refresh token\" });\n }\n\n try {\n // Verify JWT signature\n const payload = jwt.verify(refreshToken, REFRESH_SECRET);\n\n // Generate new access token\n const newAccessToken = jwt.sign(\n {\n sub: payload.sub,\n email: payload.email,\n role: payload.role,\n },\n ACCESS_SECRET,\n { expiresIn: \"15m\" },\n );\n\n res.json({ accessToken: newAccessToken });\n } catch (error) {\n return res.status(403).json({ error: \"Invalid or expired token\" });\n }\n});\n\n// 3. Protected endpoint example\napp.get(\"/api/protected\", verifyAccessToken, (req, res) => {\n res.json({\n message: \"Protected data\",\n user: req.user,\n });\n});\n\n// 4. Logout endpoint\napp.post(\"/api/logout\", (req, res) => {\n const refreshToken = req.cookies.refreshToken;\n\n // Remove t\u1eeb whitelist\n refreshTokens.delete(refreshToken);\n\n // Clear cookie\n res.clearCookie(\"refreshToken\");\n\n res.json({ message: \"Logged out\" });\n});\n\n// Middleware verify access token\nfunction verifyAccessToken(req, res, next) {\n const authHeader = req.headers.authorization;\n\n if (!authHeader || !authHeader.startsWith(\"Bearer \")) {\n return res.status(401).json({ error: \"No access token\" });\n }\n\n const token = authHeader.substring(7);\n\n try {\n const payload = jwt.verify(token, ACCESS_SECRET);\n req.user = payload;\n next();\n } catch (error) {\n return res.status(401).json({ error: \"Invalid or expired access token\" });\n }\n}\n```\n\n### 4.4 Client-Side Implementation\n\n**Frontend (React v\u1edbi Axios):**\n\n```javascript\nimport axios from \"axios\";\n\n// Axios instance v\u1edbi interceptors\nconst api = axios.create({\n baseURL: \"http://localhost:3000/api\",\n withCredentials: true, // G\u1eedi cookies\n});\n\n// Store access token trong memory\nlet accessToken = null;\n\nexport function setAccessToken(token) {\n accessToken = token;\n}\n\nexport function getAccessToken() {\n return accessToken;\n}\n\n// Request interceptor: t\u1ef1 \u0111\u1ed9ng th\u00eam Authorization header\napi.interceptors.request.use(\n (config) => {\n if (accessToken) {\n config.headers.Authorization = `Bearer ${accessToken}`;\n }\n return config;\n },\n (error) => Promise.reject(error),\n);\n\n// Response interceptor: t\u1ef1 \u0111\u1ed9ng refresh khi 401\napi.interceptors.response.use(\n (response) => response, // Success case: kh\u00f4ng l\u00e0m g\u00ec\n async (error) => {\n const originalRequest = error.config;\n\n // N\u1ebfu l\u1ed7i 401 v\u00e0 ch\u01b0a retry\n if (error.response?.status === 401 && !originalRequest._retry) {\n originalRequest._retry = true;\n\n try {\n // G\u1ecdi refresh endpoint\n const response = await axios.post(\n \"http://localhost:3000/api/refresh\",\n {},\n { withCredentials: true },\n );\n\n const newAccessToken = response.data.accessToken;\n setAccessToken(newAccessToken);\n\n // Retry request v\u1edbi token m\u1edbi\n originalRequest.headers.Authorization = `Bearer ${newAccessToken}`;\n return api(originalRequest);\n } catch (refreshError) {\n // Refresh th\u1ea5t b\u1ea1i \u2192 logout user\n setAccessToken(null);\n window.location.href = \"/login\";\n return Promise.reject(refreshError);\n }\n }\n\n return Promise.reject(error);\n },\n);\n\n// Login function\nexport async function login(email, password) {\n const response = await api.post(\"/login\", { email, password });\n const { accessToken } = response.data;\n setAccessToken(accessToken);\n return response.data;\n}\n\n// Logout function\nexport async function logout() {\n await api.post(\"/logout\");\n setAccessToken(null);\n}\n\nexport default api;\n```\n\n**Usage trong React components:**\n\n```javascript\nimport React, { useEffect, useState } from \"react\";\nimport api from \"./apiClient\";\n\nfunction Dashboard() {\n const [data, setData] = useState(null);\n\n useEffect(() => {\n // G\u1ecdi protected API - auto refresh n\u1ebfu c\u1ea7n\n api\n .get(\"/protected\")\n .then((res) => setData(res.data))\n .catch((err) => console.error(err));\n }, []);\n\n return
{data && 
{JSON.stringify(data, null, 2)}
}
;\n}\n```\n\n### 4.5 Advanced: Token Rotation\n\n**V\u1ea5n \u0111\u1ec1 v\u1edbi basic refresh:**\n\nN\u1ebfu refresh token b\u1ecb \u0111\u00e1nh c\u1eafp, attacker c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 d\u00f9ng n\u00f3 \u0111\u1ec3 generate access tokens li\u00ean t\u1ee5c cho \u0111\u1ebfn khi refresh token expire (7-30 ng\u00e0y).\n\n**Gi\u1ea3i ph\u00e1p: Refresh Token Rotation**\n\nM\u1ed7i l\u1ea7n refresh, server:\n\n1. Verify refresh token c\u0169\n2. Generate access token m\u1edbi\n3. **Generate refresh token m\u1edbi** (thay th\u1ebf token c\u0169)\n4. Revoke refresh token c\u0169\n\n```javascript\n// Server: refresh v\u1edbi rotation\napp.post(\"/api/refresh\", async (req, res) => {\n const oldRefreshToken = req.cookies.refreshToken;\n\n if (!refreshTokens.has(oldRefreshToken)) {\n return res.status(403).json({ error: \"Invalid refresh token\" });\n }\n\n try {\n const payload = jwt.verify(oldRefreshToken, REFRESH_SECRET);\n\n // Generate NEW tokens\n const newAccessToken = jwt.sign(\n { sub: payload.sub, email: payload.email, role: payload.role },\n ACCESS_SECRET,\n { expiresIn: \"15m\" },\n );\n\n const newRefreshToken = jwt.sign({ sub: payload.sub }, REFRESH_SECRET, {\n expiresIn: \"7d\",\n });\n\n // Rotate: x\u00f3a c\u0169, th\u00eam m\u1edbi\n refreshTokens.delete(oldRefreshToken);\n refreshTokens.add(newRefreshToken);\n\n // Set new refresh token cookie\n res.cookie(\"refreshToken\", newRefreshToken, {\n httpOnly: true,\n secure: true,\n sameSite: \"strict\",\n maxAge: 7 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000,\n });\n\n res.json({ accessToken: newAccessToken });\n } catch (error) {\n return res.status(403).json({ error: \"Invalid token\" });\n }\n});\n```\n\n**Benefits:**\n\n- \u2705 Gi\u1ea3m th\u1eddi gian window cho token theft\n- \u2705 Detect reuse attacks (token c\u0169 \u0111\u00e3 b\u1ecb revoke)\n- \u2705 Automatic cleanup c\u1ee7a expired tokens\n\n---\n\n## Ph\u1ea7n 5: Security Concerns - Nh\u1eefng \u0110i\u1ec1u C\u1ea7n Bi\u1ebft\n\n### 5.1 XSS (Cross-Site Scripting) Attacks\n\n**Threat scenario:**\n\nAttacker inject malicious script v\u00e0o website:\n\n```html\n\n\n```\n\n**Mitigation strategies:**\n\n1. **Kh\u00f4ng l\u01b0u sensitive tokens trong localStorage**\n\n ```javascript\n // \u274c BAD\n localStorage.setItem(\"accessToken\", token);\n\n // \u2705 GOOD - d\u00f9ng memory ho\u1eb7c httpOnly cookie\n let accessToken = null; // Memory variable\n ```\n\n2. **Content Security Policy (CSP)**\n\n ```javascript\n // Server response headers\n app.use((req, res, next) => {\n res.setHeader(\n \"Content-Security-Policy\",\n \"default-src 'self'; script-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline'\",\n );\n next();\n });\n ```\n\n3. **Sanitize user input**\n\n ```javascript\n import DOMPurify from \"dompurify\";\n\n // Tr\u01b0\u1edbc khi render user content\n const cleanHTML = DOMPurify.sanitize(userInput);\n ```\n\n4. **HttpOnly cookies cho refresh tokens**\n ```javascript\n res.cookie(\"refreshToken\", token, {\n httpOnly: true, // JavaScript kh\u00f4ng th\u1ec3 access\n secure: true,\n sameSite: \"strict\",\n });\n ```\n\n### 5.2 CSRF (Cross-Site Request Forgery) Attacks\n\n**Threat scenario:**\n\nUser \u0111ang login v\u00e0o `yourbank.com`. Attacker g\u1eedi email v\u1edbi link:\n\n```html\n\n\n```\n\nBrowser t\u1ef1 \u0111\u1ed9ng g\u1eedi cookies c\u1ee7a user \u2192 Request \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c execute!\n\n**Mitigation strategies:**\n\n1. **SameSite Cookie Attribute**\n\n ```javascript\n res.cookie(\"refreshToken\", token, {\n httpOnly: true,\n secure: true,\n sameSite: \"strict\", // Ho\u1eb7c 'lax'\n });\n ```\n\n | SameSite Value | Protection | Use Case |\n | :------------- | :--------- | :---------------------------------------------- |\n | `strict` | Strongest | Cookie KH\u00d4NG g\u1eedi v\u1edbi cross-site requests |\n | `lax` | Medium | Cookie g\u1eedi v\u1edbi top-level navigations (GET only) |\n | `none` | Weakest | Cookie g\u1eedi v\u1edbi m\u1ecdi requests (c\u1ea7n HTTPS) |\n\n2. **CSRF Token Pattern**\n\n ```javascript\n // Server: generate CSRF token\n const csrfToken = generateRandomToken();\n req.session.csrfToken = csrfToken;\n\n // Client: g\u1eedi token trong header ho\u1eb7c form\n fetch(\"/api/transfer\", {\n method: \"POST\",\n headers: {\n \"X-CSRF-Token\": csrfToken,\n },\n body: JSON.stringify({ to, amount }),\n });\n\n // Server: verify token\n function verifyCsrfToken(req, res, next) {\n const token = req.headers[\"x-csrf-token\"];\n if (token !== req.session.csrfToken) {\n return res.status(403).json({ error: \"Invalid CSRF token\" });\n }\n next();\n }\n ```\n\n3. **Double Submit Cookie Pattern**\n\n ```javascript\n // \u0110\u01a1n gi\u1ea3n h\u01a1n: kh\u00f4ng c\u1ea7n session storage\n // Server set CSRF token v\u00e0o cookie (readable t\u1eeb JS)\n res.cookie(\"csrf-token\", csrfToken, {\n httpOnly: false, // Client c\u1ea7n \u0111\u1ecdc \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c\n secure: true,\n sameSite: \"strict\",\n });\n\n // Client \u0111\u1ecdc t\u1eeb cookie v\u00e0 g\u1eedi l\u1ea1i trong header\n const csrfToken = getCookie(\"csrf-token\");\n fetch(\"/api/action\", {\n headers: {\n \"X-CSRF-Token\": csrfToken,\n },\n });\n ```\n\n### 5.3 JWT Security Best Practices\n\n#### 5.3.1 Secret Key Management\n\n```javascript\n// \u274c NEVER hardcode secrets\nconst SECRET = \"mySecretKey123\";\n\n// \u2705 Use environment variables\nconst SECRET = process.env.JWT_SECRET;\n\n// \u2705 Use strong secrets (32+ characters, random)\n// openssl rand -base64 32\nconst SECRET = \"Xy7K9mP4vN2qW8tE6rA3sD5fG7hJ1kL4\";\n```\n\n#### 5.3.2 Token Expiry Time\n\n```javascript\n// \u274c Access token qu\u00e1 d\u00e0i\njwt.sign(payload, SECRET, { expiresIn: \"30d\" });\n\n// \u2705 Access token ng\u1eafn\njwt.sign(payload, ACCESS_SECRET, { expiresIn: \"15m\" });\n\n// \u2705 Refresh token d\u00e0i h\u01a1n nh\u01b0ng c\u00f3 rotation\njwt.sign(payload, REFRESH_SECRET, { expiresIn: \"7d\" });\n```\n\n#### 5.3.3 Sensitive Data Trong Payload\n\n```javascript\n// \u274c NEVER l\u01b0u sensitive data\nconst payload = {\n userId: user.id,\n email: user.email,\n password: user.password, // \u274c NGUY HI\u1ec2M!\n creditCard: user.creditCard, // \u274c NGUY HI\u1ec2M!\n ssn: user.ssn, // \u274c NGUY HI\u1ec2M!\n};\n\n// \u2705 Ch\u1ec9 l\u01b0u identifiers v\u00e0 public info\nconst payload = {\n sub: user.id, // User ID\n email: user.email, // Public info\n role: user.role, // Authorization info\n iat: Date.now(),\n};\n```\n\n**L\u00fd do:** JWT c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 decode d\u1ec5 d\u00e0ng (base64):\n\n```javascript\n// B\u1ea5t k\u1ef3 ai c\u0169ng c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 decode JWT\nconst [header, payload, signature] = token.split(\".\");\nconst decodedPayload = JSON.parse(atob(payload));\nconsole.log(decodedPayload); // C\u00f3 th\u1ec3 \u0111\u1ecdc t\u1ea5t c\u1ea3!\n```\n\n#### 5.3.4 Algorithm Confusion Attack\n\n```javascript\n// \u274c Kh\u00f4ng verify algorithm\njwt.verify(token, SECRET);\n\n// \u2705 Specify algorithms explicitly\njwt.verify(token, SECRET, {\n algorithms: [\"HS256\"], // Ch\u1ec9 accept HS256\n});\n\n// \u274c NEVER use 'none' algorithm trong production\n// Attacker c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 t\u1ea1o unsigned tokens\n```\n\n#### 5.3.5 Token Revocation Strategy\n\nJWT l\u00e0 **stateless** \u2192 Kh\u00f4ng th\u1ec3 revoke m\u1ed9t token specific. Solutions:\n\n**Option 1: Blacklist** (Redis)\n\n```javascript\n// Khi logout ho\u1eb7c detect fraud\nawait redis.setex(`blacklist:${tokenId}`, TTL, \"1\");\n\n// Verify middleware check blacklist\nasync function verifyToken(req, res, next) {\n const token = extractToken(req);\n const payload = jwt.verify(token, SECRET);\n\n // Check blacklist\n const isBlacklisted = await redis.exists(`blacklist:${payload.jti}`);\n if (isBlacklisted) {\n return res.status(401).json({ error: \"Token revoked\" });\n }\n\n req.user = payload;\n next();\n}\n```\n\n**Option 2: Whitelist** (cho refresh tokens)\n\n```javascript\n// Ch\u1ec9 accept refresh tokens trong whitelist\nconst validRefreshTokens = new Set();\n\n// Add on login\nvalidRefreshTokens.add(refreshToken);\n\n// Check on refresh\nif (!validRefreshTokens.has(refreshToken)) {\n return res.status(403).json({ error: \"Invalid token\" });\n}\n\n// Remove on logout\nvalidRefreshTokens.delete(refreshToken);\n```\n\n**Option 3: Short expiry + refresh rotation**\n\n- Access token ng\u1eafn (5-15 min) \u2192 T\u1ef1 expire nhanh\n- Refresh token c\u00f3 rotation \u2192 Old tokens t\u1ef1 \u0111\u1ed9ng invalid\n\n### 5.4 HTTPS is Mandatory\n\n```javascript\n// \u274c NEVER s\u1eed d\u1ee5ng JWT qua HTTP\n// Tokens c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 b\u1ecb intercept trong transit\n\n// \u2705 Force HTTPS trong production\nif (process.env.NODE_ENV === \"production\" && !req.secure) {\n return res.redirect(\"https://\" + req.headers.host + req.url);\n}\n\n// \u2705 Set secure flag cho cookies\nres.cookie(\"refreshToken\", token, {\n httpOnly: true,\n secure: true, // Ch\u1ec9 g\u1eedi qua HTTPS\n sameSite: \"strict\",\n});\n```\n\n### 5.5 Rate Limiting\n\n```javascript\nconst rateLimit = require(\"express-rate-limit\");\n\n// Limit login attempts\nconst loginLimiter = rateLimit({\n windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 ph\u00fat\n max: 5, // Max 5 requests\n message: \"Too many login attempts, please try again later\",\n});\n\napp.post(\"/api/login\", loginLimiter, handleLogin);\n\n// Limit refresh attempts\nconst refreshLimiter = rateLimit({\n windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000,\n max: 10,\n message: \"Too many refresh attempts\",\n});\n\napp.post(\"/api/refresh\", refreshLimiter, handleRefresh);\n```\n\n### 5.6 Security Checklist\n\nTr\u01b0\u1edbc khi deploy JWT authentication:\n\n- [ ] Access tokens c\u00f3 expiry ng\u1eafn (\u2264 15 ph\u00fat)\n- [ ] Refresh tokens s\u1eed d\u1ee5ng httpOnly cookies\n- [ ] Secret keys l\u01b0u trong environment variables (kh\u00f4ng hardcode)\n- [ ] Secret keys \u0111\u1ee7 m\u1ea1nh (32+ characters, random)\n- [ ] HTTPS \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c enforce trong production\n- [ ] sameSite='strict' cho cookies\n- [ ] CSRF protection enabled\n- [ ] Content Security Policy headers configured\n- [ ] User input \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c sanitize (prevent XSS)\n- [ ] Rate limiting cho login v\u00e0 refresh endpoints\n- [ ] Token rotation implemented cho refresh tokens\n- [ ] Logging v\u00e0 monitoring cho suspicious activities\n- [ ] Sensitive data KH\u00d4NG l\u01b0u trong JWT payload\n- [ ] Algorithm \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c specify explicitly khi verify\n- [ ] Blacklist/whitelist mechanism cho revocation\n\n---\n\n## K\u1ebft Lu\u1eadn\n\nJWT authentication l\u00e0 m\u1ed9t c\u00f4ng c\u1ee5 m\u1ea1nh m\u1ebd nh\u01b0ng c\u1ea7n \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c implement c\u1ea9n th\u1eadn. Nh\u1eefng \u0111i\u1ec3m ch\u00ednh c\u1ea7n nh\u1edb:\n\n**1. Dual Token Strategy**\n\n- Access token ng\u1eafn (15 ph\u00fat) trong memory\n- Refresh token d\u00e0i (7 ng\u00e0y) trong httpOnly cookie\n- K\u1ebft h\u1ee3p c\u1ea3 security v\u00e0 UX\n\n**2. Storage Matters**\n\n- **KH\u00d4NG** l\u01b0u tokens trong localStorage (XSS vulnerability)\n- **N\u00caN** d\u00f9ng httpOnly cookies cho refresh tokens\n- **N\u00caN** d\u00f9ng memory variables cho access tokens\n\n**3. JSON Web Tokens (JWT) have become the de facto standard for implementing stateless authentication in web applications. In this comprehensive guide, we'll explore what JWTs are, how they work, and best practices for implementing them securely.\n\n## What is JWT?\n\nJSON Web Token (JWT) is an open standard (RFC 7519) that defines a compact and self-contained way for securely transmitting information between parties as a JSON object. This information can be verified and trusted because it is digitally signed using either a secret (with HMAC algorithm) or a public/private key pair (using RSA or ECDSA).\n\n### JWT Structure\n\nA JWT consists of three parts separated by dots (`.`):\n\n```\nxxxxx.yyyyy.zzzzz\n```\n\n1. **Header**: Contains the token type (JWT) and the signing algorithm (HMAC, RSA, etc.)\n2. **Payload**: Contains the claims - statements about the user and additional data\n3. **Signature**: Used to verify the message wasn't changed and authenticate the sender\n\nExample of a decoded JWT:\n\n```json\n// Header\n{\n \"alg\": \"HS256\",\n \"typ\": \"JWT\"\n}\n\n// Payload\n{\n \"sub\": \"1234567890\",\n \"name\": \"John Doe\",\n \"email\": \"john@example.com\",\n \"iat\": 1516239022,\n \"exp\": 1516242622\n}\n\n// Signature\nHMACSHA256(\n base64UrlEncode(header) + \".\" +\n base64UrlEncode(payload),\n secret\n)\n```\n\n### Key Characteristics of JWT\n\n- **Compact**: Small size makes it easy to send through URLs, POST parameters, or HTTP headers\n- **Self-contained**: Contains all necessary user information, avoiding database queries\n- **Stateless**: Server doesn't need to store session information\n- **Portable**: Can be used across different domains and services\n\n## Access Token vs Refresh Token\n\nWhen implementing JWT authentication, it's crucial to understand the distinction between access tokens and refresh tokens.
