Whether you're building a small project or a large-scale application, understanding these utilities can significantly improve your code quality and developer experience. Let's dive into 10 essential utility types that every TypeScript developer should know.\n\n## 1. Partial<T> - Making Properties Optional\n\n### What It Does\n\n`Partial` transforms all properties of type `T` into optional properties. This is incredibly useful when you want to update only specific fields of an object.\n\n### Example\n\n```typescript\ninterface User {\n id: number;\n name: string;\n email: string;\n age: number;\n}\n\n// All properties become optional\ntype PartialUser = Partial;\n\nfunction updateUser(id: number, updates: PartialUser) {\n // Can update any subset of properties\n console.log(`Updating user ${id}`, updates);\n}\n\n// Valid calls\nupdateUser(1, { name: \"Alice\" });\nupdateUser(2, { email: \"bob@example.com\", age: 30 });\n```\n\n### When to Use\n\n- **Update operations**: When you need to update only certain fields of an entity\n- **Form handling**: Partial form submissions where not all fields are required\n- **Configuration objects**: When some config options are optional\n\n### Real-World Scenario\n\nIn a user profile update feature, you might want to allow users to update their name without forcing them to provide all profile information:\n\n```typescript\nclass UserService {\n async updateProfile(userId: string, updates: Partial) {\n // Only update the fields provided\n return await database.update({ id: userId }, updates);\n }\n}\n\n// User can update just their name\nawait userService.updateProfile(\"123\", { name: \"New Name\" });\n```\n\n## 2. Required<T> - Making All Properties Required\n\n### What It Does\n\n`Required` is the opposite of `Partial`. It transforms all optional properties into required ones.\n\n### Example\n\n```typescript\ninterface Config {\n host?: string;\n port?: number;\n timeout?: number;\n}\n\n// All properties become required\ntype RequiredConfig = Required;\n\nfunction initializeServer(config: RequiredConfig) {\n // All properties must be provided\n console.log(`Starting server on ${config.host}:${config.port}`);\n}\n\n// Error: Missing properties\n// initializeServer({ host: \"localhost\" });\n\n// Correct\ninitializeServer({\n host: \"localhost\",\n port: 3000,\n timeout: 5000,\n});\n```\n\n### When to Use\n\n- **Validation**: Ensuring all optional fields are provided before processing\n- **Initialization**: When setting up objects that need all fields defined\n- **Type narrowing**: Converting optional types to required for specific operations\n\n### Real-World Scenario\n\nWhen initializing a database connection, you might accept optional config during setup but require all values before connecting:\n\n```typescript\ninterface DatabaseConfig {\n host?: string;\n port?: number;\n username?: string;\n password?: string;\n}\n\nclass Database {\n private config: Partial = {};\n\n configure(config: Partial) {\n this.config = { ...this.config, ...config };\n }\n\n connect(finalConfig?: Partial) {\n const fullConfig: Required = {\n host: this.config.host ?? finalConfig?.host ?? \"localhost\",\n port: this.config.port ?? finalConfig?.port ?? 5432,\n username: this.config.username ?? finalConfig?.username ?? \"\",\n password: this.config.password ?? finalConfig?.password ?? \"\",\n };\n\n // Now guaranteed to have all properties\n console.log(`Connecting to ${fullConfig.host}:${fullConfig.port}`);\n }\n}\n```\n\n## 3. Readonly<T> - Immutable Properties\n\n### What It Does\n\n`Readonly` makes all properties of type `T` read-only, preventing any modifications after creation.\n\n### Example\n\n```typescript\ninterface Point {\n x: number;\n y: number;\n}\n\nconst mutablePoint: Point = { x: 10, y: 20 };\nmutablePoint.x = 30; // OK\n\nconst immutablePoint: Readonly = { x: 10, y: 20 };\n// immutablePoint.x = 30; // Error: Cannot assign to 'x'\n```\n\n### When to Use\n\n- **Immutable data structures**: When you want to prevent accidental mutations\n- **Configuration objects**: Ensuring config isn't modified after initialization\n- **Functional programming**: Creating pure functions with immutable inputs\n\n### Real-World Scenario\n\nIn a React-like component system, you might want to ensure props aren't modified:\n\n```typescript\ninterface ButtonProps {\n label: string;\n onClick: () => void;\n disabled: boolean;\n}\n\nfunction Button(props: Readonly) {\n // props.label = \"New Label\"; // Error!\n\n return {\n render: () =>\n ``,\n };\n}\n\n// Props are protected from modification\nconst btn = Button({\n label: \"Click me\",\n onClick: () => console.log(\"Clicked\"),\n disabled: false,\n});\n```\n\n## 4. Pick<T, K> - Selecting Specific Properties\n\n### What It Does\n\n`Pick` creates a new type by selecting only specified properties `K` from type `T`.\n\n### Example\n\n```typescript\ninterface Article {\n id: number;\n title: string;\n content: string;\n author: string;\n publishedAt: Date;\n tags: string[];\n}\n\n// Only these fields\ntype ArticlePreview = Pick;\n\nfunction showPreview(preview: ArticlePreview) {\n console.log(`${preview.title} by ${preview.author}`);\n}\n\nconst article: Article = {\n id: 1,\n title: \"TypeScript Guide\",\n content: \"Long content...\",\n author: \"Alice\",\n publishedAt: new Date(),\n tags: [\"typescript\", \"tutorial\"],\n};\n\n// Only passing needed fields\nshowPreview({\n id: article.id,\n title: article.title,\n author: article.author,\n});\n```\n\n### When to Use\n\n- **API responses**: Return only necessary fields to clients\n- **Data transfer objects**: Create lightweight versions of complex types\n- **Component props**: Extract specific properties for child components\n\n### Real-World Scenario\n\nBuilding a list view that only needs summary information:\n\n```typescript\ninterface Product {\n id: string;\n name: string;\n description: string;\n price: number;\n inventory: number;\n supplier: string;\n images: string[];\n specifications: Record;\n}\n\ntype ProductListItem = Pick;\n\nclass ProductService {\n async getProductList(): Promise {\n // Fetch only necessary fields from database\n const products = await db.query(`\n SELECT id, name, price, images \n FROM products\n `);\n return products;\n }\n}\n```\n\n## 5. Omit<T, K> - Excluding Specific Properties\n\n### What It Does\n\n`Omit` creates a new type by removing specified properties `K` from type `T`. It's the opposite of `Pick`.\n\n### Example\n\n```typescript\ninterface User {\n id: number;\n name: string;\n email: string;\n password: string;\n createdAt: Date;\n}\n\n// Remove sensitive fields\ntype PublicUser = Omit;\n\nfunction displayUser(user: PublicUser) {\n console.log(user.email); // OK\n // console.log(user.password); // Error: Property doesn't exist\n}\n```\n\n### When to Use\n\n- **Security**: Remove sensitive fields before sending data\n- **Form handling**: Exclude computed or system fields from user input\n- **API responses**: Filter out internal fields\n\n### Real-World Scenario\n\nCreating a safe user object for API responses:\n\n```typescript\ninterface UserEntity {\n id: string;\n username: string;\n email: string;\n password: string;\n salt: string;\n refreshToken: string;\n role: string;\n createdAt: Date;\n}\n\ntype UserResponse = Omit;\n\nclass AuthController {\n async getProfile(userId: string): Promise {\n const user = await db.users.findById(userId);\n\n // TypeScript ensures sensitive fields are not included\n const safeUser: UserResponse = {\n id: user.id,\n username: user.username,\n email: user.email,\n role: user.role,\n createdAt: user.createdAt,\n };\n\n return safeUser;\n }\n}\n```\n\n## 6. Record<K, T> - Creating Object Types\n\n### What It Does\n\n`Record` creates an object type with keys of type `K` and values of type `T`. It's perfect for creating dictionary-like structures.\n\n### Example\n\n```typescript\n// String keys, number values\ntype PageViews = Record;\n\nconst analytics: PageViews = {\n \"/home\": 1500,\n \"/about\": 300,\n \"/contact\": 150,\n};\n\n// Union keys, specific type values\ntype Theme = \"light\" | \"dark\" | \"auto\";\ntype ThemeConfig = Record;\n\nconst themes: ThemeConfig = {\n light: { background: \"#ffffff\", text: \"#000000\" },\n dark: { background: \"#000000\", text: \"#ffffff\" },\n auto: { background: \"system\", text: \"system\" },\n};\n```\n\n### When to Use\n\n- **Dictionaries/Maps**: When you need key-value pair structures\n- **Configuration mappings**: Mapping keys to configuration objects\n- **Lookup tables**: Creating indexed data structures\n\n### Real-World Scenario\n\nManaging application permissions with role-based access:\n\n```typescript\ntype Permission = \"read\" | \"write\" | \"delete\" | \"admin\";\ntype Role = \"user\" | \"moderator\" | \"admin\";\n\ntype RolePermissions = Record;\n\nconst permissions: RolePermissions = {\n user: [\"read\"],\n moderator: [\"read\", \"write\"],\n admin: [\"read\", \"write\", \"delete\", \"admin\"],\n};\n\nfunction canPerform(role: Role, action: Permission): boolean {\n return permissions[role].includes(action);\n}\n\nconsole.log(canPerform(\"user\", \"write\")); // false\nconsole.log(canPerform(\"moderator\", \"write\")); // true\n```\n\n## 7. Exclude<T, U> - Removing Types from Unions\n\n### What It Does\n\n`Exclude` removes types from union `T` that are assignable to `U`.\n\n### Example\n\n```typescript\ntype AllowedColors = \"red\" | \"blue\" | \"green\" | \"yellow\" | \"purple\";\ntype PrimaryColors = \"red\" | \"blue\" | \"yellow\";\n\n// Remove primary colors\ntype SecondaryColors = Exclude;\n// Result: 'green' | 'purple'\n\nfunction mixSecondaryColor(color: SecondaryColors) {\n console.log(`Mixing ${color}`);\n}\n\nmixSecondaryColor(\"green\"); // OK\nmixSecondaryColor(\"purple\"); // OK\n// mixSecondaryColor('red'); // Error\n```\n\n### When to Use\n\n- **Type filtering**: Remove specific types from unions\n- **Event handling**: Exclude certain event types\n- **Validation**: Create restricted type sets\n\n### Real-World Scenario\n\nCreating a type-safe event system with specific event exclusions:\n\n```typescript\ntype AppEvent =\n | \"user:login\"\n | \"user:logout\"\n | \"user:update\"\n | \"admin:login\"\n | \"admin:action\"\n | \"system:error\"\n | \"system:warning\";\n\n// Create user-only events (exclude admin and system)\ntype UserEvent = Exclude;\n\nclass UserEventLogger {\n log(event: UserEvent, data: any) {\n // Can only log user events\n console.log(`User event: ${event}`, data);\n }\n}\n\nconst logger = new UserEventLogger();\nlogger.log(\"user:login\", { userId: \"123\" }); // OK\n// logger.log('admin:login', {}); // Error\n```\n\n## 8. Extract<T, U> - Extracting Types from Unions\n\n### What It Does\n\n`Extract` extracts from union `T` only those types that are assignable to `U`. It's the opposite of `Exclude`.\n\n### Example\n\n```typescript\ntype Response = string | number | boolean | null;\n\n// Extract only primitive types\ntype PrimitiveResponse = Extract;\n// Result: string | number | boolean\n\ntype NullableResponse = Extract;\n// Result: null\n```\n\n### When to Use\n\n- **Type narrowing**: Extract specific types from unions\n- **Conditional logic**: Work with subset of union types\n- **Filtering**: Select matching types from complex unions\n\n### Real-World Scenario\n\nHandling different response types from an API:\n\n```typescript\ntype ApiResponse =\n | { status: \"success\"; data: T }\n | { status: \"error\"; error: string }\n | { status: \"loading\" }\n | { status: \"idle\" };\n\ntype SuccessResponse = Extract, { status: \"success\" }>;\ntype ErrorResponse = Extract, { status: \"error\" }>;\n\nfunction handleSuccess(response: SuccessResponse) {\n // TypeScript knows this has 'data' property\n console.log(\"Success:\", response.data);\n}\n\nfunction handleError(response: ErrorResponse) {\n // TypeScript knows this has 'error' property\n console.error(\"Error:\", response.error);\n}\n\nconst apiResult: ApiResponse = {\n status: \"success\",\n data: { id: 1, name: \"Alice\" },\n};\n\nif (apiResult.status === \"success\") {\n handleSuccess(apiResult);\n}\n```\n\n## 9. NonNullable<T> - Excluding Null and Undefined\n\n### What It Does\n\n`NonNullable` removes `null` and `undefined` from type `T`, ensuring the type is always defined.\n\n### Example\n\n```typescript\ntype MaybeString = string | null | undefined;\n\ntype DefiniteString = NonNullable;\n// Result: string\n\nfunction processValue(value: NonNullable) {\n // value is guaranteed to be a string\n console.log(value.toUpperCase());\n}\n\nconst val1: MaybeString = \"hello\";\nconst val2: MaybeString = null;\n\nif (val1 !== null && val1 !== undefined) {\n processValue(val1); // OK\n}\n\n// processValue(val2); // Error\n```\n\n### When to Use\n\n- **Null safety**: Ensure values are defined before use\n- **API responses**: Handle optional data that must be validated\n- **Data validation**: Convert nullable types to non-nullable\n\n### Real-World Scenario\n\nSafely handling database query results:\n\n```typescript\ninterface QueryResult {\n data: T | null;\n error: string | null;\n}\n\nclass DataService {\n async getUser(id: string): Promise> {\n const result: QueryResult = await db.query(\n \"SELECT * FROM users WHERE id = ?\",\n [id],\n );\n\n if (result.data === null) {\n throw new Error(\"User not found\");\n }\n\n // TypeScript now knows result.data is User, not User | null\n return result.data;\n }\n\n async getUsers(ids: string[]): Promise[]> {\n const results = await Promise.all(ids.map((id) => db.query(\"...\")));\n\n // Filter out null values and return only valid users\n return results\n .map((r) => r.data)\n .filter((user): user is NonNullable => user !== null);\n }\n}\n```\n\n## 10. ReturnType<T> - Getting Function Return Types\n\n### What It Does\n\n`ReturnType` extracts the return type of a function type `T`. This is incredibly useful for inferring types from existing functions.\n\n### Example\n\n```typescript\nfunction createUser(name: string, age: number) {\n return {\n id: Math.random(),\n name,\n age,\n createdAt: new Date(),\n };\n}\n\n// Infer the return type\ntype User = ReturnType;\n// Result: { id: number; name: string; age: number; createdAt: Date }\n\nfunction processUser(user: User) {\n console.log(`User ${user.name} is ${user.age} years old`);\n}\n\nconst newUser = createUser(\"Alice\", 30);\nprocessUser(newUser); // Type-safe!\n```\n\n### When to Use\n\n- **Type inference**: Avoid duplicating type definitions\n- **Factory functions**: Extract types from function outputs\n- **API clients**: Infer response types from methods\n\n### Real-World Scenario\n\nBuilding type-safe API clients without duplicating types:\n\n```typescript\nclass ApiClient {\n async fetchUserProfile(userId: string) {\n const response = await fetch(`/api/users/${userId}`);\n return {\n id: userId,\n name: \"User Name\",\n email: \"user@example.com\",\n preferences: {\n theme: \"dark\",\n language: \"en\",\n },\n stats: {\n posts: 42,\n followers: 150,\n },\n };\n }\n\n async fetchPosts(userId: string) {\n return [\n { id: \"1\", title: \"Post 1\", content: \"Content...\" },\n { id: \"2\", title: \"Post 2\", content: \"Content...\" },\n ];\n }\n}\n\nconst api = new ApiClient();\n\n// Infer types from methods\ntype UserProfile =\n ReturnType extends Promise ? T : never;\ntype Post =\n ReturnType extends Promise> ? T : never;\n\n// Now we can use these types throughout our app\nfunction displayProfile(profile: UserProfile) {\n console.log(`${profile.name} (${profile.email})`);\n console.log(`Theme: ${profile.preferences.theme}`);\n}\n\nfunction displayPosts(posts: Post[]) {\n posts.forEach((post) => console.log(post.title));\n}\n\n// Usage\nconst profile = await api.fetchUserProfile(\"123\");\nconst posts = await api.fetchPosts(\"123\");\n\ndisplayProfile(profile); // Type-safe\ndisplayPosts(posts); // Type-safe\n```\n\n## Combining Utility Types\n\nThe real power comes from combining these utility types:\n\n```typescript\ninterface User {\n id: string;\n name: string;\n email: string;\n password: string;\n role: \"admin\" | \"user\";\n createdAt: Date;\n}\n\n// Create a safe, partial update type\ntype UserUpdate = Partial>;\n\n// Read-only public user\ntype PublicUser = Readonly>;\n\n// Required registration fields\ntype UserRegistration = Required>;\n\nfunction updateUser(id: string, updates: UserUpdate) {\n // Can update any field except id and createdAt\n}\n\nfunction getPublicProfile(userId: string): PublicUser {\n // Returns immutable user without password\n return {} as PublicUser;\n}\n\nfunction registerUser(data: UserRegistration) {\n // All required fields must be provided\n}\n```\n\n## Conclusion\n\nTypeScript's utility types are essential tools for writing type-safe, maintainable code. They help you:\n\n- **Transform types** without duplicating definitions\n- **Enforce constraints** at compile time\n- **Improve code safety** by catching errors early\n- **Enhance developer experience** with better autocomplete\n\nStart incorporating these utility types into your projects, and you'll find your TypeScript code becoming more robust and easier to maintain. Remember, the key is to use them where they make sense \u2013 not every type needs to be wrapped in utilities, but when you need them, they're invaluable.\n\nHappy typing! \ud83c\udf89\n"}, {"name": "typescript-utility-types-vi.md", "type": "text", "content": "# L\u00e0m Ch\u1ee7 TypeScript Utility Types: H\u01b0\u1edbng D\u1eabn To\u00e0n Di\u1ec7n\n\nC\u00e1c utility types c\u1ee7a TypeScript l\u00e0 c\u00f4ng c\u1ee5 m\u1ea1nh m\u1ebd gi\u00fap b\u1ea1n bi\u1ebfn \u0111\u1ed5i v\u00e0 thao t\u00e1c v\u1edbi types m\u1ed9t c\u00e1ch d\u1ec5 d\u00e0ng. D\u00f9 b\u1ea1n \u0111ang x\u00e2y d\u1ef1ng m\u1ed9t d\u1ef1 \u00e1n nh\u1ecf hay m\u1ed9t \u1ee9ng d\u1ee5ng quy m\u00f4 l\u1edbn, vi\u1ec7c hi\u1ec3u r\u00f5 c\u00e1c utilities n\u00e0y c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 c\u1ea3i thi\u1ec7n \u0111\u00e1ng k\u1ec3 ch\u1ea5t l\u01b0\u1ee3ng code v\u00e0 tr\u1ea3i nghi\u1ec7m l\u1eadp tr\u00ecnh. H\u00e3y c\u00f9ng t\u00ecm hi\u1ec3u 10 utility types quan tr\u1ecdng m\u00e0 m\u1ecdi developer TypeScript n\u00ean bi\u1ebft.\n\n## 1. Partial<T> - Bi\u1ebfn Properties Th\u00e0nh Optional\n\n### N\u00f3 L\u00e0m G\u00ec\n\n`Partial` bi\u1ebfn \u0111\u1ed5i t\u1ea5t c\u1ea3 c\u00e1c properties c\u1ee7a type `T` th\u00e0nh optional. \u0110i\u1ec1u n\u00e0y c\u1ef1c k\u1ef3 h\u1eefu \u00edch khi b\u1ea1n ch\u1ec9 mu\u1ed1n c\u1eadp nh\u1eadt m\u1ed9t s\u1ed1 tr\u01b0\u1eddng c\u1ee5 th\u1ec3 c\u1ee7a m\u1ed9t object.\n\n### Khi N\u00e0o S\u1eed D\u1ee5ng\n\n- **Thao t\u00e1c c\u1eadp nh\u1eadt**: Khi b\u1ea1n ch\u1ec9 c\u1ea7n c\u1eadp nh\u1eadt m\u1ed9t s\u1ed1 tr\u01b0\u1eddng c\u1ee7a entity\n- **X\u1eed l\u00fd form**: G\u1eedi form m\u1ed9t ph\u1ea7n m\u00e0 kh\u00f4ng y\u00eau c\u1ea7u t\u1ea5t c\u1ea3 c\u00e1c tr\u01b0\u1eddng\n- **Configuration objects**: Khi m\u1ed9t s\u1ed1 t\u00f9y ch\u1ecdn config updateProfile(userId: string, updates: Partial) {\n // Ch\u1ec9 c\u1eadp nh\u1eadt c\u00e1c tr\u01b0\u1eddng \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c cung c\u1ea5p\n return await database.update({ id: userId }, updates);\n }\n}\n\n// User c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 ch\u1ec9 c\u1eadp nh\u1eadt t\u00ean\nawait userService.updateProfile(\"123\", { name: \"T\u00ean M\u1edbi\" });\n```\n\n## 2. Required<T> - Bi\u1ebfn T\u1ea5t C\u1ea3 Properties Th\u00e0nh Required\n\n### N\u00f3 L\u00e0m G\u00ec\n\n`Required` l\u00e0 \u0111\u1ed1i l\u1eadp c\u1ee7a `Partial`. N\u00f3 bi\u1ebfn \u0111\u1ed5i t\u1ea5t c\u1ea3 c\u00e1c optional properties th\u00e0nh required.\n\n### V\u00ed D\u1ee5\n\n```typescript\ninterface Config {\n host?: string;\n port?: number;\n timeout?: number;\n}\n\n// T\u1ea5t c\u1ea3 properties tr\u1edf th\u00e0nh required\ntype RequiredConfig = Required;\n\nfunction initializeServer(config: RequiredConfig) {\n // T\u1ea5t c\u1ea3 properties ph\u1ea3i \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c cung c\u1ea5p\n console.log(`Kh\u1edfi \u0111\u1ed9ng server t\u1ea1i ${config.host}:${config.port}`);\n}\n\n// L\u1ed7i: Thi\u1ebfu properties\n// initializeServer({ host: \"localhost\" });\n\n// \u0110\u00fang\ninitializeServer({\n host: \"localhost\",\n port: 3000,\n timeout: 5000,\n});\n```\n\n### Khi N\u00e0o S\u1eed D\u1ee5ng\n\n- **Validation**: \u0110\u1ea3m b\u1ea3o t\u1ea5t c\u1ea3 c\u00e1c tr\u01b0\u1eddng optional \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c cung c\u1ea5p tr\u01b0\u1edbc khi x\u1eed l\u00fd\n- **Initialization**: Khi thi\u1ebft l\u1eadp objects c\u1ea7n t\u1ea5t c\u1ea3 c\u00e1c tr\u01b0\u1eddng \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c \u0111\u1ecbnh ngh\u0129a\n- **Type narrowing**: Chuy\u1ec3n \u0111\u1ed5i optional types th\u00e0nh required cho c\u00e1c thao t\u00e1c c\u1ee5 th\u1ec3\n\n### T\u00ecnh Hu\u1ed1ng Th\u1ef1c T\u1ebf\n\nKhi kh\u1edfi t\u1ea1o k\u1ebft n\u1ed1i database, b\u1ea1n c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 ch\u1ea5p nh\u1eadn config optional trong qu\u00e1 tr\u00ecnh setup nh\u01b0ng y\u00eau c\u1ea7u t\u1ea5t c\u1ea3 gi\u00e1 tr\u1ecb tr\u01b0\u1edbc khi k\u1ebft n\u1ed1i:\n\n```typescript\ninterface DatabaseConfig {\n host?: string;\n port?: number;\n username?: string;\n password?: string;\n}\n\nclass Database {\n private config: Partial = {};\n\n configure(config: Partial) {\n this.config = { ...this.config, ...config };\n }\n\n connect(finalConfig?: Partial) {\n const fullConfig: Required = {\n host: this.config.host ?? finalConfig?.host ?? \"localhost\",\n port: this.config.port ?? finalConfig?.port ?? 5432,\n username: this.config.username ?? finalConfig?.username ?? \"\",\n password: this.config.password ?? finalConfig?.password ?? \"\",\n };\n\n // B\u00e2y gi\u1edd \u0111\u1ea3m b\u1ea3o c\u00f3 t\u1ea5t c\u1ea3 properties\n console.log(`K\u1ebft n\u1ed1i \u0111\u1ebfn ${fullConfig.host}:${fullConfig.port}`);\n }\n}\n```\n\n## 3. Readonly<T> - Properties B\u1ea5t Bi\u1ebfn\n\n### N\u00f3 L\u00e0m G\u00ec\n\n`Readonly` l\u00e0m cho t\u1ea5t c\u1ea3 c\u00e1c properties c\u1ee7a type `T` ch\u1ec9 \u0111\u1ecdc (read-only), ng\u0103n ch\u1eb7n m\u1ecdi s\u1eeda \u0111\u1ed5i sau khi t\u1ea1o.\n\n### V\u00ed D\u1ee5\n\n```typescript\ninterface Point {\n x: number;\n y: number;\n}\n\nconst mutablePoint: Point = { x: 10, y: 20 };\nmutablePoint.x = 30; // OK\n\nconst immutablePoint: Readonly = { x: 10, y: 20 };\n// immutablePoint.x = 30; // L\u1ed7i: Kh\u00f4ng th\u1ec3 g\u00e1n cho 'x'\n```\n\n### Khi N\u00e0o S\u1eed D\u1ee5ng\n\n- **C\u1ea5u tr\u00fac d\u1eef li\u1ec7u b\u1ea5t bi\u1ebfn**: Khi b\u1ea1n mu\u1ed1n ng\u0103n ch\u1eb7n c\u00e1c thay \u0111\u1ed5i kh\u00f4ng mong mu\u1ed1n\n- **Configuration objects**: \u0110\u1ea3m b\u1ea3o config kh\u00f4ng b\u1ecb s\u1eeda \u0111\u1ed5i sau khi kh\u1edfi t\u1ea1o\n- **L\u1eadp tr\u00ecnh h\u00e0m**: T\u1ea1o c\u00e1c h\u00e0m thu\u1ea7n t\u00fay v\u1edbi inputs b\u1ea5t bi\u1ebfn\n\n### T\u00ecnh Hu\u1ed1ng Th\u1ef1c T\u1ebf\n\nTrong m\u1ed9t h\u1ec7 th\u1ed1ng component gi\u1ed1ng React, b\u1ea1n c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 mu\u1ed1n \u0111\u1ea3m b\u1ea3o props kh\u00f4ng b\u1ecb s\u1eeda \u0111\u1ed5i:\n\n```typescript\ninterface ButtonProps {\n label: string;\n onClick: () => void;\n disabled: boolean;\n}\n\nfunction Button(props: Readonly) {\n // props.label = \"Label M\u1edbi\"; // L\u1ed7i!\n\n return {\n render: () =>\n ``,\n };\n}\n\n// Props \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c b\u1ea3o v\u1ec7 kh\u1ecfi s\u1eeda \u0111\u1ed5i\nconst btn = Button({\n label: \"Nh\u1ea5n v\u00e0o t\u00f4i\",\n onClick: () => console.log(\"\u0110\u00e3 nh\u1ea5n\"),\n disabled: false,\n});\n```\n\n## 4. Pick<T, K> - Ch\u1ecdn Properties C\u1ee5 Th\u1ec3\n\n### N\u00f3 L\u00e0m G\u00ec\n\n`Pick` t\u1ea1o m\u1ed9t type m\u1edbi b\u1eb1ng c\u00e1ch ch\u1ec9 ch\u1ecdn c\u00e1c properties `K` \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c ch\u1ec9 \u0111\u1ecbnh t\u1eeb type `T`.\n\n### V\u00ed D\u1ee5\n\n```typescript\ninterface Article {\n id: number;\n title: string;\n content: string;\n author: string;\n publishedAt: Date;\n tags: string[];\n}\n\n// Ch\u1ec9 c\u00e1c tr\u01b0\u1eddng n\u00e0y\ntype ArticlePreview = Pick;\n\nfunction showPreview(preview: ArticlePreview) {\n console.log(`${preview.title} b\u1edfi ${preview.author}`);\n}\n\nconst article: Article = {\n id: 1,\n title: \"H\u01b0\u1edbng D\u1eabn TypeScript\",\n content: \"N\u1ed9i dung d\u00e0i...\",\n author: \"Alice\",\n publishedAt: new Date(),\n tags: [\"typescript\", \"tutorial\"],\n};\n\n// Ch\u1ec9 truy\u1ec1n c\u00e1c tr\u01b0\u1eddng c\u1ea7n thi\u1ebft\nshowPreview({\n id: article.id,\n title: article.title,\n author: article.author,\n});\n```\n\n### Khi N\u00e0o S\u1eed D\u1ee5ng\n\n- **API responses**: Tr\u1ea3 v\u1ec1 ch\u1ec9 c\u00e1c tr\u01b0\u1eddng c\u1ea7n thi\u1ebft cho clients\n- **Data transfer objects**: T\u1ea1o phi\u00ean b\u1ea3n nh\u1eb9 c\u1ee7a c\u00e1c types ph\u1ee9c t\u1ea1p\n- **Component props**: Tr\u00edch xu\u1ea5t c\u00e1c properties c\u1ee5 th\u1ec3 cho child components\n\n### T\u00ecnh Hu\u1ed1ng Th\u1ef1c T\u1ebf\n\nX\u00e2y d\u1ef1ng ch\u1ebf \u0111\u1ed9 xem danh s\u00e1ch ch\u1ec9 c\u1ea7n th\u00f4ng tin t\u00f3m t\u1eaft:\n\n```typescript\ninterface Product {\n id: string;\n name: string;\n description: string;\n price: number;\n inventory: number;\n supplier: string;\n images: string[];\n specifications: Record;\n}\n\ntype ProductListItem = Pick;\n\nclass ProductService {\n async getProductList(): Promise {\n // Ch\u1ec9 l\u1ea5y c\u00e1c tr\u01b0\u1eddng c\u1ea7n thi\u1ebft t\u1eeb database\n const products = await db.query(`\n SELECT id, name, price, images \n FROM products\n `);\n return products;\n }\n}\n```\n\n## 5. Omit<T, K> - Lo\u1ea1i B\u1ecf Properties C\u1ee5 Th\u1ec3\n\n### N\u00f3 L\u00e0m G\u00ec\n\n`Omit` t\u1ea1o m\u1ed9t type m\u1edbi b\u1eb1ng c\u00e1ch lo\u1ea1i b\u1ecf c\u00e1c properties `K` \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c ch\u1ec9 \u0111\u1ecbnh t\u1eeb type `T`. N\u00f3 l\u00e0 \u0111\u1ed1i l\u1eadp c\u1ee7a `Pick`.\n\n### V\u00ed D\u1ee5\n\n```typescript\ninterface User {\n id: number;\n name: string;\n email: string;\n password: string;\n createdAt: Date;\n}\n\n// Lo\u1ea1i b\u1ecf c\u00e1c tr\u01b0\u1eddng nh\u1ea1y c\u1ea3m\ntype PublicUser = Omit;\n\nfunction displayUser(user: PublicUser) {\n console.log(user.email); // OK\n // console.log(user.password); // L\u1ed7i: Property kh\u00f4ng t\u1ed3n t\u1ea1i\n}\n```\n\n### Khi N\u00e0o S\u1eed D\u1ee5ng\n\n- **B\u1ea3o m\u1eadt**: Lo\u1ea1i b\u1ecf c\u00e1c tr\u01b0\u1eddng nh\u1ea1y c\u1ea3m tr\u01b0\u1edbc khi g\u1eedi d\u1eef li\u1ec7u\n- **X\u1eed l\u00fd form**: Lo\u1ea1i tr\u1eeb c\u00e1c tr\u01b0\u1eddng \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c t\u00ednh to\u00e1n ho\u1eb7c tr\u01b0\u1eddng h\u1ec7 th\u1ed1ng kh\u1ecfi input c\u1ee7a user\n- **API responses**: L\u1ecdc ra c\u00e1c tr\u01b0\u1eddng n\u1ed9i b\u1ed9\n\n### T\u00ecnh Hu\u1ed1ng Th\u1ef1c T\u1ebf\n\nT\u1ea1o object user an to\u00e0n cho API responses:\n\n```typescript\ninterface UserEntity {\n id: string;\n username: string;\n email: string;\n password: string;\n salt: string;\n refreshToken: string;\n role: string;\n createdAt: Date;\n}\n\ntype UserResponse = Omit;\n\nclass AuthController {\n async getProfile(userId: string): Promise {\n const user = await db.users.findById(userId);\n\n // TypeScript \u0111\u1ea3m b\u1ea3o c\u00e1c tr\u01b0\u1eddng nh\u1ea1y c\u1ea3m kh\u00f4ng \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c bao g\u1ed3m\n const safeUser: UserResponse = {\n id: user.id,\n username: user.username,\n email: user.email,\n role: user.role,\n createdAt: user.createdAt,\n };\n\n return safeUser;\n }\n}\n```\n\n## 6. Record<K, T> - T\u1ea1o Object Types\n\n### N\u00f3 L\u00e0m G\u00ec\n\n`Record` t\u1ea1o m\u1ed9t object type v\u1edbi keys c\u1ee7a type `K` v\u00e0 values c\u1ee7a type `T`. N\u00f3 ho\u00e0n h\u1ea3o cho vi\u1ec7c t\u1ea1o c\u00e1c c\u1ea5u tr\u00fac gi\u1ed1ng dictionary.\n\n### V\u00ed D\u1ee5\n\n```typescript\n// String keys, number values\ntype PageViews = Record;\n\nconst analytics: PageViews = {\n \"/home\": 1500,\n \"/about\": 300,\n \"/contact\": 150,\n};\n\n// Union keys, specific type values\ntype Theme = \"light\" | \"dark\" | \"auto\";\ntype ThemeConfig = Record;\n\nconst themes: ThemeConfig = {\n light: { background: \"#ffffff\", text: \"#000000\" },\n dark: { background: \"#000000\", text: \"#ffffff\" },\n auto: { background: \"system\", text: \"system\" },\n};\n```\n\n### Khi N\u00e0o S\u1eed D\u1ee5ng\n\n- **Dictionaries/Maps**: Khi b\u1ea1n c\u1ea7n c\u00e1c c\u1ea5u tr\u00fac key-value pair\n- **Configuration mappings**: \u00c1nh x\u1ea1 keys \u0111\u1ebfn configuration objects\n- **Lookup tables**: T\u1ea1o c\u00e1c c\u1ea5u tr\u00fac d\u1eef li\u1ec7u \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c \u0111\u00e1nh index\n\n### T\u00ecnh Hu\u1ed1ng Th\u1ef1c T\u1ebf\n\nQu\u1ea3n l\u00fd quy\u1ec1n c\u1ee7a \u1ee9ng d\u1ee5ng v\u1edbi role-based access:\n\n```typescript\ntype Permission = \"read\" | \"write\" | \"delete\" | \"admin\";\ntype Role = \"user\" | \"moderator\" | \"admin\";\n\ntype RolePermissions = Record;\n\nconst permissions: RolePermissions = {\n user: [\"read\"],\n moderator: [\"read\", \"write\"],\n admin: [\"read\", \"write\", \"delete\", \"admin\"],\n};\n\nfunction canPerform(role: Role, action: Permission): boolean {\n return permissions[role].includes(action);\n}\n\nconsole.log(canPerform(\"user\", \"write\")); // false\nconsole.log(canPerform(\"moderator\", \"write\")); // true\n```\n\n## 7. Exclude<T, U> - Lo\u1ea1i B\u1ecf Types Kh\u1ecfi Unions\n\n### N\u00f3 L\u00e0m G\u00ec\n\n`Exclude` lo\u1ea1i b\u1ecf c\u00e1c types t\u1eeb union `T` m\u00e0 c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 g\u00e1n cho `U`.\n\n### V\u00ed D\u1ee5\n\n```typescript\ntype AllowedColors = \"red\" | \"blue\" | \"green\" | \"yellow\" | \"purple\";\ntype PrimaryColors = \"red\" | \"blue\" | \"yellow\";\n\n// Lo\u1ea1i b\u1ecf m\u00e0u nguy\u00ean th\u1ee7y\ntype SecondaryColors = Exclude;\n// K\u1ebft qu\u1ea3: 'green' | 'purple'\n\nfunction mixSecondaryColor(color: SecondaryColors) {\n console.log(`\u0110ang pha m\u00e0u ${color}`);\n}\n\nmixSecondaryColor(\"green\"); // OK\nmixSecondaryColor(\"purple\"); // OK\n// mixSecondaryColor('red'); // L\u1ed7i\n```\n\n### Khi N\u00e0o S\u1eed D\u1ee5ng\n\n- **L\u1ecdc type**: Lo\u1ea1i b\u1ecf c\u00e1c types c\u1ee5 th\u1ec3 kh\u1ecfi unions\n- **X\u1eed l\u00fd s\u1ef1 ki\u1ec7n**: Lo\u1ea1i tr\u1eeb m\u1ed9t s\u1ed1 lo\u1ea1i s\u1ef1 ki\u1ec7n nh\u1ea5t \u0111\u1ecbnh\n- **Validation**: T\u1ea1o c\u00e1c t\u1eadp h\u1ee3p type b\u1ecb h\u1ea1n ch\u1ebf\n\n### T\u00ecnh Hu\u1ed1ng Th\u1ef1c T\u1ebf\n\nT\u1ea1o m\u1ed9t h\u1ec7 th\u1ed1ng s\u1ef1 ki\u1ec7n type-safe v\u1edbi c\u00e1c lo\u1ea1i tr\u1eeb s\u1ef1 ki\u1ec7n c\u1ee5 th\u1ec3:\n\n```typescript\ntype AppEvent =\n | \"user:login\"\n | \"user:logout\"\n | \"user:update\"\n | \"admin:login\"\n | \"admin:action\"\n | \"system:error\"\n | \"system:warning\";\n\n// T\u1ea1o c\u00e1c s\u1ef1 ki\u1ec7n ch\u1ec9 cho user (lo\u1ea1i tr\u1eeb admin v\u00e0 system)\ntype UserEvent = Exclude;\n\nclass UserEventLogger {\n log(event: UserEvent, data: any) {\n // Ch\u1ec9 c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 log c\u00e1c s\u1ef1 ki\u1ec7n c\u1ee7a user\n console.log(`S\u1ef1 ki\u1ec7n user: ${event}`, data);\n }\n}\n\nconst logger = new UserEventLogger();\nlogger.log(\"user:login\", { userId: \"123\" }); // OK\n// logger.log('admin:login', {}); // L\u1ed7i\n```\n\n## 8. Extract<T, U> - Tr\u00edch Xu\u1ea5t Types T\u1eeb Unions\n\n### N\u00f3 L\u00e0m G\u00ec\n\n`Extract` tr\u00edch xu\u1ea5t t\u1eeb union `T` ch\u1ec9 nh\u1eefng types c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 g\u00e1n cho `U`. N\u00f3 l\u00e0 \u0111\u1ed1i l\u1eadp c\u1ee7a `Exclude`.\n\n### V\u00ed D\u1ee5\n\n```typescript\ntype Response = string | number | boolean | null;\n\n// Tr\u00edch xu\u1ea5t ch\u1ec9 c\u00e1c primitive types\ntype PrimitiveResponse = Extract;\n// K\u1ebft qu\u1ea3: string | number | boolean\n\ntype NullableResponse = Extract;\n// K\u1ebft qu\u1ea3: null\n```\n\n### Khi N\u00e0o S\u1eed D\u1ee5ng\n\n- **Type narrowing**: Tr\u00edch xu\u1ea5t c\u00e1c types c\u1ee5 th\u1ec3 t\u1eeb unions\n- **Logic c\u00f3 \u0111i\u1ec1u ki\u1ec7n**: L\u00e0m vi\u1ec7c v\u1edbi t\u1eadp con c\u1ee7a union types\n- **L\u1ecdc**: Ch\u1ecdn c\u00e1c types kh\u1edbp t\u1eeb unions ph\u1ee9c t\u1ea1p\n\n### T\u00ecnh Hu\u1ed1ng Th\u1ef1c T\u1ebf\n\nX\u1eed l\u00fd c\u00e1c lo\u1ea1i response kh\u00e1c nhau t\u1eeb m\u1ed9t API:\n\n```typescript\ntype ApiResponse =\n | { status: \"success\"; data: T }\n | { status: \"error\"; error: string }\n | { status: \"loading\" }\n | { status: \"idle\" };\n\ntype SuccessResponse = Extract, { status: \"success\" }>;\ntype ErrorResponse = Extract, { status: \"error\" }>;\n\nfunction handleSuccess(response: SuccessResponse) {\n // TypeScript bi\u1ebft \u0111i\u1ec1u n\u00e0y c\u00f3 property 'data'\n console.log(\"Th\u00e0nh c\u00f4ng:\", response.data);\n}\n\nfunction handleError(response: ErrorResponse) {\n // TypeScript bi\u1ebft \u0111i\u1ec1u n\u00e0y c\u00f3 property 'error'\n console.error(\"L\u1ed7i:\", response.error);\n}\n\nconst apiResult: ApiResponse = {\n status: \"success\",\n data: { id: 1, name: \"Alice\" },\n};\n\nif (apiResult.status === \"success\") {\n handleSuccess(apiResult);\n}\n```\n\n## 9. NonNullable<T> - Lo\u1ea1i Tr\u1eeb Null V\u00e0 Undefined\n\n### N\u00f3 L\u00e0m G\u00ec\n\n`NonNullable` lo\u1ea1i b\u1ecf `null` v\u00e0 `undefined` kh\u1ecfi type `T`, \u0111\u1ea3m b\u1ea3o type lu\u00f4n \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c \u0111\u1ecbnh ngh\u0129a.\n\n### V\u00ed D\u1ee5\n\n```typescript\ntype MaybeString = string | null | undefined;\n\ntype DefiniteString = NonNullable;\n// K\u1ebft qu\u1ea3: string\n\nfunction processValue(value: NonNullable) {\n // value \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c \u0111\u1ea3m b\u1ea3o l\u00e0 m\u1ed9t string\n console.log(value.toUpperCase());\n}\n\nconst val1: MaybeString = \"hello\";\nconst val2: MaybeString = null;\n\nif (val1 !== null && val1 !== undefined) {\n processValue(val1); // OK\n}\n\n// processValue(val2); // L\u1ed7i\n```\n\n### Khi N\u00e0o S\u1eed D\u1ee5ng\n\n- **Null safety**: \u0110\u1ea3m b\u1ea3o c\u00e1c gi\u00e1 tr\u1ecb \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c \u0111\u1ecbnh ngh\u0129a tr\u01b0\u1edbc khi s\u1eed d\u1ee5ng\n- **API responses**: X\u1eed l\u00fd d\u1eef li\u1ec7u optional ph\u1ea3i \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c validate\n- **Data validation**: Chuy\u1ec3n \u0111\u1ed5i nullable types th\u00e0nh non-nullable\n\n### T\u00ecnh Hu\u1ed1ng Th\u1ef1c T\u1ebf\n\nX\u1eed l\u00fd an to\u00e0n k\u1ebft qu\u1ea3 truy v\u1ea5n database:\n\n```typescript\ninterface QueryResult {\n data: T | null;\n error: string | null;\n}\n\nclass DataService {\n async getUser(id: string): Promise> {\n const result: QueryResult = await db.query(\n \"SELECT * FROM users WHERE id = ?\",\n [id],\n );\n\n if (result.data === null) {\n throw new Error(\"Kh\u00f4ng t\u00ecm th\u1ea5y user\");\n }\n\n // TypeScript b\u00e2y gi\u1edd bi\u1ebft result.data l\u00e0 User, kh\u00f4ng ph\u1ea3i User | null\n return result.data;\n }\n\n async getUsers(ids: string[]): Promise[]> {\n const results = await Promise.all(ids.map((id) => db.query(\"...\")));\n\n // L\u1ecdc c\u00e1c gi\u00e1 tr\u1ecb null v\u00e0 ch\u1ec9 tr\u1ea3 v\u1ec1 users h\u1ee3p l\u1ec7\n return results\n .map((r) => r.data)\n .filter((user): user is NonNullable => user !== null);\n }\n}\n```\n\n## 10. ReturnType<T> - L\u1ea5y Return Types C\u1ee7a Function\n\n### N\u00f3 L\u00e0m G\u00ec\n\n`ReturnType` tr\u00edch xu\u1ea5t return type c\u1ee7a m\u1ed9t function type `T`. \u0110i\u1ec1u n\u00e0y c\u1ef1c k\u1ef3 h\u1eefu \u00edch \u0111\u1ec3 suy lu\u1eadn types t\u1eeb c\u00e1c functions hi\u1ec7n c\u00f3.\n\n### V\u00ed D\u1ee5\n\n```typescript\nfunction createUser(name: string, age: number) {\n return {\n id: Math.random(),\n name,\n age,\n createdAt: new Date(),\n };\n}\n\n// Suy lu\u1eadn return type\ntype User = ReturnType;\n// K\u1ebft qu\u1ea3: { id: number; name: string; age: number; createdAt: Date }\n\nfunction processUser(user: User) {\n console.log(`User ${user.name} ${user.age} tu\u1ed5i`);\n}\n\nconst newUser = createUser(\"Alice\", 30);\nprocessUser(newUser); // Type-safe!\n```\n\n### Khi N\u00e0o S\u1eed D\u1ee5ng\n\n- **Type inference**: Tr\u00e1nh nh\u00e2n \u0111\u00f4i \u0111\u1ecbnh ngh\u0129a type\n- **Factory functions**: Tr\u00edch xu\u1ea5t types t\u1eeb outputs c\u1ee7a function\n- **API clients**: Suy lu\u1eadn response types t\u1eeb methods\n\n### T\u00ecnh Hu\u1ed1ng Th\u1ef1c T\u1ebf\n\nX\u00e2y d\u1ef1ng API clients type-safe m\u00e0 kh\u00f4ng nh\u00e2n \u0111\u00f4i types:\n\n```typescript\nclass ApiClient {\n async fetchUserProfile(userId: string) {\n const response = await fetch(`/api/users/${userId}`);\n return {\n id: userId,\n name: \"T\u00ean User\",\n email: \"user@example.com\",\n preferences: {\n theme: \"dark\",\n language: \"vi\",\n },\n stats: {\n posts: 42,\n followers: 150,\n },\n };\n }\n\n async fetchPosts(userId: string) {\n return [\n { id: \"1\", title: \"B\u00e0i vi\u1ebft 1\", content: \"N\u1ed9i dung...\" },\n { id: \"2\", title: \"B\u00e0i vi\u1ebft 2\", content: \"N\u1ed9i dung...\" },\n ];\n }\n}\n\nconst api = new ApiClient();\n\n// Suy lu\u1eadn types t\u1eeb methods\ntype UserProfile =\n ReturnType extends Promise ? T : never;\n\n// B\u00e2y gi\u1edd ch\u00fang ta c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 s\u1eed d\u1ee5ng c\u00e1c types n\u00e0y trong to\u00e0n b\u1ed9 app\nfunction displayProfile(profile: UserProfile) {\n console.log(`${profile.name} (${profile.email})`);\n console.log(`Theme: ${profile.preferences.theme}`);\n}\n\nfunction displayPosts(posts: Post[]) {\n posts.forEach((post) => console.log(post.title));\n}\n\n// S\u1eed d\u1ee5ng\nconst profile = await api.fetchUserProfile(\"123\");\nconst posts = await api.fetchPosts(\"123\");\n\ndisplayProfile(profile); // Type-safe\ndisplayPosts(posts); // Type-safe\n```\n\n## K\u1ebft H\u1ee3p Utility Types\n\nS\u1ee9c m\u1ea1nh th\u1ef1c s\u1ef1 \u0111\u1ebfn t\u1eeb vi\u1ec7c k\u1ebft h\u1ee3p c\u00e1c utility types:\n\n```typescript\ninterface User {\n id: string;\n name: string;\n email: string;\n password: string;\n role: \"admin\" | \"user\";\n createdAt: Date;\n}\n\n// T\u1ea1o type c\u1eadp nh\u1eadt an to\u00e0n, partial\ntype UserUpdate = Partial>;\n\n// Public user ch\u1ec9 \u0111\u1ecdc\ntype PublicUser = Readonly>;\n\n// C\u00e1c tr\u01b0\u1eddng \u0111\u0103ng k\u00fd b\u1eaft bu\u1ed9c\ntype UserRegistration = Required>;\n\nfunction updateUser(id: string, updates: UserUpdate) {\n // C\u00f3 th\u1ec3 c\u1eadp nh\u1eadt b\u1ea5t k\u1ef3 tr\u01b0\u1eddng n\u00e0o ngo\u1ea1i tr\u1eeb id v\u00e0 createdAt\n}\n\nfunction getPublicProfile(userId: string): PublicUser {\n // Tr\u1ea3 v\u1ec1 user b\u1ea5t bi\u1ebfn kh\u00f4ng c\u00f3 password\n return {} as PublicUser;\n}\n\nfunction registerUser(data: UserRegistration) {\n // T\u1ea5t c\u1ea3 c\u00e1c tr\u01b0\u1eddng b\u1eaft bu\u1ed9c ph\u1ea3i \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c cung c\u1ea5p\n}\n```\n\n## K\u1ebft Lu\u1eadn\n\nC\u00e1c utility types c\u1ee7a TypeScript l\u00e0 c\u00f4ng c\u1ee5 thi\u1ebft y\u1ebfu \u0111\u1ec3 vi\u1ebft code type-safe v\u00e0 d\u1ec5 b\u1ea3o tr\u00ec.       Benchmark Results

      "; html += "

      "; // Summary table html += ''; function fmtStat(stat, pct) { if (!stat) return "—"; const suffix = pct ? "%" : ""; const m = pct ?       Metric" + escapeHtml(labelA) + "" + escapeHtml(labelB) + "Delta
      Pass Rate" + fmtStat(a.pass_rate, true) + "" + fmtStat(b.pass_rate, true) + "' + (delta.pass_rate || "—") + "
      Time (s)" + fmtStat(a.time_seconds, false) + "" + fmtStat(b.time_seconds, false) + "' + (delta.time_seconds ? delta.time_seconds + "s" : "—") + "
      Tokens" + fmtStat(a.tokens, false) + "" + fmtStat(b.tokens, false) + "' + (delta.tokens || "—") + "
      "; // Per-eval breakdown (if runs data available) const runs = data.runs || []; if (runs.length > 0) { const evalIds = [...new Set(runs.map(r => r.eval_id))].sort((a, b) => a - b); html += "

      Per-Eval Breakdown

      "; const hasTime = runs.some(r => r.result && r.result.time_seconds != null); const hasErrors = runs.some(r => r.result && r.result.errors > 0); for (const evalId of evalIds) { const evalRuns = runs.filter(r => r.eval_id === evalId); const evalName = evalRuns[0] && evalRuns[0].eval_name ? evalRuns[0].eval_name : "Eval " + evalId; html += "

      " + escapeHtml(evalName) + "

      "; html += ''; html += ""; if (hasTime) html += ""; if (hasErrors) html += ""; html += ""; html += ""; // Group by config and render with average rows const configGroups = [...new Set(evalRuns.map(r => r.configuration))]; for (let ci = 0; ci < configGroups.length; ci++) { const config = configGroups[ci]; const configRuns = evalRuns.filter(r => r.configuration === config); if (configRuns.length === 0) continue; const rowClass = ci === 0 ? "benchmark-row-with" : "benchmark-row-without"; const configLabel = config.replace(/_/g, " ").replace(/\b\w/g, c => c.toUpperCase()); for (const run of configRuns) { const r = run.result || {}; const prClass = r.pass_rate >= 0.8 ? "benchmark-delta-positive" : r.pass_rate < 0.5 ? "benchmark-delta-negative" : ""; html += ''; html += ""; html += ""; html += '"; if (hasTime) html += ""; if (hasErrors) html += ""; html += ""; } // Average row const rates = configRuns.map(r => (r.result || {}).pass_rate || 0); const avgRate = rates.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) / rates.length; const avgPrClass = avgRate >= 0.8 ? "benchmark-delta-positive" : avgRate < 0.5 ? "benchmark-delta-negative" : ""; html += ''; html += ""; html += ""; html += '"; if (hasTime) { const times = configRuns.map(r => (r.result || {}).time_seconds).filter(t => t != null); html += ""; } if (hasErrors) html += ""; html += ""; } html += "
      ConfigRunPass RateTime (s)Crashes During Execution
      " + configLabel + "" + run.run_number + "' + ((r.pass_rate || 0) * 100).toFixed(0) + "% (" + (r.passed || 0) + "/" + (r.total || 0) + ")" + (r.time_seconds != null ? r.time_seconds.toFixed(1) : "—") + "" + (r.errors || 0) + "
      " + configLabel + "Avg' + (avgRate * 100).toFixed(0) + "%" + (times.length ? (times.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) / times.length).toFixed(1) : "—") + "
      "; // Per-assertion detail for this eval const runsWithExpectations = {}; for (const config of configGroups) { runsWithExpectations[config] = evalRuns.filter(r => r.configuration === config && r.expectations && r.expectations.length > 0); } const hasAnyExpectations = Object.values(runsWithExpectations).some(runs => runs.length > 0); if (hasAnyExpectations) { // Collect all unique assertion texts across all configs const allAssertions = []; const seen = new Set(); for (const config of configGroups) { for (const run of runsWithExpectations[config]) { for (const exp of (run.expectations || [])) { if (!seen.has(exp.text)) { seen.add(exp.text); allAssertions.push(exp.text); } } } } html += ''; html += ""; for (const config of configGroups) { const label = config.replace(/_/g, " ").replace(/\b\w/g, c => c.toUpperCase()); html += ""; } html += ""; for (const assertionText of allAssertions) { html += ""; for (const config of configGroups) { html += ""; } html += ""; } html += "
      Assertion" + escapeHtml(label) + "
      " + escapeHtml(assertionText) + ""; for (const run of runsWithExpectations[config]) { const exp = (run.expectations || []).find(e => e.text === assertionText); if (exp) { const cls = exp.passed ? "benchmark-delta-positive" : "benchmark-delta-negative"; const icon = exp.passed ? "\u2713" : "\u2717"; html += '' + icon + " "; } else { html += "— "; } } html += "
      "; } } } // Notes if (notes.length > 0) { html += '
      '; html += "

      Analysis Notes

      "; html += "
        "; for (const note of notes) { html += "
      • " + escapeHtml(note) + "
        • "; } html += "
      "; } container.innerHTML = html; } // ---- Start ---- init(); renderBenchmark();
